00212 const char *DKM_to_string(const unsigned int dkm) {
00213     switch (dkm) {
00214         case DKM_US:        return "us";
00215         case DKM_DEU:       return "ger";
00216         case DKM_JPN_PC98:  return "jpn_pc98";
00217         case DKM_JPN:       return "jpn";
00218         default:            break;
00219     }
00220 
00221     return "";
00222 }
00223 
00224 const char *DKM_to_descriptive_string(const unsigned int dkm) {
00225     switch (dkm) {
00226         case DKM_US:        return "US English";
00227         case DKM_DEU:       return "German";
00228         case DKM_JPN_PC98:  return "Japanese (PC-98)";
00229         case DKM_JPN:       return "Japanese";
00230         default:            break;
00231     }
00232 
00233     return "";
00234 }

00240 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
00241 void WindowsTaskbarUpdatePreviewRegion(void) {
00242     if (winTaskbarList != NULL) {
00243         /* Windows 7/8/10: Tell the taskbar which part of our window contains the DOS screen */
00244         RECT r;
00245 
00246         r.top = sdl.clip.y;
00247         r.left = sdl.clip.x;
00248         r.right = sdl.clip.x + sdl.clip.w;
00249         r.bottom = sdl.clip.y + sdl.clip.h;
00250 
00251         /* NTS: The MSDN documentation is misleading. Apparently, despite 30+ years of Windows SDK
00252                 behavior where the "client area" is the area below the menu bar and inside the frame,
00253                 ITaskbarList3's idea of the "client area" is the the area inside the frame INCLUDING
00254                 the menu bar. Why? */
00255         if (GetMenu(GetHWND()) != NULL) {
00256             r.top += GetSystemMetrics(SM_CYMENU);//HACK
00257             r.bottom += GetSystemMetrics(SM_CYMENU);//HACK
00258         }
00259 
00260         if (winTaskbarList->SetThumbnailClip(GetHWND(), &r) != S_OK)
00261             LOG_MSG("WARNING: ITaskbarList3::SetThumbnailClip() failed");
00262     }
00263 }
00264 
00265 void WindowsTaskbarResetPreviewRegion(void) {
00266     if (winTaskbarList != NULL) {
00267         /* Windows 7/8/10: Tell the taskbar which part of our window contains the client area (not including the menu bar) */
00268         RECT r;
00269 
00270         GetClientRect(GetHWND(), &r);
00271 
00272         /* NTS: The MSDN documentation is misleading. Apparently, despite 30+ years of Windows SDK
00273                 behavior where the "client area" is the area below the menu bar and inside the frame,
00274                 ITaskbarList3's idea of the "client area" is the the area inside the frame INCLUDING
00275                 the menu bar. Why? */
00276         if (GetMenu(GetHWND()) != NULL) {
00277             r.top += GetSystemMetrics(SM_CYMENU);//HACK
00278             r.bottom += GetSystemMetrics(SM_CYMENU);//HACK
00279         }
00280 
00281         if (winTaskbarList->SetThumbnailClip(GetHWND(), &r) != S_OK)
00282             LOG_MSG("WARNING: ITaskbarList3::SetThumbnailClip() failed");
00283     }
00284 }

00287 unsigned int mapper_keyboard_layout = DKM_US;
00288 unsigned int host_keyboard_layout = DKM_US;
00289 
00290 void KeyboardLayoutDetect(void) {
00291     unsigned int nlayout = DKM_US;
00292 
00293 #if defined(LINUX)
00294     unsigned int Linux_GetKeyboardLayout(void);
00295     nlayout = Linux_GetKeyboardLayout();
00296 
00297     /* BUGFIX: The xkbmap for 'jp' in Linux/X11 has a problem that maps both
00298      *         Ro and Yen to backslash, which in SDL's default state makes
00299      *         it impossible to map them properly in the mapper. */
00300     if (nlayout == DKM_JPN) {
00301         LOG_MSG("Engaging Linux/X11 fix for jp xkbmap in order to handle Ro/Yen keys");
00302 
00303         void Linux_JPXKBFix(void);
00304         Linux_JPXKBFix();
00305     }
00306 #elif defined(WIN32)
00307     WORD lid = LOWORD(GetKeyboardLayout(0));
00308 
00309     LOG_MSG("Windows keyboard layout ID is 0x%04x", lid);
00310 
00311     switch (lid) {
00312         case 0x0407:    nlayout = DKM_DEU; break;
00313         case 0x0409:    nlayout = DKM_US; break;
00314         case 0x0411:    nlayout = DKM_JPN; break;
00315         default:        break;
00316     }
00317 #endif
00318 
00319     host_keyboard_layout = nlayout;
00320 
00321     LOG_MSG("Host keyboard layout is now %s (%s)",
00322         DKM_to_string(host_keyboard_layout),
00323         DKM_to_descriptive_string(host_keyboard_layout));
00324 }
00325 
00326 void SetMapperKeyboardLayout(const unsigned int dkm) {
00327     /* TODO: Make mapper re-initialize layout. If the mapper interface is visible, redraw it. */
00328     mapper_keyboard_layout = dkm;
00329 
00330     LOG_MSG("Mapper keyboard layout is now %s (%s)",
00331         DKM_to_string(mapper_keyboard_layout),
00332         DKM_to_descriptive_string(mapper_keyboard_layout));
00333 }

00340 void CheckMapperKeyboardLayout(void) {
00341 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
00342     if (SDL1_hax_hasLayoutChanged()) {
00343         SDL1_hax_ackLayoutChanged();
00344         LOG_MSG("Keyboard layout changed");
00345         KeyboardLayoutDetect();
00346 
00347         if (host_keyboard_layout == DKM_JPN && IS_PC98_ARCH)
00348             SetMapperKeyboardLayout(DKM_JPN_PC98);
00349         else
00350             SetMapperKeyboardLayout(host_keyboard_layout);
00351     }
00352 #endif
00353 }

00418 void PrintScreenSizeInfo(void) {
00419 #if 1
00420     const char *method = "?";
00421 
00422     switch (screen_size_info.method) {
00423         case ScreenSizeInfo::METHOD_NONE:       method = "None";        break;
00424         case ScreenSizeInfo::METHOD_X11:        method = "X11";         break;
00425         case ScreenSizeInfo::METHOD_XRANDR:     method = "XRandR";      break;
00426         case ScreenSizeInfo::METHOD_WIN98BASE:  method = "Win98base";   break;
00427         case ScreenSizeInfo::METHOD_COREGRAPHICS:method = "CoreGraphics";break;
00428         default:                                                        break;
00429     }
00430 
00431     LOG_MSG("Screen report: Method '%s' (%.3f x %.3f pixels) at (%.3f x %.3f) (%.3f x %.3f mm) (%.3f x %.3f in) (%.3f x %.3f DPI)",
00432             method,
00433 
00434             screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width,
00435             screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height,
00436 
00437             screen_size_info.screen_position_pixels.x,
00438             screen_size_info.screen_position_pixels.y,
00439 
00440             screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_mm.width,
00441             screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_mm.height,
00442 
00443             screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_mm.width / 25.4,
00444             screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_mm.height / 25.4,
00445 
00446             screen_size_info.screen_dpi.width,
00447             screen_size_info.screen_dpi.height);
00448 #endif
00449 }

00451 #if defined(WIN32)
00452 void Windows_GetWindowDPI(ScreenSizeInfo &info) {
00453     info.clear();
00454 
00455 # if !defined(HX_DOS)
00456     HMONITOR mon;
00457     HWND hwnd;
00458 
00459     info.method = ScreenSizeInfo::METHOD_WIN98BASE;
00460 
00461     hwnd = GetHWND();
00462     if (hwnd == NULL) return;
00463 
00464     mon = MonitorFromWindow(hwnd, MONITOR_DEFAULTTONEAREST);
00465     if (mon == NULL) mon = MonitorFromWindow(hwnd, MONITOR_DEFAULTTOPRIMARY);
00466     if (mon == NULL) return;
00467 
00468     MONITORINFO mi;
00469     memset(&mi,0,sizeof(mi));
00470     mi.cbSize = sizeof(mi);
00471     if (!GetMonitorInfo(mon,&mi)) return;
00472 
00473     info.screen_position_pixels.x        = mi.rcMonitor.left;
00474     info.screen_position_pixels.y        = mi.rcMonitor.top;
00475 
00476     info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width  = mi.rcMonitor.right - mi.rcMonitor.left;
00477     info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height = mi.rcMonitor.bottom - mi.rcMonitor.top;
00478 
00479     /* Windows 10 build 1607 and later offer a "Get DPI of window" function */
00480     {
00481         HMODULE __user32;
00482 
00483         __user32 = GetModuleHandle("USER32.DLL");
00484         if (__user32) {
00485             UINT (WINAPI *__GetDpiForWindow)(HWND) = NULL;
00486 
00487             __GetDpiForWindow = (UINT (WINAPI *)(HWND))GetProcAddress(__user32,"GetDpiForWindow");
00488             if (__GetDpiForWindow) {
00489                 UINT dpi = __GetDpiForWindow(hwnd);
00490 
00491                 if (dpi != 0) {
00492                     info.screen_dpi.width = dpi;
00493                     info.screen_dpi.height = dpi;
00494 
00495                     info.screen_dimensions_mm.width = (25.4 * screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width) / dpi;
00496                     info.screen_dimensions_mm.height = (25.4 * screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height) / dpi;
00497                 }
00498             }
00499         }
00500     }
00501 # endif
00502 }
00503 #endif
00504 
00505 void UpdateWindowDimensions(void)
00506 {
00507 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00508     int w = 640,h = 480;
00509     SDL_GetWindowSize(sdl.window, &w, &h);
00510     UpdateWindowDimensions(w,h);
00511 
00512     Uint32 fl = SDL_GetWindowFlags(sdl.window);
00513     UpdateWindowMaximized((fl & SDL_WINDOW_MAXIMIZED) != 0);
00514 #endif
00515 #if defined(MACOSX)
00516     void MacOSX_GetWindowDPI(ScreenSizeInfo &info);
00517     MacOSX_GetWindowDPI(/*&*/screen_size_info);
00518 #endif
00519 #if defined(WIN32)
00520     // When maximized, SDL won't actually tell us our new dimensions, so get it ourselves.
00521     // FIXME: Instead of GetHWND() we need to track our own handle or add something to SDL 1.x
00522     //        to provide the handle!
00523     RECT r = { 0 };
00524 
00525     GetClientRect(GetHWND(), &r);
00526     UpdateWindowDimensions(r.right, r.bottom);
00527     UpdateWindowMaximized(IsZoomed(GetHWND()));
00528     Windows_GetWindowDPI(/*&*/screen_size_info);
00529 #endif
00530 #if defined(LINUX)
00531     void UpdateWindowDimensions_Linux(void);
00532     UpdateWindowDimensions_Linux();
00533     void Linux_GetWindowDPI(ScreenSizeInfo &info);
00534     Linux_GetWindowDPI(/*&*/screen_size_info);
00535 #endif
00536     PrintScreenSizeInfo();
00537 }

00594 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00595 # if defined(WIN32)
00596 HWND GetHWND()
00597 {
00598     SDL_SysWMinfo wmi;
00599     SDL_VERSION(&wmi.version);
00600     if (sdl.window == NULL)
00601         return nullptr;
00602     if (!SDL_GetWindowWMInfo(sdl.window, &wmi))
00603         return nullptr;
00604     return wmi.info.win.window;
00605 }

00613 void SDL_rect_cliptoscreen(SDL_Rect &r) {
00614     if (r.x < 0) {
00615         r.w += r.x;
00616         r.x = 0;
00617     }
00618     if (r.y < 0) {
00619         r.h += r.y;
00620         r.y = 0;
00621     }
00622     if ((r.x+r.w) > sdl.surface->w)
00623         r.w = sdl.surface->w - r.x;
00624     if ((r.y+r.h) > sdl.surface->h)
00625         r.h = sdl.surface->h - r.y;
00626     /* NTS: Apparently r.w and r.h are unsigned, therefore no need to check if negative */
00627 //    if (r.w < 0) r.w = 0;
00628 //    if (r.h < 0) r.h = 0;
00629 }

00632     return sdl.num_joysticks;
00633 }

00686 extern std::string dosbox_title;
00687 
00688 void GFX_SetTitle(Bit32s cycles,Bits frameskip,Bits timing,bool paused){
00689     (void)frameskip;//UNUSED
00690     (void)timing;//UNUSED
00691 //  static Bits internal_frameskip=0;
00692     static Bit32s internal_cycles=0;
00693 //  static Bits internal_timing=0;
00694     char title[200] = {0};
00695 
00696     Section_prop *section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("SDL"));
00697     assert(section != NULL);
00698     titlebar = section->Get_string("titlebar");
00699 
00700     if (cycles != -1) internal_cycles = cycles;
00701 //  if (timing != -1) internal_timing = timing;
00702 //  if (frameskip != -1) internal_frameskip = frameskip;
00703 
00704     sprintf(title,"%s%sDOSBox-X %s, %d cyc/ms",
00705         dosbox_title.c_str(),dosbox_title.empty()?"":": ",
00706         VERSION,(int)internal_cycles);
00707 
00708     {
00709         const char *what = (titlebar != NULL && *titlebar != 0) ? titlebar : RunningProgram;
00710 
00711         if (what != NULL && *what != 0) {
00712             char *p = title + strlen(title); // append to end of string
00713 
00714             sprintf(p,", %s",what);
00715         }
00716     }
00717 
00718     if (!menu.hidecycles) {
00719         char *p = title + strlen(title); // append to end of string
00720 
00721         sprintf(p,", FPS %2d",(int)frames);
00722     }
00723 
00724     if (menu.showrt) {
00725         char *p = title + strlen(title); // append to end of string
00726 
00727         sprintf(p,", %2d%%/RT",(int)floor((rtdelta / 10) + 0.5));
00728     }
00729 
00730     if (paused) strcat(title," PAUSED");
00731 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00732     SDL_SetWindowTitle(sdl.window,title);
00733 #else
00734     SDL_WM_SetCaption(title,VERSION);
00735 #endif
00736 }
00737 
00738 bool warn_on_mem_write = false;
00739 
00740 void CPU_Snap_Back_To_Real_Mode();
00741 
00742 static void KillSwitch(bool pressed) {
00743     if (!pressed) return;
00744     if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen) GFX_SwitchFullScreen();
00745 #if 0 /* Re-enable this hack IF DOSBox continues to have problems page-faulting on kill switch */
00746     CPU_Snap_Back_To_Real_Mode(); /* TEMPORARY HACK. There are portions of DOSBox that write to memory as if still running DOS. */
00747     /* ^ Without this hack, when running Windows NT 3.1 this Kill Switch effectively becomes the Instant Page Fault BSOD switch
00748      * because the DOSBox code attempting to write to real mode memory causes a page fault (though hitting the kill switch a
00749      * second time shuts DOSBox down properly). It's sort of the same issue behind the INT 33h emulation causing instant BSOD
00750      * in Windows NT the instant you moved or clicked the mouse. The purpose of this hack is that, before any of that DOSBox
00751      * code has a chance, we force the CPU back into real mode so that the code doesn't trigger funny page faults and DOSBox
00752      * shuts down properly. */
00753 #endif
00754     warn_on_mem_write = true;
00755     throw 1;
00756 }

00758 void BlankDisplay(void) {
00759     if (OpenGL_using()) {
00760         LOG_MSG("FIXME: BlankDisplay() not implemented for OpenGL mode");
00761     }
00762     else {
00763         SDL_FillRect(sdl.surface,0,0);
00764 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00765         SDL_UpdateWindowSurface(sdl.window);
00766 #else
00767         SDL_Flip(sdl.surface);
00768 #endif
00769     }
00770 }
00771 
00772 void GFX_SDL_Overscan(void) {
00773     sdl.overscan_color=0;
00774     if (sdl.overscan_width) {
00775         Bitu border_color =  GFX_GetRGB(vga.dac.rgb[vga.attr.overscan_color].red<<2,
00776             vga.dac.rgb[vga.attr.overscan_color].green<<2, vga.dac.rgb[vga.attr.overscan_color].blue<<2);
00777         if (border_color != sdl.overscan_color) {
00778             sdl.overscan_color = border_color;
00779 
00780         // Find four rectangles forming the border
00781             SDL_Rect *rect = &sdl.updateRects[0];
00782             rect->x = 0; rect->y = 0; rect->w = sdl.draw.width+(unsigned int)(2*sdl.clip.x); rect->h = (uint16_t)sdl.clip.y; // top
00783             if ((Bitu)rect->h > (Bitu)sdl.overscan_width) { rect->y += (int)(rect->h-sdl.overscan_width); rect->h = (uint16_t)sdl.overscan_width; }
00784             if ((Bitu)sdl.clip.x > (Bitu)sdl.overscan_width) { rect->x += (int)sdl.clip.x-(int)sdl.overscan_width; rect->w -= (uint16_t)(2*((int)sdl.clip.x-(int)sdl.overscan_width)); }
00785             rect = &sdl.updateRects[1];
00786             rect->x = 0; rect->y = sdl.clip.y; rect->w = (uint16_t)sdl.clip.x; rect->h = (uint16_t)sdl.draw.height; // left
00787             if ((unsigned int)rect->w > (unsigned int)sdl.overscan_width) { rect->x += (int)rect->w-(int)sdl.overscan_width; rect->w = (uint16_t)sdl.overscan_width; }
00788             rect = &sdl.updateRects[2];
00789             rect->x = (int)sdl.clip.x+(int)sdl.draw.width; rect->y = sdl.clip.y; rect->w = (uint16_t)sdl.clip.x; rect->h = (uint16_t)sdl.draw.height; // right
00790             if ((unsigned int)rect->w > (unsigned int)sdl.overscan_width) { rect->w = (uint16_t)sdl.overscan_width; }
00791             rect = &sdl.updateRects[3];
00792             rect->x = 0; rect->y = (int)sdl.clip.y+(int)sdl.draw.height; rect->w = sdl.draw.width+(unsigned int)(2*sdl.clip.x); rect->h = (uint16_t)sdl.clip.y; // bottom
00793             if ((Bitu)rect->h > (Bitu)sdl.overscan_width) { rect->h = (uint16_t)sdl.overscan_width; }
00794             if ((Bitu)sdl.clip.x > (Bitu)sdl.overscan_width) { rect->x += (int)sdl.clip.x-(int)sdl.overscan_width; rect->w -= (unsigned int)(2*((int)sdl.clip.x-(int)sdl.overscan_width)); }
00795 
00796             if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 8) { // SDL_FillRect seems to have some issues with palettized hw surfaces
00797                 Bit8u* pixelptr = (Bit8u*)sdl.surface->pixels;
00798                 Bitu linepitch = sdl.surface->pitch;
00799                 for (Bitu i=0; i<4; i++) {
00800                     rect = &sdl.updateRects[i];
00801                     Bit8u* start = pixelptr + (unsigned int)rect->y*(unsigned int)linepitch + (unsigned int)rect->x;
00802                     for (Bitu j=0; j<(unsigned int)rect->h; j++) {
00803                         memset(start, vga.attr.overscan_color, rect->w);
00804                         start += linepitch;
00805                     }
00806                 }
00807             } else {
00808                 for (Bitu i=0; i<4; i++)
00809                     SDL_FillRect(sdl.surface, &sdl.updateRects[i], (Uint32)border_color);
00810 
00811 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00812                 SDL_UpdateWindowSurfaceRects(sdl.window, sdl.updateRects, 4);
00813 #else
00814                 SDL_UpdateRects(sdl.surface, 4, sdl.updateRects);
00815 #endif
00816             }
00817         }
00818     }
00819 }

00837 bool is_paused = false;
00838 bool unpause_now = false;

00843 void PushDummySDL(void) {
00844     SDL_Event event;
00845 
00846     memset(&event,0,sizeof(event));
00847     event.type = SDL_KEYUP;
00848     SDL_PushEvent(&event);
00849 }

00851 static void HandleMouseMotion(SDL_MouseMotionEvent * motion);
00852 static void HandleMouseButton(SDL_MouseButtonEvent * button);
00853 
00854 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00855 # if !defined(IGNORE_TOUCHSCREEN)
00856 static void HandleTouchscreenFinger(SDL_TouchFingerEvent * finger);
00857 # endif
00858 #endif
00859 
00860 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00861 static const SDL_TouchID no_touch_id = (SDL_TouchID)(~0ULL);
00862 static const SDL_FingerID no_finger_id = (SDL_FingerID)(~0ULL);
00863 static SDL_FingerID touchscreen_finger_lock = no_finger_id;
00864 static SDL_TouchID touchscreen_touch_lock = no_touch_id;
00865 #endif
00866 
00867 void PauseDOSBoxLoop(Bitu /*unused*/) {
00868     bool paused = true;
00869     SDL_Event event;
00870 
00871     /* reflect in the menu that we're paused now */
00872     mainMenu.get_item("mapper_pause").check(true).refresh_item(mainMenu);
00873 
00874     void MAPPER_ReleaseAllKeys(void);
00875     MAPPER_ReleaseAllKeys();
00876 
00877     GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,true);
00878 //  KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
00879     GFX_LosingFocus();
00880     while (SDL_PollEvent(&event)); // flush event queue.
00881 
00882     // reset pause conditions
00883     pause_on_vsync = false;
00884 
00885     // give mouse to win32 (ex. alt-tab)
00886 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00887     SDL_SetRelativeMouseMode(SDL_FALSE);
00888 #else
00889     SDL_WM_GrabInput(SDL_GRAB_OFF);
00890 #endif
00891 
00892     is_paused = true;
00893 
00894     while (paused) {
00895         if (unpause_now) {
00896             unpause_now = false;
00897             break;
00898         }
00899 
00900 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
00901         emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
00902         SDL_PollEvent(&event);
00903 #else
00904         SDL_WaitEvent(&event);    // since we're not polling, cpu usage drops to 0.
00905 #endif
00906 
00907 #ifdef __WIN32__
00908   #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_HMENU
00909         if (event.type==SDL_SYSWMEVENT && event.syswm.msg->msg == WM_COMMAND && (LOWORD(event.syswm.msg->wParam) == ID_WIN_SYSMENU_PAUSE || LOWORD(event.syswm.msg->wParam) == (mainMenu.get_item("mapper_pause").get_master_id()+DOSBoxMenu::winMenuMinimumID))) {
00910             paused=false;
00911             GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,false);   
00912             break;
00913         }
00914         if (event.type == SDL_SYSWMEVENT && event.syswm.msg->msg == WM_SYSCOMMAND && LOWORD(event.syswm.msg->wParam) == ID_WIN_SYSMENU_PAUSE) {
00915             paused = false;
00916             GFX_SetTitle(-1, -1, -1, false);
00917             break;
00918         }
00919   #endif
00920 #endif
00921         switch (event.type) {
00922 
00923             case SDL_QUIT: KillSwitch(true); break;
00924             case SDL_KEYDOWN:   // Must use Pause/Break or escape Key to resume.
00925             if(event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_PAUSE || event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_ESCAPE) {
00926 
00927                 paused = false;
00928                 GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,false);
00929                 break;
00930             }
00931             else if (event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_SPACE) { /* spacebar = single frame step */
00932                 /* resume, but let the VGA code know to call us on vertical retrace */
00933                 paused = false;
00934                 pause_on_vsync = true;
00935                 GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,false);
00936                 break;
00937             }
00938 #if defined (MACOSX) && !defined(C_SDL2)
00939             if (event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_q && (event.key.keysym.mod == KMOD_RMETA || event.key.keysym.mod == KMOD_LMETA) ) {
00940                 /* On macs, all apps exit when pressing cmd-q */
00941                 KillSwitch(true);
00942                 break;
00943             } 
00944 #endif
00945         case SDL_MOUSEMOTION:
00946 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00947             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == no_finger_id &&
00948                 touchscreen_touch_lock == no_touch_id &&
00949                 event.motion.which != SDL_TOUCH_MOUSEID) { /* don't handle mouse events faked by touchscreen */
00950                 HandleMouseMotion(&event.motion);
00951             }
00952 #else
00953             HandleMouseMotion(&event.motion);
00954 #endif
00955             break;
00956         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN:
00957         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONUP:
00958 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00959             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == no_finger_id &&
00960                 touchscreen_touch_lock == no_touch_id &&
00961                 event.button.which != SDL_TOUCH_MOUSEID) { /* don't handle mouse events faked by touchscreen */
00962                 HandleMouseButton(&event.button);
00963             }
00964 #else
00965             HandleMouseButton(&event.button);
00966 #endif
00967             break;
00968 #if defined(C_SDL2)
00969 # if !defined(IGNORE_TOUCHSCREEN)
00970         case SDL_FINGERDOWN:
00971         case SDL_FINGERUP:
00972         case SDL_FINGERMOTION:
00973             HandleTouchscreenFinger(&event.tfinger);
00974             break;
00975 # endif
00976 #endif
00977         }
00978     }
00979 
00980     // restore mouse state
00981     void GFX_UpdateSDLCaptureState();
00982     GFX_UpdateSDLCaptureState();
00983 
00984     void MAPPER_ReleaseAllKeys(void);
00985     MAPPER_ReleaseAllKeys();
00986 
00987 //  KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
00988     GFX_LosingFocus();
00989 
00990     // redraw screen (ex. fullscreen - pause - alt+tab x2 - unpause)
00991     if (sdl.draw.callback) (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackReset );
00992 
00993     /* reflect in the menu that we're paused now */
00994     mainMenu.get_item("mapper_pause").check(false).refresh_item(mainMenu);
00995 
00996     is_paused = false;
00997 }
00998 
00999 void PauseDOSBox(bool pressed) {
01000     if (pressed) {
01001         if (is_paused) {
01002             unpause_now = true;
01003             PushDummySDL();
01004         }
01005         else {
01006             PIC_AddEvent(PauseDOSBoxLoop,0.001);
01007         }
01008     }
01009 }

01011 #if defined(C_SDL2)
01012 static bool SDL2_resize_enable = false;
01013 
01014 SDL_Window* GFX_GetSDLWindow(void) {
01015     return sdl.window;
01016 }
01017 
01018 SDL_Window* GFX_SetSDLWindowMode(Bit16u width, Bit16u height, SCREEN_TYPES screenType) 
01019 {
01020     static SCREEN_TYPES lastType = SCREEN_SURFACE;
01021     if (sdl.renderer) {
01022         SDL_DestroyRenderer(sdl.renderer);
01023         sdl.renderer=0;
01024     }
01025     if (sdl.texture.pixelFormat) {
01026         SDL_FreeFormat(sdl.texture.pixelFormat);
01027         sdl.texture.pixelFormat = 0;
01028     }
01029     if (sdl.texture.texture) {
01030         SDL_DestroyTexture(sdl.texture.texture);
01031         sdl.texture.texture=0;
01032     }
01033     sdl.window_desired_width = width;
01034     sdl.window_desired_height = height;
01035     int currWidth, currHeight;
01036     if (sdl.window) {
01037         //SDL_GetWindowSize(sdl.window, &currWidth, &currHeight);
01038         if (!sdl.update_window) {
01039             SDL_GetWindowSize(sdl.window, &currWidth, &currHeight);
01040             sdl.update_display_contents = ((width == currWidth) && (height == currHeight));
01041 
01042             currentWindowWidth = currWidth;
01043             currentWindowHeight = currHeight;
01044 
01045             return sdl.window;
01046         }
01047     }
01048 
01049 #if C_OPENGL
01050     if (sdl_opengl.context) {
01051         SDL_GL_DeleteContext(sdl_opengl.context);
01052         sdl_opengl.context=0;
01053     }
01054 #endif
01055 
01056     /* If we change screen type, recreate the window. Furthermore, if
01057      * it is our very first time then we simply create a new window.
01058      */
01059     if (!sdl.window
01060             || (lastType != screenType)
01061 //          || (currWidth != width) || (currHeight != height)
01062 //          || (glwindow != (0 != (SDL_GetWindowFlags(sdl.window) & SDL_WINDOW_OPENGL)))
01063 //          || (fullscreen && (0 == (SDL_GetWindowFlags(sdl.window) & SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN)))
01064 //          || (fullscreen != (SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN == (SDL_GetWindowFlags(sdl.window) & SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN)))
01065 //          || (fullscreen && ((width != currWidth) || (height != currHeight)))
01066        ) {
01067         lastType = screenType;
01068         if (sdl.window) {
01069             SDL_DestroyWindow(sdl.window);
01070         }
01071 
01072         sdl.window = SDL_CreateWindow("",
01073                                       SDL_WINDOWPOS_UNDEFINED_DISPLAY(sdl.displayNumber),
01074                                       SDL_WINDOWPOS_UNDEFINED_DISPLAY(sdl.displayNumber),
01075                                       width, height,
01076                                       (GFX_IsFullscreen() ? (sdl.desktop.full.display_res ? SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN_DESKTOP : SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN) : 0)
01077                                       | ((screenType == SCREEN_OPENGL) ? SDL_WINDOW_OPENGL : 0) | SDL_WINDOW_SHOWN
01078                                       | (SDL2_resize_enable ? SDL_WINDOW_RESIZABLE : 0)
01079                                       | (dpi_aware_enable ? SDL_WINDOW_ALLOW_HIGHDPI : 0));
01080         if (sdl.window) {
01081             GFX_SetTitle(-1, -1, -1, false); //refresh title.
01082         }
01083         sdl.surface = SDL_GetWindowSurface(sdl.window);
01084         SDL_GetWindowSize(sdl.window, &currWidth, &currHeight);
01085         sdl.update_display_contents = ((width == currWidth) && (height == currHeight));
01086 
01087         currentWindowWidth = currWidth;
01088         currentWindowHeight = currHeight;
01089 
01090 #if C_OPENGL
01091         if (screenType == SCREEN_OPENGL) {
01092             sdl_opengl.context = SDL_GL_CreateContext(sdl.window);
01093             if (sdl_opengl.context == NULL) LOG_MSG("WARNING: SDL2 unable to create GL context");
01094             if (SDL_GL_MakeCurrent(sdl.window, sdl_opengl.context) != 0) LOG_MSG("WARNING: SDL2 unable to make current GL context");
01095         }
01096 #endif
01097 
01098         return sdl.window;
01099     }
01100     /* Fullscreen mode switching has its limits, and is also problematic on
01101      * some window managers. For now, the following may work up to some
01102      * level. On X11, SDL_VIDEO_X11_LEGACY_FULLSCREEN=1 can also help,
01103      * although it has its own issues.
01104      * Suggestion: Use the desktop res if possible, with output=surface
01105      * if one is not interested in scaling.
01106      * On Android, desktop res is the only way.
01107      */
01108     SDL_SetWindowResizable(sdl.window, SDL2_resize_enable ? SDL_TRUE : SDL_FALSE);
01109     if (GFX_IsFullscreen()) {
01110         SDL_DisplayMode displayMode;
01111         SDL_GetWindowDisplayMode(sdl.window, &displayMode);
01112         displayMode.w = width;
01113         displayMode.h = height;
01114         SDL_SetWindowDisplayMode(sdl.window, &displayMode);
01115 
01116         SDL_SetWindowFullscreen(sdl.window, SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN_DESKTOP);
01117     } else {
01118         SDL_SetWindowFullscreen(sdl.window, 0);
01119 
01120         SDL_SetWindowSize(sdl.window, width, height);
01121     }
01122     /* Maybe some requested fullscreen resolution is unsupported? */
01123     SDL_GetWindowSize(sdl.window, &currWidth, &currHeight);
01124     sdl.update_display_contents = ((width == currWidth) && (height == currHeight));
01125     sdl.surface = SDL_GetWindowSurface(sdl.window);
01126 
01127     currentWindowWidth = currWidth;
01128     currentWindowHeight = currHeight;
01129 
01130 #if C_OPENGL
01131     if (screenType == SCREEN_OPENGL) {
01132         sdl_opengl.context = SDL_GL_CreateContext(sdl.window);
01133         if (sdl_opengl.context == NULL) LOG_MSG("WARNING: SDL2 unable to create GL context");
01134         if (SDL_GL_MakeCurrent(sdl.window, sdl_opengl.context) != 0) LOG_MSG("WARNING: SDL2 unable to make current GL context");
01135     }
01136 #endif
01137 
01138     return sdl.window;
01139 }
01140 
01141 void GFX_SetResizeable(bool enable) {
01142     if (SDL2_resize_enable != enable) {
01143         SDL2_resize_enable = enable;
01144 
01145         if (sdl.window != NULL)
01146             SDL_SetWindowResizable(sdl.window, SDL2_resize_enable ? SDL_TRUE : SDL_FALSE);
01147     }
01148 }

01150 // Used for the mapper UI and more: Creates a fullscreen window with desktop res
01151 // on Android, and a non-fullscreen window with the input dimensions otherwise.
01152 SDL_Window * GFX_SetSDLSurfaceWindow(Bit16u width, Bit16u height) {
01153     return GFX_SetSDLWindowMode(width, height, SCREEN_SURFACE);
01154 }

01156 // Returns the rectangle in the current window to be used for scaling a
01157 // sub-window with the given dimensions, like the mapper UI.
01158 SDL_Rect GFX_GetSDLSurfaceSubwindowDims(Bit16u width, Bit16u height) {
01159     SDL_Rect rect;
01160     rect.x=rect.y=0;
01161     rect.w=width;
01162     rect.h=height;
01163     return rect;
01164 }

01166 # if !defined(C_SDL2)
01167 // Currently used for an initial test here

01183 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
01184 /* Reset the screen with current values in the sdl structure */
01185 Bitu GFX_GetBestMode(Bitu flags) 
01186 {
01187     Bitu retFlags = 0;
01188 
01189     switch (sdl.desktop.want_type) 
01190     {
01191         case SCREEN_SURFACE:
01192             retFlags = OUTPUT_SURFACE_GetBestMode(flags);
01193             break;
01194 
01195 #if C_OPENGL
01196         case SCREEN_OPENGL:
01197             retFlags = OUTPUT_OPENGL_GetBestMode(flags);
01198             break;
01199 #endif
01200 
01201 #if C_DIRECT3D
01202         case SCREEN_DIRECT3D:
01203             retFlags = OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_GetBestMode(flags);
01204             break;
01205 #endif
01206 
01207         default:
01208             // we should never reach here
01209             retFlags = 0;
01210             break;
01211     }
01212 
01213     if (!retFlags)
01214     {
01215         if (sdl.desktop.want_type != SCREEN_SURFACE)
01216         {
01217             // try falling back down to surface
01218             OUTPUT_SURFACE_Select();
01219             retFlags = OUTPUT_SURFACE_GetBestMode(flags);
01220         }
01221         if (retFlags == 0)
01222             LOG_MSG("SDL:Failed everything including falling back to surface GFX_GetBestMode"); // completely failed it seems
01223     }
01224 
01225     return retFlags;
01226 }
01227 #endif

01229 /* FIXME: This prepares the SDL library to accept Win32 drag+drop events from the Windows shell.
01230  *        So it should be named something like EnableDragAcceptFiles() not SDL_Prepare() */
01231 void SDL_Prepare(void) {
01232     if (menu_compatible) return;
01233 
01234 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS) // Microsoft Windows specific
01235     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Win32: Preparing main window to accept files dragged in from the Windows shell");
01236 
01237     SDL_PumpEvents(); SDL_EventState(SDL_SYSWMEVENT, SDL_ENABLE);
01238     DragAcceptFiles(GetHWND(), TRUE);
01239 #endif
01240 }

01242 void GFX_ForceRedrawScreen(void) {
01243     GFX_Stop();
01244     if (sdl.draw.callback)
01245         (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackReset );
01246     GFX_Start();
01247 }

01249 void GFX_ResetScreen(void) {
01250     fullscreen_switch=false; 
01251     GFX_Stop();
01252     if (sdl.draw.callback)
01253         (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackReset );
01254     GFX_Start();
01255     CPU_Reset_AutoAdjust();
01256     fullscreen_switch=true;
01257 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
01258     if (!sdl.desktop.fullscreen) DOSBox_RefreshMenu(); // for menu
01259 #endif
01260 }

01262 void GFX_ForceFullscreenExit(void) {
01263     if (sdl.desktop.lazy_fullscreen) {
01264         LOG_MSG("GFX LF: invalid screen change");
01265     } else {
01266         sdl.desktop.fullscreen=false;
01267         GFX_ResetScreen();
01268     }
01269 }

01285 void GFX_LogSDLState(void) 
01286 {
01287     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("SDL video mode: %ux%u (clip %ux%u with upper-left at %ux%u) %ubpp",
01288         (unsigned)sdl.surface->w,(unsigned)sdl.surface->h,
01289         (unsigned)sdl.clip.w,(unsigned)sdl.clip.h,
01290         (unsigned)sdl.clip.x,(unsigned)sdl.clip.y,
01291         (unsigned)sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel);
01292     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("   red: shift=%u mask=0x%08lx",
01293         (unsigned)sdl.surface->format->Rshift,
01294         (unsigned long)sdl.surface->format->Rmask);
01295     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("   green: shift=%u mask=0x%08lx",
01296         (unsigned)sdl.surface->format->Gshift,
01297         (unsigned long)sdl.surface->format->Gmask);
01298     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("   blue: shift=%u mask=0x%08lx",
01299         (unsigned)sdl.surface->format->Bshift,
01300         (unsigned long)sdl.surface->format->Bmask);
01301     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("   alpha: shift=%u mask=0x%08lx",
01302         (unsigned)sdl.surface->format->Ashift,
01303         (unsigned long)sdl.surface->format->Amask);
01304 
01305     GFX_bpp = sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel;
01306     GFX_Rmask = sdl.surface->format->Rmask;
01307     GFX_Rshift = sdl.surface->format->Rshift;
01308     GFX_Gmask = sdl.surface->format->Gmask;
01309     GFX_Gshift = sdl.surface->format->Gshift;
01310     GFX_Bmask = sdl.surface->format->Bmask;
01311     GFX_Bshift = sdl.surface->format->Bshift;
01312     GFX_Amask = sdl.surface->format->Amask;
01313     GFX_Ashift = sdl.surface->format->Ashift;

01318         GFX_EndUpdate( 0 );

01326 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW
01327 void MenuShadeRect(int x,int y,int w,int h) {
01328     if (OpenGL_using()) {
01329 #if C_OPENGL
01330         glShadeModel (GL_FLAT);
01331         glBlendFunc(GL_ONE, GL_SRC_ALPHA);
01332         glDisable (GL_DEPTH_TEST);
01333         glDisable (GL_LIGHTING);
01334         glEnable(GL_BLEND);
01335         glDisable(GL_CULL_FACE);
01336         glDisable(GL_ALPHA_TEST);
01337         glDisable(GL_FOG);
01338         glDisable(GL_SCISSOR_TEST);
01339         glDisable(GL_STENCIL_TEST);
01340         glDisable(GL_TEXTURE_2D);
01341 
01342         glColor4ub(0, 0, 0, 64);
01343         glBegin(GL_QUADS);
01344         glVertex2i(x  ,y  );
01345         glVertex2i(x+w,y  );
01346         glVertex2i(x+w,y+h);
01347         glVertex2i(x  ,y+h);
01348         glEnd();
01349 
01350         glBlendFunc(GL_ONE, GL_ZERO);
01351         glEnable(GL_TEXTURE_2D);
01352 #endif
01353     }
01354     else {
01355         if (x < 0) {
01356             w += x;
01357             x = 0;
01358         }
01359         if (y < 0) {
01360             y += h;
01361             y = 0;
01362         }
01363         if ((x+w) > sdl.surface->w)
01364             w = sdl.surface->w - x;
01365         if ((y+h) > sdl.surface->h)
01366             h = sdl.surface->h - y;
01367         if (w <= 0 || h <= 0)
01368             return;
01369 
01370         if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 32) {
01371             unsigned char *scan;
01372             uint32_t *row,mask;
01373 
01374             mask = ((sdl.surface->format->Rmask >> 2) & sdl.surface->format->Rmask) |
01375                 ((sdl.surface->format->Gmask >> 2) & sdl.surface->format->Gmask) |
01376                 ((sdl.surface->format->Bmask >> 2) & sdl.surface->format->Bmask);
01377 
01378             assert(sdl.surface->pixels != NULL);
01379 
01380             scan  = (unsigned char*)sdl.surface->pixels;
01381             scan += y * sdl.surface->pitch;
01382             scan += x * 4;
01383             while (h-- > 0) {
01384                 row = (uint32_t*)scan;
01385                 scan += sdl.surface->pitch;
01386                 for (unsigned int c=0;c < (unsigned int)w;c++) row[c] = (row[c] >> 2) & mask;
01387             }
01388         }
01389         else if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 16) {
01390             unsigned char *scan;
01391             uint16_t *row,mask;
01392 
01393             mask = ((sdl.surface->format->Rmask >> 2) & sdl.surface->format->Rmask) |
01394                 ((sdl.surface->format->Gmask >> 2) & sdl.surface->format->Gmask) |
01395                 ((sdl.surface->format->Bmask >> 2) & sdl.surface->format->Bmask);
01396 
01397             assert(sdl.surface->pixels != NULL);
01398 
01399             scan  = (unsigned char*)sdl.surface->pixels;
01400             scan += y * sdl.surface->pitch;
01401             scan += x * 2;
01402             while (h-- > 0) {
01403                 row = (uint16_t*)scan;
01404                 scan += sdl.surface->pitch;
01405                 for (unsigned int c=0;c < (unsigned int)w;c++) row[c] = (row[c] >> 2) & mask;
01406             }
01407         }
01408         else {
01409             /* TODO */
01410         }
01411     }
01412 }
01413 
01414 void MenuDrawRect(int x,int y,int w,int h,Bitu color) {
01415     if (OpenGL_using()) {
01416 #if C_OPENGL
01417         glShadeModel (GL_FLAT);
01418         glBlendFunc(GL_ONE, GL_ZERO);
01419         glDisable (GL_DEPTH_TEST);
01420         glDisable (GL_LIGHTING);
01421         glDisable(GL_BLEND);
01422         glDisable(GL_CULL_FACE);
01423         glDisable(GL_ALPHA_TEST);
01424         glDisable(GL_FOG);
01425         glDisable(GL_SCISSOR_TEST);
01426         glDisable(GL_STENCIL_TEST);
01427         glDisable(GL_TEXTURE_2D);
01428 
01429         glColor3ub((color >> 16UL) & 0xFF,(color >> 8UL) & 0xFF,(color >> 0UL) & 0xFF);
01430         glBegin(GL_QUADS);
01431         glVertex2i(x  ,y  );
01432         glVertex2i(x+w,y  );
01433         glVertex2i(x+w,y+h);
01434         glVertex2i(x  ,y+h);
01435         glEnd();
01436 
01437         glBlendFunc(GL_ONE, GL_ZERO);
01438         glEnable(GL_TEXTURE_2D);
01439 #endif
01440     }
01441     else {
01442         if (x < 0) {
01443             w += x;
01444             x = 0;
01445         }
01446         if (y < 0) {
01447             y += h;
01448             y = 0;
01449         }
01450         if ((x+w) > sdl.surface->w)
01451             w = sdl.surface->w - x;
01452         if ((y+h) > sdl.surface->h)
01453             h = sdl.surface->h - y;
01454         if (w <= 0 || h <= 0)
01455             return;
01456 
01457         if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 32) {
01458             unsigned char *scan;
01459             uint32_t *row;
01460 
01461             assert(sdl.surface->pixels != NULL);
01462 
01463             scan  = (unsigned char*)sdl.surface->pixels;
01464             scan += y * sdl.surface->pitch;
01465             scan += x * 4;
01466             while (h-- > 0) {
01467                 row = (uint32_t*)scan;
01468                 scan += sdl.surface->pitch;
01469                 for (unsigned int c=0;c < (unsigned int)w;c++) row[c] = (uint32_t)color;
01470             }
01471         }
01472         else if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 16) {
01473             unsigned char *scan;
01474             uint16_t *row;
01475 
01476             assert(sdl.surface->pixels != NULL);
01477 
01478             scan  = (unsigned char*)sdl.surface->pixels;
01479             scan += y * sdl.surface->pitch;
01480             scan += x * 2;
01481             while (h-- > 0) {
01482                 row = (uint16_t*)scan;
01483                 scan += sdl.surface->pitch;
01484                 for (unsigned int c=0;c < (unsigned int)w;c++) row[c] = (uint16_t)color;
01485             }
01486         }
01487         else {
01488             /* TODO */
01489         }
01490     }
01491 }
01492 
01493 extern Bit8u int10_font_14[256 * 14];
01494 extern Bit8u int10_font_16[256 * 16];
01495 
01496 void MenuDrawTextChar(int x,int y,unsigned char c,Bitu color) {
01497     static const unsigned int fontHeight = 16;
01498 
01499     if (x < 0 || y < 0 ||
01500         (unsigned int)(x+8) > (unsigned int)sdl.surface->w ||
01501         (unsigned int)(y+(int)fontHeight) > (unsigned int)sdl.surface->h)
01502         return;
01503 
01504     unsigned char *bmp = (unsigned char*)int10_font_16 + (c * fontHeight);
01505 
01506     if (OpenGL_using()) {
01507 #if C_OPENGL
01508         unsigned int tx = (c % 16u) * 8u;
01509         unsigned int ty = (c / 16u) * 16u;
01510 
01511         /* MenuDrawText() has prepared OpenGL state for us */
01512         glBegin(GL_QUADS);
01513         // lower left
01514         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+0,    (int)ty                ); glVertex2i((int)x,  (int)y                );
01515         // lower right
01516         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+8,    (int)ty                ); glVertex2i((int)x+8,(int)y                );
01517         // upper right
01518         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+8,    (int)ty+(int)fontHeight); glVertex2i((int)x+8,(int)y+(int)fontHeight);
01519         // upper left
01520         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+0,    (int)ty+(int)fontHeight); glVertex2i((int)x,  (int)y+(int)fontHeight);
01521         glEnd();
01522 #endif
01523     }
01524     else {
01525         unsigned char *scan;
01526 
01527         assert(sdl.surface->pixels != NULL);
01528 
01529         if (x < 0 || y < 0)
01530             return;
01531         if ((x + 8) > sdl.surface->w)
01532             return;
01533         if ((y + (int)fontHeight) > sdl.surface->h)
01534             return;
01535 
01536         scan  = (unsigned char*)sdl.surface->pixels;
01537         scan += (unsigned int)y * (unsigned int)sdl.surface->pitch;
01538         scan += (unsigned int)x * (((unsigned int)sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel+7u)/8u);
01539 
01540         for (unsigned int row=0;row < fontHeight;row++) {
01541             unsigned char rb = bmp[row];
01542 
01543             if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 32) {
01544                 uint32_t *dp = (uint32_t*)scan;
01545                 for (unsigned int colm=0x80;colm != 0;colm >>= 1) {
01546                     if (rb & colm) *dp = (uint32_t)color;
01547                     dp++;
01548                 }
01549             }
01550             else if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 16) {
01551                 uint16_t *dp = (uint16_t*)scan;
01552                 for (unsigned int colm=0x80;colm != 0;colm >>= 1) {
01553                     if (rb & colm) *dp = (uint16_t)color;
01554                     dp++;
01555                 }
01556             }
01557 
01558             scan += (size_t)sdl.surface->pitch;
01559         }
01560     }
01561 }
01562 
01563 void MenuDrawTextChar2x(int x,int y,unsigned char c,Bitu color) {
01564     static const unsigned int fontHeight = 16;
01565 
01566     if (x < 0 || y < 0 ||
01567         (unsigned int)(x+8) > (unsigned int)sdl.surface->w ||
01568         (unsigned int)(y+(int)fontHeight) > (unsigned int)sdl.surface->h)
01569         return;
01570 
01571     unsigned char *bmp = (unsigned char*)int10_font_16 + (c * fontHeight);
01572 
01573     if (OpenGL_using()) {
01574 #if C_OPENGL
01575         unsigned int tx = (c % 16u) * 8u;
01576         unsigned int ty = (c / 16u) * 16u;
01577 
01578         /* MenuDrawText() has prepared OpenGL state for us */
01579         glBegin(GL_QUADS);
01580         // lower left
01581         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+0,    (int)ty                ); glVertex2i(x,      y                    );
01582         // lower right
01583         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+8,    (int)ty                ); glVertex2i(x+(8*2),y                    );
01584         // upper right
01585         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+8,    (int)ty+(int)fontHeight); glVertex2i(x+(8*2),y+((int)fontHeight*2));
01586         // upper left
01587         glTexCoord2i((int)tx+0,    (int)ty+(int)fontHeight); glVertex2i(x,      y+((int)fontHeight*2));
01588         glEnd();
01589 #endif
01590     }
01591     else { 
01592         unsigned char *scan;
01593 
01594         assert(sdl.surface->pixels != NULL);
01595 
01596         if (x < 0 || y < 0)
01597             return;
01598         if ((x + 16) > sdl.surface->w)
01599             return;
01600         if ((y + ((int)fontHeight * 2)) > sdl.surface->h)
01601             return;
01602 
01603         scan  = (unsigned char*)sdl.surface->pixels;
01604         scan += y * sdl.surface->pitch;
01605         scan += x * ((sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel+7)/8);
01606 
01607         for (unsigned int row=0;row < (fontHeight*2);row++) {
01608             unsigned char rb = bmp[row>>1U];
01609 
01610             if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 32) {
01611                 uint32_t *dp = (uint32_t*)scan;
01612                 for (unsigned int colm=0x80;colm != 0;colm >>= 1) {
01613                     if (rb & colm) {
01614                         *dp++ = (uint32_t)color;
01615                         *dp++ = (uint32_t)color;
01616                     }
01617                     else {
01618                         dp += 2;
01619                     }
01620                 }
01621             }
01622             else if (sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel == 16) {
01623                 uint16_t *dp = (uint16_t*)scan;
01624                 for (unsigned int colm=0x80;colm != 0;colm >>= 1) {
01625                     if (rb & colm) {
01626                         *dp++ = (uint16_t)color;
01627                         *dp++ = (uint16_t)color;
01628                     }
01629                     else {
01630                         dp += 2;
01631                     }
01632                 }
01633             }
01634 
01635             scan += sdl.surface->pitch;
01636         }
01637     }
01638 }
01639 
01640 void MenuDrawText(int x,int y,const char *text,Bitu color) {
01641 #if C_OPENGL
01642     if (OpenGL_using()) {
01643         glBindTexture(GL_TEXTURE_2D,SDLDrawGenFontTexture);
01644 
01645         glPushMatrix();
01646 
01647         glMatrixMode (GL_TEXTURE);
01648         glLoadIdentity ();
01649         glScaled(1.0 / SDLDrawGenFontTextureWidth, 1.0 / SDLDrawGenFontTextureHeight, 1.0);
01650 
01651         glColor4ub((color >> 16UL) & 0xFF,(color >> 8UL) & 0xFF,(color >> 0UL) & 0xFF,0xFF);
01652         glTexEnvi(GL_TEXTURE_ENV, GL_TEXTURE_ENV_MODE, GL_MODULATE);
01653 
01654         glBlendFunc(GL_SRC_ALPHA, GL_ONE_MINUS_SRC_ALPHA);
01655         glEnable(GL_TEXTURE_2D);
01656         glEnable(GL_ALPHA_TEST);
01657         glEnable(GL_BLEND);
01658     }
01659 #endif
01660 
01661     while (*text != 0) {
01662         if (mainMenu.fontCharScale >= 2)
01663             MenuDrawTextChar2x(x,y,(unsigned char)(*text++),color);
01664         else
01665             MenuDrawTextChar(x,y,(unsigned char)(*text++),color);
01666 
01667         x += (int)mainMenu.fontCharWidth;
01668     }
01669 
01670 #if C_OPENGL
01671     if (OpenGL_using()) {
01672         glTexEnvi (GL_TEXTURE_ENV, GL_TEXTURE_ENV_MODE, GL_REPLACE);
01673         glBlendFunc(GL_ONE, GL_ZERO);
01674         glDisable(GL_ALPHA_TEST);
01675         glEnable(GL_TEXTURE_2D);
01676 
01677         glPopMatrix();
01678 
01679         glBindTexture(GL_TEXTURE_2D,sdl_opengl.texture);
01680     }
01681 #endif
01682 }
01683 
01684 void DOSBoxMenu::item::drawMenuItem(DOSBoxMenu &menu) {
01685     (void)menu;//UNUSED
01686 
01687     Bitu bgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(63, 63, 63);
01688     Bitu fgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(191, 191, 191);
01689     Bitu fgshortcolor = GFX_GetRGB(127, 127, 191);
01690     Bitu fgcheckcolor = GFX_GetRGB(191, 191, 127);
01691 
01692     if (type >= separator_type_id) {
01693         /* separators never change visual state on hover/select */
01694     }
01695     else if (!status.enabled) {
01696         if (itemHover)
01697             bgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(79, 79, 79);
01698 
01699         fgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(144, 144, 144);
01700         fgshortcolor = GFX_GetRGB(63, 63, 144);
01701         fgcheckcolor = GFX_GetRGB(144, 144, 63);
01702     }
01703     else if (itemHilight) {
01704         bgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(0, 0, 63);
01705         fgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(255, 255, 255);
01706         fgshortcolor = GFX_GetRGB(191, 191, 255);
01707     }
01708     else if (itemHover) {
01709         bgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(127, 127, 127);
01710         fgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(255, 255, 255);
01711         fgshortcolor = GFX_GetRGB(191, 191, 255);
01712     }
01713 
01714     itemHoverDrawn = itemHover;
01715     itemHilightDrawn = itemHilight;
01716 
01717     if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
01718         SDL_LockSurface(sdl.surface);
01719 
01720     MenuDrawRect(screenBox.x, screenBox.y, screenBox.w, screenBox.h, bgcolor);
01721     if (checkBox.w != 0 && checkBox.h != 0) {
01722         const char *str = status.checked ? "\xFB" : " ";
01723 
01724         MenuDrawText(screenBox.x+checkBox.x, screenBox.y+checkBox.y, str, fgcheckcolor);
01725     }
01726     if (textBox.w != 0 && textBox.h != 0)
01727         MenuDrawText(screenBox.x+textBox.x, screenBox.y+textBox.y, text.c_str(), fgcolor);
01728     if (shortBox.w != 0 && shortBox.h != 0)
01729         MenuDrawText(screenBox.x+shortBox.x, screenBox.y+shortBox.y, shortcut_text.c_str(), fgshortcolor);
01730 
01731     if (type == submenu_type_id && borderTop/*not toplevel*/)
01732         MenuDrawText((int)((int)screenBox.x+(int)screenBox.w - (int)mainMenu.fontCharWidth - 1), (int)((int)screenBox.y+(int)textBox.y), "\x10", fgcheckcolor);
01733 
01734     if (type == separator_type_id)
01735         MenuDrawRect((int)screenBox.x, (int)screenBox.y + ((int)screenBox.h/2), (int)screenBox.w, 1, fgcolor);
01736     else if (type == vseparator_type_id)
01737         MenuDrawRect((int)screenBox.x + ((int)screenBox.w/2), (int)screenBox.y, 1, (int)screenBox.h, fgcolor);
01738 
01739     if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
01740         SDL_UnlockSurface(sdl.surface);
01741 }
01742 
01743 void DOSBoxMenu::displaylist::DrawDisplayList(DOSBoxMenu &menu,bool updateScreen) {
01744     for (auto &id : disp_list) {
01745         DOSBoxMenu::item &item = menu.get_item(id);
01746 
01747         item.drawMenuItem(menu);
01748         if (updateScreen) item.updateScreenFromItem(menu);
01749     }
01750 }

01752 bool DOSBox_isMenuVisible(void);
01753 
01754 void GFX_DrawSDLMenu(DOSBoxMenu &menu, DOSBoxMenu::displaylist &dl) {
01755     if (!menu.needsRedraw() || (sdl.updating && !OpenGL_using())) {
01756         return;
01757     }
01758     if (!DOSBox_isMenuVisible() || sdl.desktop.fullscreen) {
01759         // BUGFIX: If the menu is hidden then silently clear "needs redraw" to avoid excess redraw of nothing
01760         menu.clearRedraw();
01761         return;
01762     }
01763 
01764     bool mustLock = !OpenGL_using() && SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface);
01765 
01766     if (mustLock) {
01767         SDL_LockSurface(sdl.surface);
01768     }
01769 
01770     if (&dl == &menu.display_list) { /* top level menu, draw background */
01771         MenuDrawRect(menu.menuBox.x, menu.menuBox.y, menu.menuBox.w, menu.menuBox.h - 1, GFX_GetRGB(63, 63, 63));
01772         MenuDrawRect(menu.menuBox.x, menu.menuBox.y + menu.menuBox.h - 1, menu.menuBox.w, 1,
01773                      GFX_GetRGB(31, 31, 31));
01774     }
01775 
01776     if (mustLock) {
01777         SDL_UnlockSurface(sdl.surface);
01778     }
01779 
01780 #if 0
01781     LOG_MSG("menudraw %u",(unsigned int)SDL_GetTicks());
01782 #endif
01783 
01784     menu.clearRedraw();
01785     menu.display_list.DrawDisplayList(menu,/*updateScreen*/false);
01786 
01787     if (!OpenGL_using()) {
01788 #if defined(C_SDL2)
01789         SDL_UpdateWindowSurfaceRects( sdl.window, &menu.menuBox, 1 );
01790 #else
01791         SDL_UpdateRects(sdl.surface, 1, &menu.menuBox);
01792 #endif
01793     }
01794 }
01795 #endif

01797 void RENDER_Reset(void);
01798 
01799 Bitu GFX_SetSize(Bitu width, Bitu height, Bitu flags, double scalex, double scaley, GFX_CallBack_t callback) 
01800 {
01801     if (width == 0 || height == 0) {
01802         E_Exit("GFX_SetSize with width=%d height=%d zero dimensions not allowed",(int)width,(int)height);
01803         return 0;
01804     }
01805 
01806     if (sdl.updating)
01807         GFX_EndUpdate( 0 );
01808 
01809     sdl.must_redraw_all = true;
01810 
01811     sdl.draw.width = (Bit32u)width;
01812     sdl.draw.height = (Bit32u)height;
01813     sdl.draw.flags = flags;
01814     sdl.draw.callback = callback;
01815     sdl.draw.scalex = scalex;
01816     sdl.draw.scaley = scaley;
01817 
01818     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("GFX_SetSize %ux%u flags=0x%x scale=%.3fx%.3f",
01819         (unsigned int)width,(unsigned int)height,
01820         (unsigned int)flags,
01821         scalex,scaley);
01822 
01823 //    Bitu bpp = 0;
01824     Bitu retFlags = 0;
01825 
01826     if (sdl.blit.surface) {
01827         SDL_FreeSurface(sdl.blit.surface);
01828         sdl.blit.surface=0;
01829     }
01830 
01831     switch (sdl.desktop.want_type) {
01832         case SCREEN_SURFACE:
01833             retFlags = OUTPUT_SURFACE_SetSize();
01834             break;
01835 
01836 #if C_OPENGL
01837         case SCREEN_OPENGL:
01838             retFlags = OUTPUT_OPENGL_SetSize();
01839             break;
01840 #endif
01841 
01842 #if C_DIRECT3D
01843         case SCREEN_DIRECT3D: 
01844             retFlags = OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_SetSize();
01845             break;
01846 #endif
01847 
01848         default:
01849             // we should never reach here
01850             retFlags = 0;
01851             break;
01852     }
01853 
01854     if (!retFlags)
01855     {
01856         if (sdl.desktop.want_type != SCREEN_SURFACE)
01857         {
01858             // try falling back down to surface
01859             OUTPUT_SURFACE_Select();
01860             retFlags = OUTPUT_SURFACE_SetSize();
01861         }
01862         if (retFlags == 0)
01863             LOG_MSG("SDL:Failed everything including falling back to surface in GFX_GetSize"); // completely failed it seems
01864     }
01865 
01866     // we have selected an actual desktop type
01867     sdl.desktop.type = sdl.desktop.want_type;
01868 
01869     GFX_LogSDLState();
01870 
01871     if (retFlags) 
01872         GFX_Start();
01873 
01874     if (!sdl.mouse.autoenable && !sdl.mouse.locked)
01875         SDL_ShowCursor(sdl.mouse.autolock?SDL_DISABLE:SDL_ENABLE);
01876 
01877     UpdateWindowDimensions();
01878 
01879 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
01880     WindowsTaskbarUpdatePreviewRegion();
01881 #endif
01882 
01883     return retFlags;
01884 }
01885 
01886 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
01887 // WARNING: Not recommended, there is danger you cannot exit emulator because mouse+keyboard are taken
01888 static bool enable_hook_everything = false;
01889 #endif
01890 
01891 // Whether or not to hook the keyboard and block special keys.
01892 // Setting this is recommended so that your keyboard is fully usable in the guest OS when you
01893 // enable the mouse+keyboard capture. But hooking EVERYTHING is not recommended because there is a
01894 // danger you become trapped in the DOSBox emulator!
01895 static bool enable_hook_special_keys = true;
01896 
01897 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
01898 // Whether or not to hook Num/Scroll/Caps lock in order to give the guest OS full control of the
01899 // LEDs on the keyboard (i.e. the LEDs do not change until the guest OS changes their state).
01900 // This flag also enables code to set the LEDs to guest state when setting mouse+keyboard capture,
01901 // and restoring LED state when releasing capture.
01902 static bool enable_hook_lock_toggle_keys = true;
01903 #endif
01904 
01905 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS)
01906 // and this is where we store host LED state when capture is set.
01907 static bool on_capture_num_lock_was_on = true; // reasonable guess
01908 static bool on_capture_scroll_lock_was_on = false;
01909 static bool on_capture_caps_lock_was_on = false;
01910 #endif
01911 
01912 static bool exthook_enabled = false;
01913 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS)
01914 static HHOOK exthook_winhook = NULL;
01915 
01916 #if !defined(__MINGW32__)
01917 extern "C" void SDL_DOSBox_X_Hack_Set_Toggle_Key_WM_USER_Hack(unsigned char x);
01918 #endif
01919 
01920 static LRESULT CALLBACK WinExtHookKeyboardHookProc(int nCode,WPARAM wParam,LPARAM lParam) {
01921     if (nCode == HC_ACTION) {
01922         HWND myHwnd = GetHWND();
01923 
01924         if (exthook_enabled && GetFocus() == myHwnd) { /* intercept only if DOSBox-X is the focus and the keyboard is hooked */
01925             if (wParam == WM_SYSKEYDOWN || wParam == WM_KEYDOWN || wParam == WM_SYSKEYUP || wParam == WM_KEYUP) {
01926                 KBDLLHOOKSTRUCT *st_hook = (KBDLLHOOKSTRUCT*)lParam;
01927 
01928                 if (st_hook->flags & LLKHF_INJECTED) {
01929                     // injected keys are automatically allowed, especially if we are injecting keyboard input into ourself
01930                     // to control Num/Scroll/Caps Lock LEDs. If we don't check this we cannot control the LEDs. Injecting
01931                     // keydown/keyup for Num Lock is the only means provided by Windows to control those LEDs.
01932                 }
01933                 else if (st_hook->vkCode == VK_MENU/*alt*/ || st_hook->vkCode == VK_CONTROL ||
01934                     st_hook->vkCode == VK_LSHIFT || st_hook->vkCode == VK_RSHIFT) {
01935                     // always allow modifier keys through, so other applications are not left with state inconsistent from
01936                     // actual keyboard state.
01937                 }
01938                 else {
01939                     bool nopass = enable_hook_everything; // if the user wants us to hook ALL keys then that's where this signals it
01940                     bool alternate_message = false; // send as WM_USER+0x100 instead of WM_KEYDOWN
01941 
01942                     if (!nopass) {
01943                         // hook only certain keys Windows is likely to act on by itself.
01944 
01945                         // FIXME: Hooking the keyboard does NOT prevent Fn+SPACE (zoom) from triggering screen resolution
01946                         //        changes in Windows 10! How do we stop that?
01947 
01948                         // FIXME: It might be nice to let the user decide whether or not Print Screen is intercepted.
01949 
01950                         // TODO: We do not hook the volume up/down/mute keys. This is to be kind to the user. They may
01951                         // appreciate the ability to dial down the volume if a loud DOS program comes up. But
01952                         // if the user WANTS us to, we should allow hooking those keys.
01953 
01954                         // TODO: Allow (if instructed) hooking the VK_SLEEP key so pushing the sleep key (the
01955                         // one with the icon of the moon on Microsoft keyboards) can be sent instead to the
01956                         // guest OS. Also add code where if we're not hooking the key, then we should listen
01957                         // for signals the guest OS is suspending or hibernating and auto-disconnect the
01958                         // mouse capture and keyboard hook.
01959 
01960                         switch (st_hook->vkCode) {
01961                         case VK_LWIN:   // left Windows key (normally triggers Start menu)
01962                         case VK_RWIN:   // right Windows key (normally triggers Start menu)
01963                         case VK_APPS:   // Application key (normally open to the user, but just in case)
01964                         case VK_PAUSE:  // pause key
01965                         case VK_SNAPSHOT: // print screen
01966                         case VK_TAB:    // try to catch ALT+TAB too (not blocking VK_TAB will allow host OS to switch tasks)
01967                         case VK_ESCAPE: // try to catch CTRL+ESC as well (so Windows 95 Start Menu is accessible)
01968                         case VK_SPACE:  // and space (catching VK_ZOOM isn't enough to prevent Windows 10 from changing res)
01969                         // these keys have no meaning to DOSBox and so we hook them by default to allow the guest OS to use them
01970                         case VK_BROWSER_BACK: // Browser Back key
01971                         case VK_BROWSER_FORWARD: // Browser Forward key
01972                         case VK_BROWSER_REFRESH: // Browser Refresh key
01973                         case VK_BROWSER_STOP: // Browser Stop key
01974                         case VK_BROWSER_SEARCH: // Browser Search key
01975                         case VK_BROWSER_FAVORITES: // Browser Favorites key
01976                         case VK_BROWSER_HOME: // Browser Start and Home key
01977                         case VK_MEDIA_NEXT_TRACK: // Next Track key
01978                         case VK_MEDIA_PREV_TRACK: // Previous Track key
01979                         case VK_MEDIA_STOP: // Stop Media key
01980                         case VK_MEDIA_PLAY_PAUSE: // Play / Pause Media key
01981                         case VK_LAUNCH_MAIL: // Start Mail key
01982                         case VK_LAUNCH_MEDIA_SELECT: // Select Media key
01983                         case VK_LAUNCH_APP1: // Start Application 1 key
01984                         case VK_LAUNCH_APP2: // Start Application 2 key
01985                         case VK_PLAY: // Play key
01986                         case VK_ZOOM: // Zoom key (the (+) magnifying glass keyboard shortcut laptops have these days on the spacebar?)
01987                             nopass = true;
01988                             break;
01989 
01990                             // IME Hiragana key, otherwise inaccessible to us
01991                         case 0xF2:
01992                             nopass = true; // FIXME: This doesn't (yet) cause a SDL key event.
01993                             break;
01994 
01995                             // we allow hooking Num/Scroll/Caps Lock keys so that pressing them does not toggle the LED.
01996                             // we then take Num/Scroll/Caps LED state from the guest and let THAT control the LED state.
01997                         case VK_CAPITAL:
01998                         case VK_NUMLOCK:
01999                         case VK_SCROLL:
02000                             nopass = enable_hook_lock_toggle_keys;
02001                             alternate_message = true;
02002                             break;
02003                         }
02004                     }
02005 
02006                     if (nopass) {
02007                         // convert WM_KEYDOWN/WM_KEYUP if obfuscating the message to distinguish between real and injected events
02008                         if (alternate_message) {
02009                             if (wParam == WM_KEYDOWN || wParam == WM_SYSKEYDOWN)
02010                                 wParam = WM_USER + 0x100;
02011                             else if (wParam == WM_KEYUP || wParam == WM_SYSKEYUP)
02012                                 wParam = WM_USER + 0x101;
02013                         }
02014 
02015                         DWORD lParam =
02016                             (st_hook->scanCode << 8U) +
02017                             ((st_hook->flags & LLKHF_EXTENDED) ? 0x01000000 : 0) +
02018                             ((wParam == WM_KEYUP || wParam == WM_SYSKEYUP) ? 0xC0000000 : 0);
02019 
02020                         // catch the keystroke, post it to ourself, do not pass it on
02021                         PostMessage(myHwnd, (UINT)wParam, st_hook->vkCode, lParam);
02022                         return TRUE;
02023                     }
02024                 }
02025             }
02026         }
02027     }
02028 
02029     return CallNextHookEx(exthook_winhook, nCode, wParam, lParam);
02030 }
02031 
02032 // Microsoft doesn't have an outright "set toggle key state" call, they expect you
02033 // to know the state and then fake input to toggle. Blegh. Fine.
02034 void WinSetKeyToggleState(unsigned int vkCode, bool state) {
02035     bool curState = (GetKeyState(vkCode) & 1) ? true : false;
02036     INPUT inps;
02037 
02038     // if we're already in that state, then there is nothing to do.
02039     if (curState == state) return;
02040 
02041     // fake keyboard input.
02042     memset(&inps, 0, sizeof(inps));
02043     inps.type = INPUT_KEYBOARD;
02044     inps.ki.wVk = vkCode;
02045     inps.ki.dwFlags = KEYEVENTF_EXTENDEDKEY; // pressed, use wVk.
02046     SendInput(1, &inps, sizeof(INPUT));
02047 
02048     memset(&inps, 0, sizeof(inps));
02049     inps.type = INPUT_KEYBOARD;
02050     inps.ki.wVk = vkCode;
02051     inps.ki.dwFlags = KEYEVENTF_EXTENDEDKEY | KEYEVENTF_KEYUP; // release, use wVk.
02052     SendInput(1, &inps, sizeof(INPUT));
02053 }
02054 #endif

02056 Bitu Keyboard_Guest_LED_State();
02057 void UpdateKeyboardLEDState(Bitu led_state/* in the same bitfield arrangement as using command 0xED on PS/2 keyboards */);
02058 
02059 void UpdateKeyboardLEDState(Bitu led_state/* in the same bitfield arrangement as using command 0xED on PS/2 keyboards */) {
02060     (void)led_state;//POSSIBLY UNUSED
02061 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS) /* Microsoft Windows */
02062     if (exthook_enabled) { // ONLY if ext hook is enabled, else we risk infinite loops with keyboard events
02063         //WinSetKeyToggleState(VK_NUMLOCK, !!(led_state & 2));
02064         //WinSetKeyToggleState(VK_SCROLL, !!(led_state & 1));
02065         //WinSetKeyToggleState(VK_CAPITAL, !!(led_state & 4));
02066     }
02067 #endif
02068 }
02069 
02070 void DoExtendedKeyboardHook(bool enable) {
02071     if (exthook_enabled == enable)
02072         return;
02073 
02074 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS)
02075     if (enable) {
02076         if (!exthook_winhook) {
02077             exthook_winhook = SetWindowsHookEx(WH_KEYBOARD_LL, WinExtHookKeyboardHookProc, GetModuleHandle(NULL), 0);
02078             if (exthook_winhook == NULL) return;
02079         }
02080 
02081         // it's on
02082         exthook_enabled = enable;
02083 
02084         // flush out and handle pending keyboard I/O
02085         {
02086             MSG msg;
02087 
02088             while (PeekMessage(&msg, NULL, 0, 0, PM_REMOVE)) {
02089                 TranslateMessage(&msg);
02090                 DispatchMessage(&msg);
02091             }
02092         }
02093 
02094 #if !defined(__MINGW32__)
02095         // Enable the SDL hack for Win32 to handle Num/Scroll/Caps
02096         SDL_DOSBox_X_Hack_Set_Toggle_Key_WM_USER_Hack(1);
02097 #endif
02098 
02099         // if hooking Num/Scroll/Caps Lock then record the toggle state of those keys.
02100         // then read from the keyboard emulation the LED state set by the guest and apply it to the host keyboard.
02101         if (enable_hook_lock_toggle_keys) {
02102             // record state
02103             on_capture_num_lock_was_on = (GetKeyState(VK_NUMLOCK) & 1) ? true : false;
02104             on_capture_scroll_lock_was_on = (GetKeyState(VK_SCROLL) & 1) ? true : false;
02105             on_capture_caps_lock_was_on = (GetKeyState(VK_CAPITAL) & 1) ? true : false;
02106             // change to guest state (FIXME: Read emulated keyboard state and apply!)
02107             UpdateKeyboardLEDState(Keyboard_Guest_LED_State());
02108         }
02109     }
02110     else {
02111         if (exthook_winhook) {
02112             if (enable_hook_lock_toggle_keys) {
02113                 // restore state
02114                 //WinSetKeyToggleState(VK_NUMLOCK, on_capture_num_lock_was_on);
02115                 //WinSetKeyToggleState(VK_SCROLL, on_capture_scroll_lock_was_on);
02116                 //WinSetKeyToggleState(VK_CAPITAL, on_capture_caps_lock_was_on);
02117             }
02118 
02119             {
02120                 MSG msg;
02121 
02122                 // before we disable the SDL hack make sure we flush out and handle any pending keyboard events.
02123                 // if we don't do this the posted Num/Scroll/Caps events will stay in the queue and will be handled
02124                 // by SDL after turning off the toggle key hack.
02125                 Sleep(1); // make sure Windows posts the keystrokes
02126                 while (PeekMessage(&msg, NULL, 0, 0, PM_REMOVE)) {
02127                     TranslateMessage(&msg);
02128                     DispatchMessage(&msg);
02129                 }
02130             }
02131 
02132 #if !defined(__MINGW32__)
02133             // Disable the SDL hack for Win32 to handle Num/Scroll/Caps
02134             SDL_DOSBox_X_Hack_Set_Toggle_Key_WM_USER_Hack(0);
02135 #endif
02136 
02137             UnhookWindowsHookEx(exthook_winhook);
02138             exthook_winhook = NULL;
02139         }
02140 
02141         exthook_enabled = enable;
02142     }
02143 #endif
02144 }

02146 void GFX_ReleaseMouse(void) {
02147     if (sdl.mouse.locked)
02148         GFX_CaptureMouse();
02149 }
02150 
02151 void GFX_CaptureMouse(void) {
02152     GFX_CaptureMouse(!sdl.mouse.locked);
02153 }
02154 
02155 void GFX_CaptureMouse(bool capture) {
02156     sdl.mouse.locked=capture;
02157     if (sdl.mouse.locked) {
02158 #if defined(C_SDL2)
02159         SDL_SetRelativeMouseMode(SDL_TRUE);
02160 #else
02161         SDL_WM_GrabInput(SDL_GRAB_ON);
02162 #endif
02163         if (enable_hook_special_keys) DoExtendedKeyboardHook(true);
02164         SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_DISABLE);
02165     } else {
02166         DoExtendedKeyboardHook(false);
02167 #if defined(C_SDL2)
02168         SDL_SetRelativeMouseMode(SDL_FALSE);
02169 #else
02170         SDL_WM_GrabInput(SDL_GRAB_OFF);
02171 #endif
02172         if (sdl.mouse.autoenable || !sdl.mouse.autolock) SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_ENABLE);
02173     }
02174         mouselocked=sdl.mouse.locked;
02175 
02176 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW /* SDL drawn menus */
02177         if (sdl.mouse.locked) {
02178             void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
02179             void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
02180 
02181             GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
02182             GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
02183         }
02184 #endif
02185 
02186     /* keep the menu updated (it might not exist yet) */
02187     if (mainMenu.item_exists("mapper_capmouse"))
02188         mainMenu.get_item("mapper_capmouse").check(sdl.mouse.locked).refresh_item(mainMenu);
02189 }
02190 
02191 void GFX_UpdateSDLCaptureState(void) {
02192     if (sdl.mouse.locked) {
02193 #if defined(C_SDL2)
02194         SDL_SetRelativeMouseMode(SDL_TRUE);
02195 #else
02196         SDL_WM_GrabInput(SDL_GRAB_ON);
02197 #endif
02198         if (enable_hook_special_keys) DoExtendedKeyboardHook(true);
02199         SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_DISABLE);
02200     } else {
02201         DoExtendedKeyboardHook(false);
02202 #if defined(C_SDL2)
02203         SDL_SetRelativeMouseMode(SDL_FALSE);
02204 #else
02205         SDL_WM_GrabInput(SDL_GRAB_OFF);
02206 #endif
02207         if (sdl.mouse.autoenable || !sdl.mouse.autolock) SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_ENABLE);
02208     }
02209     CPU_Reset_AutoAdjust();
02210     GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,false);
02211 }

02213 #if WIN32
02214 void CaptureMouseNotifyWin32(bool lck)
02215 {
02216     switch (sdl.mouse.autolock_feedback)
02217     {
02218     case AUTOLOCK_FEEDBACK_NONE: break;
02219     case AUTOLOCK_FEEDBACK_BEEP:
02220     {
02221         const auto lo = 1000;
02222         const auto hi = 2000;
02223         const auto t1 = 50;
02224         const auto t2 = 25;
02225         const auto f1 = lck ? hi : lo;
02226         const auto f2 = lck ? lo : hi;
02227         const auto tt = lck ? t1 : t2;
02228         Beep(f1, tt);
02229         Beep(f2, tt);
02230     }
02231     break;
02232     case AUTOLOCK_FEEDBACK_FLASH:
02233     {
02234 # if !defined(HX_DOS)
02235         const auto cnt = lck ? 4 : 2;
02236         const auto tim = lck ? 80 : 40;
02237         const auto wnd = GetHWND();
02238         if (wnd != nullptr)
02239         {
02240             FLASHWINFO fi;
02241             fi.cbSize    = sizeof(FLASHWINFO);
02242             fi.hwnd      = wnd;
02243             fi.dwFlags   = FLASHW_CAPTION;
02244             fi.uCount    = cnt;
02245             fi.dwTimeout = tim;
02246             FlashWindowEx(&fi);
02247         }
02248 # endif
02249         break;
02250     }
02251     default: ;
02252     }
02253 }
02254 #endif

02279 #if defined (WIN32)
02280 STICKYKEYS stick_keys = {sizeof(STICKYKEYS), 0};
02281 void sticky_keys(bool restore){
02282     static bool inited = false;
02283     if (!inited){
02284         inited = true;
02285         SystemParametersInfo(SPI_GETSTICKYKEYS, sizeof(STICKYKEYS), &stick_keys, 0);
02286     } 
02287     if (restore) {
02288         SystemParametersInfo(SPI_SETSTICKYKEYS, sizeof(STICKYKEYS), &stick_keys, 0);
02289         return;
02290     }
02291     //Get current sticky keys layout:
02292     STICKYKEYS s = {sizeof(STICKYKEYS), 0};
02293     SystemParametersInfo(SPI_GETSTICKYKEYS, sizeof(STICKYKEYS), &s, 0);
02294     if ( !(s.dwFlags & SKF_STICKYKEYSON)) { //Not on already
02295         s.dwFlags &= ~SKF_HOTKEYACTIVE;
02296         SystemParametersInfo(SPI_SETSTICKYKEYS, sizeof(STICKYKEYS), &s, 0);
02297     }
02298 }
02299 #else
02300 #define sticky_keys(a)
02301 #endif

02303 void GetDesktopResolution(int* width, int* height)
02304 {
02305 #ifdef WIN32
02306     RECT rDdesk;
02307     auto hDesk = GetDesktopWindow();
02308     GetWindowRect(hDesk, &rDdesk);
02309     *width = rDdesk.right - rDdesk.left;
02310     *height = rDdesk.bottom - rDdesk.top;
02311 #elif defined(LINUX)
02312     void Linux_GetDesktopResolution(int *width,int *height);
02313     Linux_GetDesktopResolution(width,height); /* this is MESSY but there's too much namespace collision going on here */
02314 #else
02315     *width = 1024; // guess
02316     *height = 768;
02317 #endif
02318 }
