02320 void res_init(void) {
02321     Section * sec = control->GetSection("sdl");
02322     Section_prop * section=static_cast<Section_prop *>(sec);
02323     sdl.desktop.full.fixed=false;
02324     const char* fullresolution=section->Get_string("fullresolution");
02325     sdl.desktop.full.width  = 0; sdl.desktop.full.height = 0;
02326     if(fullresolution && *fullresolution) {
02327         char res[100];
02328         safe_strncpy( res, fullresolution, sizeof( res ));
02329         fullresolution = lowcase (res);//so x and X are allowed
02330         if (strcmp(fullresolution,"original")) {
02331             sdl.desktop.full.fixed = true;
02332             if (strcmp(fullresolution,"desktop")) { //desktop = 0x0
02333                 char* height = const_cast<char*>(strchr(fullresolution,'x'));
02334                 if(height && * height) {
02335                     *height = 0;
02336                     sdl.desktop.full.height = atoi(height+1);
02337                     sdl.desktop.full.width  = atoi(res);
02338                 }
02339             }
02340         }
02341     }
02342 
02343     sdl.desktop.window.width  = 0;
02344     sdl.desktop.window.height = 0;
02345     const char* windowresolution=section->Get_string("windowresolution");
02346     if(windowresolution && *windowresolution) {
02347         //if(sdl.desktop.type==SCREEN_SURFACE) return;
02348         char res[100];
02349         safe_strncpy( res,windowresolution, sizeof( res ));
02350         windowresolution = lowcase (res);//so x and X are allowed
02351         if(strcmp(windowresolution,"original")) {
02352             char* height = const_cast<char*>(strchr(windowresolution,'x'));
02353             if(height && *height) {
02354                 *height = 0;
02355                 sdl.desktop.window.height = (Bit16u)atoi(height+1);
02356                 sdl.desktop.window.width  = (Bit16u)atoi(res);
02357             }
02358         }
02359     }
02360     sdl.desktop.doublebuf=section->Get_bool("fulldouble");
02361 
02362     int width = 1024;
02363     int height = 768;
02364     
02365     // fullresolution == desktop -> get/set desktop size
02366     auto sdlSection = control->GetSection("sdl");
02367     auto sdlSectionProp = static_cast<Section_prop*>(sdlSection);
02368     auto fullRes = sdlSectionProp->Get_string("fullresolution");
02369     if (!strcmp(fullRes, "desktop")) GetDesktopResolution(&width, &height);
02370     
02371     if (!sdl.desktop.full.width) {
02372         sdl.desktop.full.width=width;
02373     }
02374     if (!sdl.desktop.full.height) {
02375         sdl.desktop.full.height=height;
02376     }
02377     if(sdl.desktop.type==SCREEN_SURFACE && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen) return;
02378     else {
02379         GFX_Stop();
02380         if (sdl.draw.callback)
02381             (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackReset );
02382         GFX_Start();
02383     }
02384 }
02385 
02386 void res_input(bool type, const char * res) {
02387     Section* sec = control->GetSection("sdl");
02388     char win_res[11];
02389     if(sec) {
02390         strcpy(win_res,res);
02391         if(type) {
02392             std::string tmp("windowresolution="); tmp.append(win_res);
02393             sec->HandleInputline(tmp);
02394         } else {
02395             std::string tmp("fullresolution="); tmp.append(win_res);
02396             sec->HandleInputline(tmp);
02397         }
02398 
02399         res_init();
02400     }
02401 }
02402 
02403 void change_output(int output) {
02404     GFX_Stop();
02405     Section * sec = control->GetSection("sdl");
02406     Section_prop * section=static_cast<Section_prop *>(sec);
02407     sdl.overscan_width=(unsigned int)section->Get_int("overscan");
02408     UpdateOverscanMenu();
02409 
02410     switch (output) {
02411     case 0:
02412         OUTPUT_SURFACE_Select();
02413         break;
02414     case 1:
02415         OUTPUT_SURFACE_Select();
02416         break;
02417     case 2: /* do nothing */
02418         break;
02419     case 3:
02420 #if C_OPENGL
02421         change_output(2);
02422         OUTPUT_OPENGL_Select();
02423         sdl_opengl.bilinear = true;
02424 #endif
02425         break;
02426     case 4:
02427 #if C_OPENGL
02428         change_output(2);
02429         OUTPUT_OPENGL_Select();
02430         sdl_opengl.bilinear = false; //NB
02431 #endif
02432         break;
02433 #if C_DIRECT3D
02434     case 5:
02435         OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_Select();
02436         break;
02437 #endif
02438     case 6:
02439         break;
02440     case 7:
02441         // do not set want_type
02442         break;
02443     case 8:
02444 #if C_DIRECT3D
02445         if (sdl.desktop.want_type == SCREEN_DIRECT3D) 
02446             OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_Select();
02447 #endif
02448         break;
02449 
02450     default:
02451         LOG_MSG("SDL:Unsupported output device %d, switching back to surface",output);
02452         OUTPUT_SURFACE_Select();
02453         break;
02454     }
02455 
02456     const char* windowresolution=section->Get_string("windowresolution");
02457     if (windowresolution && *windowresolution) 
02458     {
02459         char res[100];
02460         safe_strncpy( res,windowresolution, sizeof( res ));
02461         windowresolution = lowcase (res);//so x and X are allowed
02462         if (strcmp(windowresolution,"original")) 
02463         {
02464             if (output == 0) 
02465             {
02466                 std::string tmp("windowresolution=original");
02467                 sec->HandleInputline(tmp);
02468             }
02469         }
02470     }
02471     res_init();
02472 
02473     if (sdl.draw.callback)
02474         (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackReset );
02475 
02476     GFX_SetTitle((Bit32s)CPU_CycleMax,-1,-1,false);
02477     GFX_LogSDLState();
02478 
02479     UpdateWindowDimensions();
02480 }

02482 #if !defined(HX_DOS) && defined(SDL_DOSBOX_X_SPECIAL)
02483 extern "C" void SDL_hax_SetFSWindowPosition(int x,int y,int w,int h);
02484 #endif
02485 
02486 void GFX_SwitchFullScreen(void)
02487 {
02488 #if !defined(HX_DOS)
02489     if (sdl.desktop.prevent_fullscreen)
02490         return;
02491 
02492     if (!sdl.desktop.fullscreen) {/*is GOING fullscreen*/
02493         UpdateWindowDimensions();
02494 
02495         if (screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width != 0 && screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height != 0) {
02496             if (sdl.desktop.full.width_auto)
02497                 sdl.desktop.full.width = (unsigned int)screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width;
02498             if (sdl.desktop.full.height_auto)
02499                 sdl.desktop.full.height = (unsigned int)screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height;
02500 
02501 #if !defined(C_SDL2) && defined(MACOSX)
02502             /* Mac OS X has this annoying problem with their API where the System Preferences app, display settings panel
02503                allows setting 720p and 1080i/1080p modes on monitors who's native resolution is less than 1920x1080 but
02504                supports 1920x1080.
02505 
02506                This is a problem with HDTV sets made in the late 2000s early 2010s when "HD" apparently meant LCD displays
02507                with 1368x768 resolution that will nonetheless accept 1080i (and later, 1080p) and downscale on display.
02508 
02509                The problem is that with these monitors, Mac OS X's display API will NOT list 1920x1080 as one of the
02510                display modes even when the freaking desktop is obviously set to 1920x1080 on that monitor!
02511 
02512                If the screen reporting code says 1920x1080 and we try to go fullscreen, SDL1 will intervene and say
02513                "hey wait there's no 1920x1080 in the mode list" and then fail the call.
02514 
02515                So to work around this, we have to go check SDL's mode list before using the screen size returned by the
02516                API.
02517 
02518                Oh and for extra fun, Mac OS X is one of those modern systems where "setting the video mode" apparently
02519                means NOT setting the video hardware mode but just changing how the GPU scales the display... EXCEPT when
02520                talking to these older displays where if the user set it to 1080i/1080p, our request to set 1368x768
02521                actually DOES change the video mode. This is just wonderful considering the old HDTV set I bought back in
02522                2008 takes 1-2 seconds to adjust to the mode change on it's HDMI input.
02523 
02524                Frankly I wish I knew how to fix the SDL1 Quartz code to use whatever abracadabra magic code is required
02525                to enumerate these extra HDTV modes so this hack isn't necessary, except that experience says this hack is
02526                always necesary because it might not always work.
02527 
02528                This magic hidden super secret API bullshit is annoying. You're worse than Microsoft with this stuff, Apple --J.C. */
02529             {
02530                 SDL_Rect **ls = SDLCALL SDL_ListModes(NULL, SDL_FULLSCREEN);
02531                 if (ls != NULL) {
02532                     unsigned int maxwidth = 0,maxheight = 0;
02533 
02534                     for (size_t i=0;ls[i] != NULL;i++) {
02535                         unsigned int w = ls[i]->w;
02536                         unsigned int h = ls[i]->h;
02537 
02538                         if (maxwidth < w || maxheight < h) {
02539                             maxwidth = w;
02540                             maxheight = h;
02541                         }
02542                     }
02543 
02544                     if (maxwidth != 0 && maxheight != 0) {
02545                         LOG_MSG("OS X: Actual maximum screen resolution is %d x %d\n",maxwidth,maxheight);
02546 
02547                         if (sdl.desktop.full.width_auto) {
02548                             if (sdl.desktop.full.width > maxwidth)
02549                                 sdl.desktop.full.width = maxwidth;
02550                         }
02551                         if (sdl.desktop.full.height_auto) {
02552                             if (sdl.desktop.full.height > maxheight)
02553                                 sdl.desktop.full.height = maxheight;
02554                         }
02555                     }
02556                 }
02557             }
02558 #endif
02559 
02560 #if !defined(C_SDL2) && defined(SDL_DOSBOX_X_SPECIAL)
02561             SDL_hax_SetFSWindowPosition(
02562                 (int)screen_size_info.screen_position_pixels.x, (int)screen_size_info.screen_position_pixels.y,
02563                 (int)screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width, (int)screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height);
02564 #endif
02565         }
02566         else {
02567 #if !defined(C_SDL2) && defined(SDL_DOSBOX_X_SPECIAL)
02568             SDL_hax_SetFSWindowPosition(0,0,0,0);
02569 #endif
02570         }
02571     }
02572 
02573     menu.resizeusing = true;
02574 
02575     sdl.desktop.fullscreen = !sdl.desktop.fullscreen;
02576 
02577     auto full = sdl.desktop.fullscreen;
02578 
02579     // if we're going fullscreen and current scaler exceeds screen size,
02580     // cancel the fullscreen change -> fixes scaler crashes
02581     // TODO this will need further changes to accomodate different outputs (e.g. stretched)
02582     if (full)
02583     {
02584         int width, height;
02585         GetDesktopResolution(&width, &height);
02586         auto width1 = sdl.draw.width;
02587         auto height1 = sdl.draw.height;
02588         if ((unsigned int)width < width1 || (unsigned int)height < height1) {
02589             sdl.desktop.fullscreen = false;
02590             LOG_MSG("WARNING: full screen canceled, surface size (%ix%i) exceeds screen size (%ix%i).",
02591                 width1, height1, width, height);
02592             return;
02593         }
02594     }
02595 
02596     LOG_MSG("INFO: switched to %s mode", full ? "full screen" : "window");
02597 
02598 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
02599     // (re-)assign menu to window
02600     void DOSBox_SetSysMenu(void);
02601     DOSBox_SetSysMenu();
02602 #endif
02603 
02604     // ensure mouse capture when fullscreen || (re-)capture if user said so when windowed
02605     auto locked = sdl.mouse.locked;
02606     if ((full && !locked) || (!full && locked)) GFX_CaptureMouse();
02607 
02608     // disable/enable sticky keys for fullscreen/desktop
02609 #if defined (WIN32)     
02610     sticky_keys(!full);
02611 #endif
02612 
02613     GFX_ResetScreen();
02614 
02615     // set vsync to host
02616     // NOTE why forcing ???
02617 #ifdef WIN32
02618     if (menu.startup) // NOTE should be always true I suppose ???
02619     {
02620         auto vsync = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("vsync"));
02621         if (vsync)
02622         {
02623             auto vsyncMode = vsync->Get_string("vsyncmode");
02624             if (!strcmp(vsyncMode, "host")) SetVal("vsync", "vsyncmode", "host");
02625         }
02626     }
02627 #endif
02628 #endif
02629 }

02633         return;

02635     GFX_LosingFocus();
02636     if (sdl.desktop.lazy_fullscreen) {
02637         LOG_MSG("GFX LF: fullscreen switching not supported");
02638     } else {
02639         GFX_SwitchFullScreen();
02640     }
02641 }

02682         return;

02688 
02689 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
02690 static bool GFX_GetSurfacePtrLock = false;
02691 
02692 unsigned char *GFX_GetSurfacePtr(size_t *pitch, unsigned int x, unsigned int y) {
02693     if (sdl.surface->pixels == NULL) {
02694         if (!GFX_GetSurfacePtrLock) {
02695             if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface) && SDL_LockSurface(sdl.surface))
02696                 return NULL;
02697 
02698             GFX_GetSurfacePtrLock = true;
02699         }
02700     }
02701 
02702     *pitch = sdl.surface->pitch;
02703     if (sdl.surface->pixels != NULL) {
02704         unsigned char *p = (unsigned char*)(sdl.surface->pixels);
02705         p += y * sdl.surface->pitch;
02706         p += x * ((unsigned int)sdl.surface->format->BitsPerPixel >> 3U);
02707         return p;
02708     }
02709 
02710     return NULL;
02711 }
02712 
02713 void GFX_ReleaseSurfacePtr(void) {
02714     if (GFX_GetSurfacePtrLock) {
02715         if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
02716             SDL_UnlockSurface(sdl.surface);
02717  
02718         GFX_GetSurfacePtrLock = false;
02719     }
02720 }
02721 #endif
02722 
02723 bool GFX_StartUpdate(Bit8u* &pixels,Bitu &pitch) 
02724 {
02725     if (!sdl.active || sdl.updating)
02726         return false;
02727 
02728     switch (sdl.desktop.type) 
02729     {
02730         case SCREEN_SURFACE:
02731             return OUTPUT_SURFACE_StartUpdate(pixels, pitch);
02732 
02733 #if C_OPENGL
02734         case SCREEN_OPENGL:
02735             return OUTPUT_OPENGL_StartUpdate(pixels, pitch);
02736 #endif
02737 
02738 #if C_DIRECT3D
02739         case SCREEN_DIRECT3D:
02740             return OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_StartUpdate(pixels, pitch);
02741 #endif
02742 
02743         default:
02744             break;
02745     }
02746 
02747     return false;
02748 }
02749 
02750 void GFX_OpenGLRedrawScreen(void) {
02751 #if C_OPENGL
02752     if (OpenGL_using()) {
02753         if (sdl_opengl.clear_countdown > 0) {
02754             sdl_opengl.clear_countdown--;
02755             glClearColor (0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
02756             glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT);
02757         }
02758 
02759         if (sdl_opengl.pixel_buffer_object) {
02760             glUnmapBufferARB(GL_PIXEL_UNPACK_BUFFER_EXT);
02761             glBindTexture(GL_TEXTURE_2D, sdl_opengl.texture);
02762             glBindBufferARB(GL_PIXEL_UNPACK_BUFFER_EXT, 0);
02763             glCallList(sdl_opengl.displaylist);
02764         } else {
02765             glBindTexture(GL_TEXTURE_2D, sdl_opengl.texture);
02766             glCallList(sdl_opengl.displaylist);
02767         }
02768     }
02769 #endif
02770 }
02771 
02772 void GFX_EndUpdate(const Bit16u *changedLines) {
02773 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
02774     emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
02775 #endif
02776 
02777     /* don't present our output if 3Dfx is in OpenGL mode */
02778     if (sdl.desktop.prevent_fullscreen)
02779         return;
02780 
02781 #if C_DIRECT3D
02782     // we may have to do forced update in D3D case
02783     if (d3d && d3d->getForceUpdate());
02784     else
02785 #endif
02786     if (!sdl.updating)
02787         return;
02788 
02789     sdl.updating = false;
02790     switch (sdl.desktop.type) 
02791     {
02792         case SCREEN_SURFACE:
02793             OUTPUT_SURFACE_EndUpdate(changedLines);
02794             break;
02795 
02796 #if C_OPENGL
02797         case SCREEN_OPENGL:
02798             OUTPUT_OPENGL_EndUpdate(changedLines);
02799             break;
02800 #endif
02801 
02802 #if C_DIRECT3D
02803         case SCREEN_DIRECT3D:
02804             OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_EndUpdate(changedLines);
02805             break;
02806 #endif
02807 
02808         default:
02809             break;
02810     }
02811 
02812     if (changedLines != NULL) 
02813     {
02814         sdl.must_redraw_all = false;
02815 
02816 #if !defined(C_SDL2) && defined(SDL_DOSBOX_X_SPECIAL)
02817         sdl.surface->flags &= ~((unsigned int)SDL_HAX_NOREFRESH);
02818 #endif
02819 
02820         if (changedLines != NULL && sdl.deferred_resize) 
02821         {
02822             sdl.deferred_resize = false;
02823 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
02824             void GFX_RedrawScreen(Bit32u nWidth, Bit32u nHeight);
02825             GFX_RedrawScreen(sdl.draw.width, sdl.draw.height);
02826 #endif
02827         }
02828         else if (sdl.gfx_force_redraw_count > 0) 
02829         {
02830             void RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackFunctions_t function );
02831             RENDER_CallBack(GFX_CallBackRedraw);
02832             sdl.gfx_force_redraw_count--;
02833         }
02834     }
02835 }
02836 
02837 void GFX_SetPalette(Bitu start,Bitu count,GFX_PalEntry * entries) {
02838     (void)start;
02839     (void)count;
02840     (void)entries;
02841 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
02842     /* I should probably not change the GFX_PalEntry :) */
02843     if (sdl.surface->flags & SDL_HWPALETTE) {
02844         if (!SDL_SetPalette(sdl.surface,SDL_PHYSPAL,(SDL_Color *)entries,(int)start,(int)count)) {
02845             E_Exit("SDL:Can't set palette");
02846         }
02847     } else {
02848         if (!SDL_SetPalette(sdl.surface,SDL_LOGPAL,(SDL_Color *)entries,(int)start,(int)count)) {
02849             E_Exit("SDL:Can't set palette");
02850         }
02851     }
02852 #endif
02853 }
02854 
02855 Bitu GFX_GetRGB(Bit8u red, Bit8u green, Bit8u blue) {
02856     switch (sdl.desktop.type) {
02857         case SCREEN_SURFACE:
02858             return SDL_MapRGB(sdl.surface->format, red, green, blue);
02859 
02860 #if C_OPENGL
02861         case SCREEN_OPENGL:
02862 # if SDL_BYTEORDER == SDL_LIL_ENDIAN && defined(MACOSX) /* Mac OS X Intel builds use a weird RGBA order (alpha in the low 8 bits) */
02863             //USE BGRA
02864             return (((unsigned long)blue << 24ul) | ((unsigned long)green << 16ul) | ((unsigned long)red <<  8ul)) | (255ul <<  0ul);
02865 # else
02866             //USE ARGB
02867             return (((unsigned long)blue <<  0ul) | ((unsigned long)green <<  8ul) | ((unsigned long)red << 16ul)) | (255ul << 24ul);
02868 # endif
02869 #endif
02870 
02871 #if C_DIRECT3D
02872         case SCREEN_DIRECT3D:
02873             return SDL_MapRGB(sdl.surface->format, red, green, blue);
02874 #endif
02875 
02876         default:
02877             break;
02878     }
02879     return 0;
02880 }
02881 
02882 void GFX_Stop() {
02883     if (sdl.updating)
02884         GFX_EndUpdate( 0 );
02885     sdl.active=false;
02886 }
02887 
02888 void GFX_Start() {
02889     sdl.active=true;
02890 }
02891 
02892 static void GUI_ShutDown(Section * /*sec*/) {
02893     GFX_Stop();
02894     if (sdl.draw.callback) (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackStop );
02895     if (sdl.mouse.locked) GFX_CaptureMouse();
02896     if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen) GFX_SwitchFullScreen();
02897     switch (sdl.desktop.type)
02898     {
02899         case SCREEN_SURFACE:
02900             OUTPUT_SURFACE_Shutdown();
02901             break;
02902 
02903 #if C_OPENGL
02904         case SCREEN_OPENGL:
02905             OUTPUT_OPENGL_Shutdown();
02906             break;
02907 #endif
02908 
02909 #if C_DIRECT3D
02910         case SCREEN_DIRECT3D:
02911             OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_Shutdown();
02912             break;
02913 #endif
02914 
02915         default:
02916                 break;
02917     }
02918 }
02919 
02920 static void SetPriority(PRIORITY_LEVELS level) {
02921 
02922 #if C_SET_PRIORITY
02923 // Do nothing if priorties are not the same and not root, else the highest
02924 // priority can not be set as users can only lower priority (not restore it)
02925 
02926     if((sdl.priority.focus != sdl.priority.nofocus ) &&
02927         (getuid()!=0) ) return;
02928 
02929 #endif
02930     switch (level) {
02931 #ifdef WIN32
02932     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_PAUSE:  // if DOSBox is paused, assume idle priority
02933     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWEST:
02934         SetPriorityClass(GetCurrentProcess(),IDLE_PRIORITY_CLASS);
02935         break;
02936     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWER:
02937         SetPriorityClass(GetCurrentProcess(),BELOW_NORMAL_PRIORITY_CLASS);
02938         break;
02939     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_NORMAL:
02940         SetPriorityClass(GetCurrentProcess(),NORMAL_PRIORITY_CLASS);
02941         break;
02942     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHER:
02943         SetPriorityClass(GetCurrentProcess(),ABOVE_NORMAL_PRIORITY_CLASS);
02944         break;
02945     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHEST:
02946         SetPriorityClass(GetCurrentProcess(),HIGH_PRIORITY_CLASS);
02947         break;
02948 #elif C_SET_PRIORITY
02949 /* Linux use group as dosbox has mulitple threads under linux */
02950     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_PAUSE:  // if DOSBox is paused, assume idle priority
02951     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWEST:
02952         setpriority (PRIO_PGRP, 0,PRIO_MAX);
02953         break;
02954     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWER:
02955         setpriority (PRIO_PGRP, 0,PRIO_MAX-(PRIO_TOTAL/3));
02956         break;
02957     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_NORMAL:
02958         setpriority (PRIO_PGRP, 0,PRIO_MAX-(PRIO_TOTAL/2));
02959         break;
02960     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHER:
02961         setpriority (PRIO_PGRP, 0,PRIO_MAX-((3*PRIO_TOTAL)/5) );
02962         break;
02963     case PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHEST:
02964         setpriority (PRIO_PGRP, 0,PRIO_MAX-((3*PRIO_TOTAL)/4) );
02965         break;
02966 #endif
02967     default:
02968         break;
02969     }
02970 }
02971 
02972 extern Bit8u int10_font_14[256 * 14];
02973 static void OutputString(Bitu x,Bitu y,const char * text,Bit32u color,Bit32u color2,SDL_Surface * output_surface) {
02974     Bit32u * draw=(Bit32u*)(((Bit8u *)output_surface->pixels)+((y)*output_surface->pitch))+x;
02975     while (*text) {
02976         Bit8u * font=&int10_font_14[(*text)*14];
02977         Bitu i,j;
02978         Bit32u * draw_line=draw;
02979         for (i=0;i<14;i++) {
02980             Bit8u map=*font++;
02981             for (j=0;j<8;j++) {
02982                 if (map & 0x80) *((Bit32u*)(draw_line+j))=color; else *((Bit32u*)(draw_line+j))=color2;
02983                 map<<=1;
02984             }
02985             draw_line+=output_surface->pitch/4;
02986         }
02987         text++;
02988         draw+=8;
02989     }
02990 }

02995     throw int(3);
02996 }

03033 static void GUI_StartUp() {
03034     DOSBoxMenu::item *item;

03043 #else
03044     LOG(LOG_GUI,LOG_DEBUG)("This version compiled against SDL 1.x");
03045 #endif
03046 
03047 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03048     /* while we're here, SDL 2.0.5 has some issues with Linux/X11, encourage the user to update SDL2. */
03049     {
03050         SDL_version v;
03051         SDL_GetVersion(&v);
03052         LOG(LOG_GUI,LOG_DEBUG)("SDL2 version %u.%u.%u",v.major,v.minor,v.patch);
03053 
03054 # if defined(LINUX)
03055         /* Linux/X11 2.0.5 has window positioning issues i.e. with XFCE */
03056         if (v.major == 2 && v.minor == 0 && v.patch == 5)
03057             LOG_MSG("WARNING: Your SDL2 library is known to have some issues with Linux/X11, please update your SDL2 library");
03058 # endif
03059     }
03060 #endif
03061 
03062     AddExitFunction(AddExitFunctionFuncPair(GUI_ShutDown));
03063     GUI_LoadFonts();
03064 
03065     sdl.active=false;
03066     sdl.updating=false;
03067 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03068     sdl.update_window=true;
03069 #endif
03070

03072 
03073     sdl.desktop.lazy_fullscreen=false;
03074     sdl.desktop.lazy_fullscreen_req=false;
03075     sdl.desktop.prevent_fullscreen=false;

03078     assert(section != NULL);

03084     std::string focus = p->GetSection()->Get_string("active");
03085     std::string notfocus = p->GetSection()->Get_string("inactive");
03086 
03087     if      (focus == "lowest")  { sdl.priority.focus = PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWEST;  }
03088     else if (focus == "lower")   { sdl.priority.focus = PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWER;   }
03089     else if (focus == "normal")  { sdl.priority.focus = PRIORITY_LEVEL_NORMAL;  }
03090     else if (focus == "higher")  { sdl.priority.focus = PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHER;  }
03091     else if (focus == "highest") { sdl.priority.focus = PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHEST; }
03092

03094     else if (notfocus == "lower")   { sdl.priority.nofocus=PRIORITY_LEVEL_LOWER;   }
03095     else if (notfocus == "normal")  { sdl.priority.nofocus=PRIORITY_LEVEL_NORMAL;  }
03096     else if (notfocus == "higher")  { sdl.priority.nofocus=PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHER;  }
03097     else if (notfocus == "highest") { sdl.priority.nofocus=PRIORITY_LEVEL_HIGHEST; }

03100          * for DOSBox to be paused while it has focus
03101          */
03102         sdl.priority.nofocus=PRIORITY_LEVEL_PAUSE;

03110     const char* fullresolution=section->Get_string("fullresolution");
03111     sdl.desktop.full.width  = 0;
03112     sdl.desktop.full.height = 0;
03113     if(fullresolution && *fullresolution) {
03114         char res[100];
03115         safe_strncpy(res, fullresolution, sizeof(res));
03116         fullresolution = lowcase (res);//so x and X are allowed
03117         if (strcmp(fullresolution,"original")) {
03118             sdl.desktop.full.fixed = true;
03119             if (strcmp(fullresolution,"desktop")) { //desktop = 0x0
03120                 char* height = const_cast<char*>(strchr(fullresolution,'x'));
03121                 if (height && * height) {
03122                     *height = 0;
03123                     sdl.desktop.full.height = (Bit16u)atoi(height+1);
03124                     sdl.desktop.full.width  = (Bit16u)atoi(res);
03125                 }
03126             }
03127         }
03128     }
03129 
03130     sdl.desktop.window.width  = 0;
03131     sdl.desktop.window.height = 0;
03132     const char* windowresolution=section->Get_string("windowresolution");
03133     if(windowresolution && *windowresolution) {
03134         char res[100];
03135         safe_strncpy(res, windowresolution, sizeof(res));
03136         windowresolution = lowcase (res);//so x and X are allowed
03137         if(strcmp(windowresolution,"original")) {
03138             char* height = const_cast<char*>(strchr(windowresolution,'x'));
03139             if(height && *height) {
03140                 *height = 0;
03141                 sdl.desktop.window.height = (Bit16u)atoi(height+1);
03142                 sdl.desktop.window.width  = (Bit16u)atoi(res);
03143             }
03144         }
03145     }
03146     sdl.desktop.doublebuf=section->Get_bool("fulldouble");
03147 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03148     {
03149         SDL_DisplayMode dm;
03150         if (SDL_GetDesktopDisplayMode(0/*FIXME display index*/,&dm) == 0) {
03151             if (sdl.desktop.full.width == 0) {
03152                 sdl.desktop.full.width_auto = true;
03153                 sdl.desktop.full.width = dm.w;
03154             }
03155             if (sdl.desktop.full.height == 0) {
03156                 sdl.desktop.full.height_auto = true;
03157                 sdl.desktop.full.height = dm.h;
03158             }
03159             LOG_MSG("SDL2 reports desktop display mode %u x %u",dm.w,dm.h);
03160         }
03161         else {
03162             LOG_MSG("SDL2 unable to determine desktop display mode, error %s",SDL_GetError());
03163         }
03164     }
03165 #endif
03166 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
03167   #if SDL_VERSION_ATLEAST(1, 2, 10)
03168   #ifdef WIN32
03169     /* NTS: This should not print any warning whatsoever because Windows builds by default will use
03170      *      the Windows API to disable DPI scaling of the main window, unless the user modifies the
03171      *      setting through dosbox.conf or the command line. */
03172     /* NTS: Mac OS X has high DPI scaling too, though Apple is wise to enable it by default only for
03173      *      Macbooks with "Retina" displays. On Mac OS X, unless otherwise wanted by the user, it is
03174      *      wise to let Mac OS X scale up the DOSBox-X window by 2x so that the DOS prompt is not
03175      *      a teeny tiny window on the screen. */
03176     const SDL_VideoInfo* vidinfo = SDL_GetVideoInfo();
03177     if (vidinfo) {
03178         int sdl_w = vidinfo->current_w;
03179         int sdl_h = vidinfo->current_h;
03180         int win_w = GetSystemMetrics(SM_CXSCREEN);
03181         int win_h = GetSystemMetrics(SM_CYSCREEN);
03182         if (sdl_w != win_w && sdl_h != win_h) 
03183             LOG_MSG("Windows dpi/blurry apps scaling detected! The screen might be too large or not show properly,\n"
03184                 "please see the DOSBox Manual/README for details.\n");
03185         }
03186   #else
03187     if (!sdl.desktop.full.width || !sdl.desktop.full.height){
03188         //Can only be done on the very first call! Not restartable.
03189         //On windows don't use it as SDL returns the values without taking in account the dpi scaling
03190         const SDL_VideoInfo* vidinfo = SDL_GetVideoInfo();
03191         if (vidinfo) {
03192             if (sdl.desktop.full.width == 0) {
03193                 sdl.desktop.full.width_auto = true;
03194                 sdl.desktop.full.width = vidinfo->current_w;
03195             }
03196             if (sdl.desktop.full.height == 0) {
03197                 sdl.desktop.full.height_auto = true;
03198                 sdl.desktop.full.height = vidinfo->current_h;
03199             }
03200 
03201             LOG_MSG("SDL1 auto-detected desktop as %u x %u",
03202                 (unsigned int)sdl.desktop.full.width,
03203                 (unsigned int)sdl.desktop.full.height);
03204         }
03205     }
03206   #endif
03207   #endif
03208 #endif
03209 
03210     int width=1024;
03211     int height=768;
03212     if (!sdl.desktop.full.width) {
03213         sdl.desktop.full.width_auto = true;
03214         sdl.desktop.full.width=width;
03215     }
03216     if (!sdl.desktop.full.height) {
03217         sdl.desktop.full.height_auto = true;
03218         sdl.desktop.full.height=height;

03221     if (!sdl.mouse.autoenable) SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_DISABLE);

03238     if (emulation == "always")

03259 #endif
03260

03262     // "overlay" was removed, pre-map to Direct3D or OpenGL or surface
03263     if (output == "overlay")

03265 #if C_DIRECT3D

03281 #if C_OPENGL

03286         sdl_opengl.bilinear = true;
03287     }
03288     else if (output == "openglnb")

03292 #endif
03293 #if C_DIRECT3D

03296     {
03297         OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_Select();
03298 #if LOG_D3D
03299         LOG_MSG("SDL:Direct3D activated");
03300 #endif
03301 #endif
03302     } 
03303     else 
03304     {
03305         LOG_MSG("SDL:Unsupported output device %s, switching back to surface",output.c_str());
03306         OUTPUT_SURFACE_Select(); // should not reach there anymore
03307     }
03308 
03309     sdl.overscan_width=(unsigned int)section->Get_int("overscan");
03310 //  sdl.overscan_color=section->Get_int("overscancolor");
03311 
03312 #if defined(C_SDL2)

03314     GFX_SetResizeable(true);
03315     if (!GFX_SetSDLSurfaceWindow(640,400))
03316         E_Exit("Could not initialize video: %s",SDL_GetError());
03317     sdl.surface = SDL_GetWindowSurface(sdl.window);
03318 //    SDL_Rect splash_rect=GFX_GetSDLSurfaceSubwindowDims(640,400);
03319     sdl.desktop.pixelFormat = SDL_GetWindowPixelFormat(sdl.window);
03320     LOG_MSG("SDL:Current window pixel format: %s", SDL_GetPixelFormatName(sdl.desktop.pixelFormat));
03321     sdl.desktop.bpp=8*SDL_BYTESPERPIXEL(sdl.desktop.pixelFormat);
03322     if (SDL_BITSPERPIXEL(sdl.desktop.pixelFormat) == 24)
03323         LOG_MSG("SDL: You are running in 24 bpp mode, this will slow down things!");
03324 #else
03325     /* Initialize screen for first time */

03395 void Mouse_AutoLock(bool enable) {
03396     if (sdl.mouse.autolock == enable)
03397         return;
03398 
03399     sdl.mouse.autolock=enable;
03400     if (sdl.mouse.autoenable) sdl.mouse.requestlock=enable;
03401     else {
03402         SDL_ShowCursor(enable?SDL_DISABLE:SDL_ENABLE);
03403         sdl.mouse.requestlock=false;
03404     }
03405 }
03406 
03407 bool Mouse_IsLocked()
03408 {
03409     return sdl.mouse.locked;
03410 }
03411 
03412 static void RedrawScreen(Bit32u nWidth, Bit32u nHeight) {
03413     (void)nWidth;//UNUSED
03414     (void)nHeight;//UNUSED
03415 //  int width;
03416 //  int height;
03417 #ifdef __WIN32__
03418 //   width=sdl.clip.w; 
03419 //   height=sdl.clip.h;
03420 #else
03421 //  width=sdl.draw.width; 
03422 //  height=sdl.draw.height;
03423 #endif
03424     void RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackFunctions_t function );
03425 #if 0
03426     while (sdl.desktop.fullscreen) {
03427         int temp_size;
03428         temp_size=render.scale.size;
03429         if(!sdl.desktop.fullscreen) { render.scale.size=temp_size; RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackReset); return; }
03430     }
03431 #endif
03432 #ifdef WIN32
03433     if(menu.resizeusing) {
03434         RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackReset);
03435         return;
03436     }
03437 #endif
03438 #if 0 /* FIXME: This code misbehaves when doublescan=false on Linux/X11 */
03439     if((Bitu)nWidth == (Bitu)width && (Bitu)nHeight == (Bitu)height) {
03440         RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackReset);
03441         return;
03442     }
03443     Section_prop * section=static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("sdl")); 
03444     if ((!strcmp(section->Get_string("windowresolution"),"original") || (!strcmp(section->Get_string("windowresolution"),"desktop"))) && (render.src.dblw && render.src.dblh)) {
03445         switch (render.scale.op) {
03446             case scalerOpNormal:
03447                 if(!render.scale.hardware) {
03448                     if((Bitu)nWidth>(Bitu)width || (Bitu)nHeight>(Bitu)height) {
03449                         if (render.scale.size <= 4 && render.scale.size >=1) ++render.scale.size; break;
03450                     } else {
03451                         if (render.scale.size <= 5 && render.scale.size >= 2) --render.scale.size; break;
03452                     }
03453                 } else {
03454                     if((Bitu)nWidth>(Bitu)width || (Bitu)nHeight>(Bitu)height) {
03455                         if (render.scale.size == 1) { render.scale.size=4; break; }
03456                         if (render.scale.size == 4) { render.scale.size=6; break; }
03457                         if (render.scale.size == 6) { render.scale.size=8; break; }
03458                         if (render.scale.size == 8) { render.scale.size=10; break; }
03459                     }
03460                     if((Bitu)nWidth<(Bitu)width || (Bitu)nHeight<(Bitu)height) {
03461                         if (render.scale.size == 10) { render.scale.size=8; break; }
03462                         if (render.scale.size == 8) { render.scale.size=6; break; }
03463                         if (render.scale.size == 6) { render.scale.size=4; break; }
03464                         if (render.scale.size == 4) { render.scale.size=1; break; }
03465                     }
03466                 }
03467                 break;
03468             case scalerOpAdvMame:
03469             case scalerOpHQ:
03470             case scalerOpAdvInterp:
03471             case scalerOpTV:
03472             case scalerOpRGB:
03473             case scalerOpScan:
03474                 if((Bitu)nWidth>(Bitu)width || (Bitu)nHeight>(Bitu)height) { if (render.scale.size == 2) ++render.scale.size; }
03475                 if((Bitu)nWidth<(Bitu)width || (Bitu)nHeight<(Bitu)height) { if (render.scale.size == 3) --render.scale.size; }
03476                 break;
03477             case scalerOpSaI:
03478             case scalerOpSuperSaI:
03479             case scalerOpSuperEagle:
03480             default: // other scalers
03481                 break;
03482         }
03483     }
03484 #endif
03485     RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackReset);
03486 }
03487 
03488 void GFX_RedrawScreen(Bit32u nWidth, Bit32u nHeight) {
03489     RedrawScreen(nWidth, nHeight);
03490 }

03492 bool GFX_MustActOnResize() {
03493     if (!GFX_IsFullscreen())
03494         return false;
03495 
03496     return true;
03497 }
03498 
03499 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03500 void GFX_HandleVideoResize(int width, int height) {
03501     /* Maybe a screen rotation has just occurred, so we simply resize.
03502        There may be a different cause for a forced resized, though.    */
03503     if (sdl.desktop.full.display_res && IsFullscreen()) {
03504         /* Note: We should not use GFX_ObtainDisplayDimensions
03505            (SDL_GetDisplayBounds) on Android after a screen rotation:
03506            The older values from application startup are returned. */
03507         sdl.desktop.full.width = width;
03508         sdl.desktop.full.height = height;
03509     }
03510 
03511     /* assume the resize comes from user preference UNLESS the window
03512      * is fullscreen or maximized */
03513     if (!menu.maxwindow && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen && !sdl.init_ignore && NonUserResizeCounter == 0 && !window_was_maximized) {
03514         UpdateWindowDimensions();
03515         UpdateWindowDimensions((unsigned int)width, (unsigned int)height);
03516 
03517         /* if the dimensions actually changed from our surface dimensions, then
03518            assume it's the user's input. Linux/X11 is good at doing this anyway,
03519            but the Windows SDL 1.x support will return us a resize event for the
03520            window size change resulting from SDL mode set. */
03521         if (width != sdl.surface->w || height != sdl.surface->h) {
03522             userResizeWindowWidth = (unsigned int)width;
03523             userResizeWindowHeight = (unsigned int)height;
03524         }
03525     }
03526     else {
03527         UpdateWindowDimensions();
03528     }
03529 
03530     /* TODO: Only if FULLSCREEN_DESKTOP */
03531     if (screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width != 0 && screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height != 0) {
03532         sdl.desktop.full.width = (Bit16u)screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.width;
03533         sdl.desktop.full.height = (Bit16u)screen_size_info.screen_dimensions_pixels.height;
03534     }
03535     else {
03536         SDL_DisplayMode dm;
03537         if (SDL_GetDesktopDisplayMode(0/*FIXME display index*/,&dm) == 0) {
03538             sdl.desktop.full.width = dm.w;
03539             sdl.desktop.full.height = dm.h;
03540             LOG_MSG("SDL2 reports desktop display mode %u x %u",dm.w,dm.h);
03541         }
03542         else {
03543             LOG_MSG("SDL2 unable to determine desktop display mode, error %s",SDL_GetError());
03544         }
03545     }
03546 
03547     window_was_maximized = menu.maxwindow;
03548     if (NonUserResizeCounter > 0)
03549         NonUserResizeCounter--;
03550 
03551     /* Even if the new window's dimensions are actually the desired ones
03552      * we may still need to re-obtain a new window surface or do
03553      * a different thing. So we basically call GFX_SetSize, but without
03554      * touching the window itself (or else we may end in an infinite loop).
03555      *
03556      * Furthermore, if the new dimensions are *not* the desired ones, we
03557      * don't fight it. Rather than attempting to resize it back, we simply
03558      * keep the window as-is and disable screen updates. This is done
03559      * in SDL_SetSDLWindowSurface by setting sdl.update_display_contents
03560      * to false.
03561      */
03562     sdl.update_window = false;
03563     GFX_ResetScreen();
03564     sdl.update_window = true;
03565 }
03566 #else
03567 static void HandleVideoResize(void * event) {
03568     if(sdl.desktop.fullscreen) return;
03569 
03570     /* don't act on resize events if we made the window non-resizeable.
03571      * especially if 3Dfx voodoo emulation is active. */
03572     if (!(sdl.surface->flags & SDL_RESIZABLE)) return;
03573 
03574     /* don't act if 3Dfx OpenGL emulation is active */
03575     if (GFX_GetPreventFullscreen()) return;
03576 
03577     SDL_ResizeEvent* ResizeEvent = (SDL_ResizeEvent*)event;
03578 
03579     /* assume the resize comes from user preference UNLESS the window
03580      * is fullscreen or maximized */
03581     if (!menu.maxwindow && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen && !sdl.init_ignore && NonUserResizeCounter == 0 && !window_was_maximized) {
03582         UpdateWindowDimensions();
03583         UpdateWindowDimensions((unsigned int)ResizeEvent->w, (unsigned int)ResizeEvent->h);
03584 
03585         /* if the dimensions actually changed from our surface dimensions, then
03586            assume it's the user's input. Linux/X11 is good at doing this anyway,
03587            but the Windows SDL 1.x support will return us a resize event for the
03588            window size change resulting from SDL mode set. */
03589         if (ResizeEvent->w != sdl.surface->w || ResizeEvent->h != sdl.surface->h) {
03590             userResizeWindowWidth = (unsigned int)ResizeEvent->w;
03591             userResizeWindowHeight = (unsigned int)ResizeEvent->h;
03592         }
03593     }
03594     else {
03595         UpdateWindowDimensions();
03596     }
03597 
03598     window_was_maximized = menu.maxwindow;
03599     if (NonUserResizeCounter > 0)
03600         NonUserResizeCounter--;
03601 
03602     if (sdl.updating && !GFX_MustActOnResize()) {
03603         /* act on resize when updating is complete */
03604         sdl.deferred_resize = true;
03605     }
03606     else {
03607         sdl.deferred_resize = false;
03608         RedrawScreen((unsigned int)ResizeEvent->w, (unsigned int)ResizeEvent->h);
03609     }
03610 #ifdef WIN32
03611     menu.resizeusing=false;
03612 #endif
03613 }
03614 #endif

03616 extern unsigned int mouse_notify_mode;
03617 
03618 bool user_cursor_locked = false;
03619 MOUSE_EMULATION user_cursor_emulation = MOUSE_EMULATION_NEVER;
03620 int user_cursor_x = 0,user_cursor_y = 0;
03621 int user_cursor_sw = 640,user_cursor_sh = 480;

03623 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW /* SDL drawn menus */
03624 DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t DOSBoxMenu::displaylist::itemFromPoint(DOSBoxMenu &menu,int x,int y) {
03625     for (auto &id : disp_list) {
03626         DOSBoxMenu::item &item = menu.get_item(id);
03627         if (x >= item.screenBox.x && y >= item.screenBox.y) {
03628             int sx = x - item.screenBox.x;
03629             int sy = y - item.screenBox.y;
03630             int adj = (this != &menu.display_list && item.get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::submenu_type_id) ? 2 : 0;
03631             if (sx < (item.screenBox.w+adj) && sy < item.screenBox.h)
03632                 return id;
03633         }
03634     }
03635 
03636     return unassigned_item_handle;
03637 }
03638 
03639 void DOSBoxMenu::item::updateScreenFromItem(DOSBoxMenu &menu) {
03640     (void)menu;//UNUSED
03641     if (!OpenGL_using()) {
03642         SDL_Rect uprect = screenBox;
03643 
03644         SDL_rect_cliptoscreen(uprect);
03645 
03646 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03647         SDL_UpdateWindowSurfaceRects(sdl.window, &uprect, 1);
03648 #else
03649         SDL_UpdateRects( sdl.surface, 1, &uprect );
03650 #endif
03651     }
03652 }
03653 
03654 void DOSBoxMenu::item::updateScreenFromPopup(DOSBoxMenu &menu) {
03655     (void)menu;//UNUSED
03656     if (!OpenGL_using()) {
03657         SDL_Rect uprect = popupBox;
03658 
03659         uprect.w += DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX;
03660         uprect.h += DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY;
03661         SDL_rect_cliptoscreen(uprect);
03662 
03663 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03664         SDL_UpdateWindowSurfaceRects(sdl.window, &uprect, 1);
03665 #else
03666         SDL_UpdateRects( sdl.surface, 1, &uprect );
03667 #endif
03668     }
03669 }
03670 
03671 void DOSBoxMenu::item::drawBackground(DOSBoxMenu &menu) {
03672     (void)menu;//UNUSED
03673     Bitu bordercolor = GFX_GetRGB(31, 31, 31);
03674     Bitu bgcolor = GFX_GetRGB(63, 63, 63);
03675 
03676     if (popupBox.w <= 1 || popupBox.h <= 1)
03677         return;
03678 
03679     MenuDrawRect(popupBox.x, popupBox.y, popupBox.w, popupBox.h, bgcolor);
03680 
03681     if (borderTop)
03682         MenuDrawRect(popupBox.x, popupBox.y, popupBox.w, 1, bordercolor);
03683 
03684     MenuDrawRect(popupBox.x, popupBox.y + popupBox.h - 1, popupBox.w, 1, bordercolor);
03685 
03686     MenuDrawRect(popupBox.x, popupBox.y, 1, popupBox.h, bordercolor);
03687     MenuDrawRect(popupBox.x + popupBox.w - 1, popupBox.y, 1, popupBox.h, bordercolor);
03688 
03689     if (type == DOSBoxMenu::submenu_type_id) {
03690         MenuShadeRect((int)popupBox.x + (int)popupBox.w, (int)popupBox.y + (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY,
03691                       (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX, (int)popupBox.h);
03692         MenuShadeRect((int)popupBox.x + (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX, (int)popupBox.y + (int)popupBox.h,
03693                       (int)popupBox.w - (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX, (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY);
03694     }
03695 }
03696 #endif

03698 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW /* SDL drawn menus */
03699 void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id) {
03700     (void)menu;//UNUSED
03701     if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != item_id) {
03702         if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
03703             auto &item = mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt);
03704             item.setHover(mainMenu,false);
03705             if (item.checkResetRedraw()) {
03706                 item.drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
03707                 item.updateScreenFromItem(mainMenu);
03708             }
03709         }
03710 
03711         mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt = item_id;
03712 
03713         if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
03714             auto &item = mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt);
03715             item.setHover(mainMenu,true);
03716             if (item.checkResetRedraw()) {
03717                 item.drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
03718                 item.updateScreenFromItem(mainMenu);
03719             }
03720         }
03721 
03722         if (OpenGL_using())
03723             mainMenu.setRedraw();
03724     }
03725 }

03734                 item.drawMenuItem(mainMenu);

03737         }
03738

03740 
03741         if (mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
03742             auto &item = mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt);
03743             item.setHilight(mainMenu,true);
03744             if (item.checkResetRedraw()) {
03745                 item.drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
03746                 item.updateScreenFromItem(mainMenu);
03747             }
03748         }
03749

03751             mainMenu.setRedraw();
