03755 
03756 uint8_t Mouse_GetButtonState(void);
03757 
03758 bool GFX_CursorInOrNearScreen(int wx,int wy) {
03759     int minx = sdl.clip.x - (sdl.clip.w / 10);
03760     int miny = sdl.clip.y - (sdl.clip.h / 10);
03761     int maxx = sdl.clip.x + sdl.clip.w + (sdl.clip.w / 10);
03762     int maxy = sdl.clip.y + sdl.clip.h + (sdl.clip.h / 10);
03763 
03764     return  (wx >= minx && wx < maxx) && (wy >= miny && wy < maxy);
03765 }
03766 
03767 static void HandleMouseMotion(SDL_MouseMotionEvent * motion) {
03768     bool inputToScreen = false;
03769 
03770     /* limit mouse input to whenever the cursor is on the screen, or near the edge of the screen. */
03771     if (is_paused)
03772         inputToScreen = false;
03773     else if (sdl.mouse.locked || Mouse_GetButtonState() != 0)
03774         inputToScreen = true;
03775     else
03776         inputToScreen = GFX_CursorInOrNearScreen(motion->x,motion->y);
03777 
03778 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW /* SDL drawn menus */
03779     if (GFX_GetPreventFullscreen()) {
03780         /* do NOT draw SDL menu in OpenGL mode when 3Dfx emulation is using OpenGL */
03781     }
03782     else if (!sdl.mouse.locked && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen && mainMenu.isVisible() && motion->y < mainMenu.menuBox.h && Mouse_GetButtonState() == 0) {
03783         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list.itemFromPoint(mainMenu,motion->x,motion->y));
03784         SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_ENABLE);
03785 
03786         if (OpenGL_using() && mainMenu.needsRedraw()) {
03787 #if C_OPENGL
03788             sdl_opengl.menudraw_countdown = 2; // two GL buffers
03789             GFX_OpenGLRedrawScreen();
03790             GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
03791 # if defined(C_SDL2)
03792             SDL_GL_SwapWindow(sdl.window);
03793 # else
03794             SDL_GL_SwapBuffers();
03795 # endif
03796 #endif
03797         }
03798  
03799         return;
03800     }
03801     else {
03802         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
03803 
03804         if (OpenGL_using() && mainMenu.needsRedraw()) {
03805 #if C_OPENGL
03806             sdl_opengl.menudraw_countdown = 2; // two GL buffers
03807             GFX_OpenGLRedrawScreen();
03808             GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
03809 # if defined(C_SDL2)
03810             SDL_GL_SwapWindow(sdl.window);
03811 # else
03812             SDL_GL_SwapBuffers();
03813 # endif
03814 #endif
03815         }
03816     }
03817 #endif
03818 
03819     if (!inputToScreen) {
03820 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03821         if (!sdl.mouse.locked)
03822 #else
03823         /* SDL1 has some sort of weird mouse warping bug in fullscreen mode no matter whether the mouse is captured or not (Windows, Linux/X11) */
03824         if (!sdl.mouse.locked && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen)
03825 #endif
03826             SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_ENABLE);
03827  
03828         return;
03829     }
03830 
03831     user_cursor_x      = motion->x - sdl.clip.x;
03832     user_cursor_y      = motion->y - sdl.clip.y;
03833     user_cursor_locked = sdl.mouse.locked;
03834     user_cursor_emulation = sdl.mouse.emulation;
03835     user_cursor_sw     = sdl.clip.w;
03836     user_cursor_sh     = sdl.clip.h;
03837 
03838     auto xrel = static_cast<float>(motion->xrel) * sdl.mouse.xsensitivity / 100.0f;
03839     auto yrel = static_cast<float>(motion->yrel) * sdl.mouse.ysensitivity / 100.0f;
03840     auto x    = static_cast<float>(motion->x - sdl.clip.x) / (sdl.clip.w - 1) * sdl.mouse.xsensitivity / 100.0f;
03841     auto y    = static_cast<float>(motion->y - sdl.clip.y) / (sdl.clip.h - 1) * sdl.mouse.ysensitivity / 100.0f;
03842     auto emu  = sdl.mouse.locked;
03843 
03844     const auto inside =
03845         motion->x >= sdl.clip.x && motion->x < sdl.clip.x + sdl.clip.w &&
03846         motion->y >= sdl.clip.y && motion->y < sdl.clip.y + sdl.clip.h;
03847 
03848     if (mouse_notify_mode != 0)
03849     {
03850         /* for mouse integration driver */
03851         if (!sdl.mouse.locked)
03852             xrel = yrel = x = y = 0.0f;
03853 
03854         emu               = sdl.mouse.locked;
03855         const auto isdown = Mouse_GetButtonState() != 0;
03856 
03857 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03858         if (!sdl.mouse.locked)
03859 #else
03860         /* SDL1 has some sort of weird mouse warping bug in fullscreen mode no matter whether the mouse is captured or not (Windows, Linux/X11) */
03861         if (!sdl.mouse.locked && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen)
03862 #endif
03863             SDL_ShowCursor((isdown || inside) ? SDL_DISABLE : SDL_ENABLE);
03864     }
03865     else if (!user_cursor_locked)
03866     {
03867         extern bool MOUSE_HasInterruptSub();
03868         extern bool MOUSE_IsBeingPolled();
03869         extern bool MOUSE_IsHidden();
03870         /* Show only when DOS app is not using mouse */
03871 
03872 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03873         if (!sdl.mouse.locked)
03874 #else
03875         /* SDL1 has some sort of weird mouse warping bug in fullscreen mode no matter whether the mouse is captured or not (Windows, Linux/X11) */
03876         if (!sdl.mouse.locked && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen)
03877 #endif
03878             SDL_ShowCursor(((!inside) || ((MOUSE_IsHidden()) && !(MOUSE_IsBeingPolled() || MOUSE_HasInterruptSub()))) ? SDL_ENABLE : SDL_DISABLE);
03879     }
03880     Mouse_CursorMoved(xrel, yrel, x, y, emu);
03881 }
03882 
03883 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW /* SDL drawn menus */
03884 void MenuFullScreenRedraw(void) {
03885 #if defined(C_SDL2)
03886     SDL_UpdateWindowSurface(sdl.window);
03887 #else
03888     SDL_Flip(sdl.surface);
03889 #endif
03890 }
03891 
03892 static struct {
03893     unsigned char*      bmp = NULL;
03894     unsigned int        stride = 0,height = 0;
03895 } menuSavedScreen;
03896 
03897 void MenuSaveScreen(void) {
03898     if (!OpenGL_using()) {
03899         if (menuSavedScreen.bmp == NULL) {
03900             menuSavedScreen.height = (unsigned int)sdl.surface->h;
03901             menuSavedScreen.stride = (unsigned int)sdl.surface->pitch;
03902             menuSavedScreen.bmp = new unsigned char[menuSavedScreen.height * menuSavedScreen.stride];
03903         }
03904 
03905         if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
03906             SDL_LockSurface(sdl.surface);
03907 
03908         memcpy(menuSavedScreen.bmp, sdl.surface->pixels, menuSavedScreen.height * menuSavedScreen.stride);
03909 
03910         if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
03911             SDL_UnlockSurface(sdl.surface);
03912     }
03913 }
03914 
03915 void MenuRestoreScreen(void) {
03916     if (!OpenGL_using()) {
03917         if (menuSavedScreen.bmp == NULL)
03918             return;
03919 
03920         if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
03921             SDL_LockSurface(sdl.surface);
03922 
03923         memcpy(sdl.surface->pixels, menuSavedScreen.bmp, menuSavedScreen.height * menuSavedScreen.stride);
03924 
03925         if (SDL_MUSTLOCK(sdl.surface))
03926             SDL_UnlockSurface(sdl.surface);
03927     }
03928 }
03929 
03930 void MenuFreeScreen(void) {
03931     if (menuSavedScreen.bmp == NULL)
03932         return;
03933 
03934     delete[] menuSavedScreen.bmp;
03935     menuSavedScreen.bmp = NULL;
03936 }
03937 #endif
03938 
03939 static void HandleMouseButton(SDL_MouseButtonEvent * button) {
03940     bool inputToScreen = false;
03941     bool inMenu = false;
03942 
03943 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW /* SDL drawn menus */
03944     if (GFX_GetPreventFullscreen()) {
03945         /* do NOT draw SDL menu in OpenGL mode when 3Dfx emulation is using OpenGL */
03946         mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt = DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle;
03947     }
03948     else if (!sdl.mouse.locked && !sdl.desktop.fullscreen && mainMenu.isVisible() && button->y < mainMenu.menuBox.h) {
03949         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list.itemFromPoint(mainMenu,button->x,button->y));
03950         inMenu = true;
03951     }
03952     else {
03953         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
03954     }
03955 
03956     if (button->button == SDL_BUTTON_LEFT) {
03957         if (button->state == SDL_PRESSED) {
03958             GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt);
03959             if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
03960                 std::vector<DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t> popup_stack;
03961                 DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t choice_item;
03962                 DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t psel_item;
03963                 DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t sel_item;
03964                 bool button_holding=true;
03965                 bool redrawAll=false;
03966                 bool resized=false;
03967                 bool runloop=true;
03968                 SDL_Rect uprect;
03969                 SDL_Event event;
03970 
03971                 psel_item = DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle;
03972                 choice_item = mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt = mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt;
03973 
03974                 popup_stack.push_back(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt);
03975 
03976 #if C_DIRECT3D
03977         if (sdl.desktop.want_type == SCREEN_DIRECT3D) {
03978             /* In output=direct3d mode, SDL still has a surface but this code ignores SDL
03979              * and draws directly to a Direct3D9 backbuffer which is presented to the window
03980              * client area. However, GDI output to the window still works, and this code
03981              * uses the SDL surface still. Therefore, for menus to draw correctly atop the
03982              * Direct3D output, this code copies the Direct3D backbuffer to the SDL surface
03983              * first.
03984              *
03985              * WARNING: This happens to work with Windows (even Windows 10 build 18xx as of
03986              * 2018/05/21) because Windows appears to permit mixing Direct3D and GDI rendering
03987              * to the window.
03988              *
03989              * Someday, if Microsoft should break that ability, this code will need to be
03990              * revised to send screen "updates" to the Direct3D backbuffer first, then
03991              * Present to the window client area. */
03992             if (d3d) d3d->UpdateRectToSDLSurface(0, 0, sdl.surface->w, sdl.surface->h);
03993         }
03994 #endif
03995 
03996                 if (OpenGL_using()) {
03997 #if C_OPENGL
03998                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHilight(mainMenu,false);
03999                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04000 
04001                     /* show the menu */
04002                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHilight(mainMenu,true);
04003                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHover(mainMenu,true);
04004 
04005                     glClearColor (0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
04006                     glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT);
04007 
04008                     GFX_OpenGLRedrawScreen();
04009 
04010                     /* give the menu bar a drop shadow */
04011                     MenuShadeRect(
04012                             (int)mainMenu.menuBox.x + (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX,
04013                             (int)mainMenu.menuBox.y + (int)mainMenu.menuBox.h,
04014                             (int)mainMenu.menuBox.w,
04015                             (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY - 1/*menubar border*/);
04016 
04017                     mainMenu.setRedraw();                  
04018                     GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
04019 
04020                     for (auto i=popup_stack.begin();i!=popup_stack.end();i++) {
04021                         if (mainMenu.get_item(*i).get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::submenu_type_id) {
04022                             mainMenu.get_item(*i).drawBackground(mainMenu);
04023                             mainMenu.get_item(*i).display_list.DrawDisplayList(mainMenu,/*updateScreen*/false);
04024                         }
04025                     }
04026 
04027 # if defined(C_SDL2)
04028                     SDL_GL_SwapWindow(sdl.window);
04029 # else
04030                     SDL_GL_SwapBuffers();
04031 # endif
04032 #endif
04033                 }
04034                 else {
04035                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHilight(mainMenu,false);
04036                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04037                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
04038                     MenuSaveScreen();
04039 
04040                     /* give the menu bar a drop shadow */
04041                     MenuShadeRect(
04042                             (int)mainMenu.menuBox.x + (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX,
04043                             (int)mainMenu.menuBox.y + (int)mainMenu.menuBox.h,
04044                             (int)mainMenu.menuBox.w,
04045                             (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY - 1/*menubar border*/);
04046 
04047                     uprect.x = 0;
04048                     uprect.y = mainMenu.menuBox.y + mainMenu.menuBox.h;
04049                     uprect.w = mainMenu.menuBox.w;
04050                     uprect.h = DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY;
04051 #if defined(C_SDL2)
04052                     SDL_UpdateWindowSurfaceRects(sdl.window, &uprect, 1);
04053 #else
04054                     SDL_UpdateRects( sdl.surface, 1, &uprect );
04055 #endif
04056 
04057                     /* show the menu */
04058                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHilight(mainMenu,true);
04059                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).setHover(mainMenu,true);
04060                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).drawBackground(mainMenu);
04061                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).display_list.DrawDisplayList(mainMenu,/*updateScreen*/false);
04062                     mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt).updateScreenFromPopup(mainMenu);
04063                 }
04064 
04065                 /* hack */
04066                 mainMenu.menuUserAttentionAt = DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle;
04067 
04068                 /* fall into another loop to process the menu */
04069                 while (runloop) {
04070 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
04071                     emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
04072                     if (!SDL_PollEvent(&event)) continue;
04073 #else
04074                     if (!SDL_WaitEvent(&event)) break;
04075 #endif
04076 
04077 #if defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(IGNORE_TOUCHSCREEN)
04078                     switch (event.type) {
04079                         case SDL_FINGERDOWN:
04080                             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == no_finger_id &&
04081                                 touchscreen_touch_lock == no_touch_id) {
04082                                 touchscreen_finger_lock = event.tfinger.fingerId;
04083                                 touchscreen_touch_lock = event.tfinger.touchId;
04084                                 Sint32 x,y;
04085 
04086                                 x = (Sint32)(event.tfinger.x * currentWindowWidth);
04087                                 y = (Sint32)(event.tfinger.y * currentWindowHeight);
04088 
04089                                 memset(&event.button,0,sizeof(event.button));
04090                                 event.type = SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN;
04091                                 event.button.x = x;
04092                                 event.button.y = y;
04093                             }
04094                             else {
04095                                 event.type = -1;
04096                             }
04097                             break;
04098                         case SDL_FINGERUP:
04099                             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == event.tfinger.fingerId &&
04100                                 touchscreen_touch_lock == event.tfinger.touchId) {
04101                                 touchscreen_finger_lock = no_finger_id;
04102                                 touchscreen_touch_lock = no_touch_id;
04103                                 Sint32 x,y;
04104 
04105                                 x = (Sint32)(event.tfinger.x * currentWindowWidth);
04106                                 y = (Sint32)(event.tfinger.y * currentWindowHeight);
04107                                 
04108                                 memset(&event.button,0,sizeof(event.button));
04109                                 event.type = SDL_MOUSEBUTTONUP;
04110                                 event.button.x = x;
04111                                 event.button.y = y;
04112                             }
04113                             else {
04114                                 event.type = -1;
04115                             }
04116                             break;
04117                         case SDL_FINGERMOTION:
04118                             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == event.tfinger.fingerId &&
04119                                 touchscreen_touch_lock == event.tfinger.touchId) {
04120                                 Sint32 x,y;
04121 
04122                                 x = (Sint32)(event.tfinger.x * currentWindowWidth);
04123                                 y = (Sint32)(event.tfinger.y * currentWindowHeight);
04124 
04125                                 memset(&event.button,0,sizeof(event.button));
04126                                 event.type = SDL_MOUSEMOTION;
04127                                 event.button.x = x;
04128                                 event.button.y = y;
04129                             }
04130                             else if (touchscreen_finger_lock != no_finger_id ||
04131                                      touchscreen_touch_lock != no_touch_id) {
04132                                 event.type = -1;
04133                             }
04134                             break;
04135                     }
04136 #endif
04137 
04138                     switch (event.type) {
04139                         case SDL_QUIT:
04140                             throw(0);
04141                             break;
04142                         case SDL_KEYUP:
04143                             if (event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_ESCAPE) {
04144                                 choice_item = DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle;
04145                                 runloop = false;
04146                             }
04147                             break;
04148 #if defined(C_SDL2)
04149                         case SDL_WINDOWEVENT:
04150                             switch (event.window.event) {
04151                                 case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_RESIZED:
04152                                     GFX_HandleVideoResize(event.window.data1, event.window.data2);
04153                                     runloop = false;
04154                                     resized = true;
04155                                     break;
04156                                 default:
04157                                     break;
04158                             }
04159 #endif
04160 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
04161                         case SDL_VIDEORESIZE:
04162                             UpdateWindowDimensions(); // FIXME: Use SDL window dimensions, except that on Windows, SDL won't tell us our actual dimensions
04163                             HandleVideoResize(&event.resize);
04164 
04165                             runloop = false;
04166                             resized = true;
04167                             break;
04168 #endif
04169                         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN:
04170                             button_holding=true;
04171                             choice_item = mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt;
04172                             if (choice_item != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
04173                                 DOSBoxMenu::item &item = mainMenu.get_item(choice_item);
04174                                 item.setHilight(mainMenu,true);
04175                                 item.drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
04176                                 if (OpenGL_using())
04177                                     redrawAll = true;
04178                                 else
04179                                     item.updateScreenFromItem(mainMenu);
04180                             }
04181                             else {
04182                                 /* clicking on nothing should dismiss */
04183                                 runloop = false;
04184                             }
04185                             break;
04186                         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONUP:
04187                             button_holding=false;
04188                             choice_item = mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt;
04189                             if (choice_item != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
04190                                 if (choice_item == psel_item) { /* clicking something twice should dismiss */
04191                                     runloop = false;
04192                                 }
04193                                 else {
04194                                     DOSBoxMenu::item &item = mainMenu.get_item(choice_item);
04195                                     if (item.get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::item_type_id && item.is_enabled())
04196                                         runloop = false;
04197                                 }
04198 
04199                                 psel_item = choice_item;
04200                             }
04201                             else {
04202                                 /* not selecting anything counts as a reason to exit */
04203                                 runloop = false;
04204                             }
04205                             break;
04206                         case SDL_MOUSEMOTION:
04207                             {
04208                                 bool noRedrawNew = false,noRedrawOld = false;
04209 
04210                                 sel_item = DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle;
04211 
04212                                 auto search = popup_stack.end();
04213                                 if (search != popup_stack.begin()) {
04214                                     do {
04215                                         search--;
04216 
04217                                         sel_item = mainMenu.get_item(*search).display_list.itemFromPoint(mainMenu,event.button.x,event.button.y);
04218                                         if (sel_item != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
04219                                             assert(search != popup_stack.end());
04220                                             search++;
04221                                             break;
04222                                         }
04223                                     } while (search != popup_stack.begin());
04224                                 }
04225 
04226                                 if (sel_item == DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle)
04227                                     sel_item = mainMenu.display_list.itemFromPoint(mainMenu,event.button.x,event.button.y);
04228 
04229                                 /* at this point:
04230                                  *  sel_item = item under cursor, or unassigned if no item
04231                                  *  search = iterator just past the item's level (to remove items if changing) */
04232 
04233                                 if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != sel_item) {
04234                                     if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
04235                                         mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04236                                         if (mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::item_type_id)
04237                                             mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).setHilight(mainMenu,false);
04238                                         else if (mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::submenu_type_id) {
04239                                             if (mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).isHilight()) {
04240                                                 noRedrawOld = true;
04241                                             }
04242                                         }
04243                                     }
04244 
04245                                     if (sel_item != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
04246                                         if (mainMenu.get_item(sel_item).get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::submenu_type_id) {
04247                                             if (!mainMenu.get_item(sel_item).isHilight()) {
04248                                                 /* use a copy of the iterator to scan forward and un-hilight the menu items.
04249                                                  * then use the original iterator to erase from the vector. */
04250                                                 for (auto ss=search;ss != popup_stack.end();ss++) {
04251                                                     for (auto &id : mainMenu.get_item(*ss).display_list.get_disp_list())
04252                                                         mainMenu.get_item(id).setHilight(mainMenu,false).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04253 
04254                                                     mainMenu.get_item(*ss).setHilight(mainMenu,false).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04255                                                 }
04256 
04257                                                 popup_stack.erase(search,popup_stack.end());
04258                                                 mainMenu.get_item(sel_item).setHilight(mainMenu,true).setHover(mainMenu,true);
04259                                                 popup_stack.push_back(sel_item);
04260                                                 redrawAll = true;
04261                                             }
04262                                             else {
04263                                                 /* no change in item state, don't bother redrawing */
04264                                                 noRedrawNew = true;
04265                                             }
04266                                         }
04267                                         else {
04268                                             /* use a copy of the iterator to scan forward and un-hilight the menu items.
04269                                              * then use the original iterator to erase from the vector. */
04270                                             for (auto ss=search;ss != popup_stack.end();ss++) {
04271                                                 for (auto &id : mainMenu.get_item(*ss).display_list.get_disp_list())
04272                                                     mainMenu.get_item(id).setHilight(mainMenu,false).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04273 
04274                                                 mainMenu.get_item(*ss).setHilight(mainMenu,false).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04275                                                 redrawAll = true;
04276                                             }
04277 
04278                                             popup_stack.erase(search,popup_stack.end());
04279                                         }
04280 
04281                                         if (OpenGL_using())
04282                                             redrawAll = true;
04283 
04284                                         mainMenu.get_item(sel_item).setHover(mainMenu,true);
04285                                         if (mainMenu.get_item(sel_item).get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::item_type_id && button_holding)
04286                                             mainMenu.get_item(sel_item).setHilight(mainMenu,true);
04287                                     }
04288                                     else {
04289                                         if (OpenGL_using())
04290                                             redrawAll = true;
04291                                     }
04292 
04293                                     if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle && !OpenGL_using() && !redrawAll && !noRedrawOld) {
04294                                         if (mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).checkResetRedraw()) {
04295                                             mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
04296                                             mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).updateScreenFromItem(mainMenu);
04297                                         }
04298                                     }
04299 
04300                                     mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt = sel_item;
04301 
04302                                     if (mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle && !OpenGL_using() && !redrawAll && !noRedrawNew) {
04303                                         if (mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).checkResetRedraw()) {
04304                                             mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).drawMenuItem(mainMenu);
04305                                             mainMenu.get_item(mainMenu.menuUserHoverAt).updateScreenFromItem(mainMenu);
04306                                         }
04307                                     }
04308                                 }
04309                             }
04310                             break;
04311                     }
04312 
04313                     if (redrawAll) {
04314                         redrawAll = false;
04315 
04316 #if 0/*DEBUG*/
04317                         LOG_MSG("Redraw %u",(unsigned int)SDL_GetTicks());
04318 #endif
04319 
04320                         if (OpenGL_using()) {
04321 #if C_OPENGL
04322                             glClearColor (0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
04323                             glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT);
04324 
04325                             GFX_OpenGLRedrawScreen();
04326   
04327                             mainMenu.setRedraw();                  
04328                             GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
04329 #endif
04330                         }
04331                         else {
04332                             MenuRestoreScreen();
04333                             mainMenu.display_list.DrawDisplayList(mainMenu,/*updateScreen*/false);
04334                         }
04335 
04336                         /* give the menu bar a drop shadow */
04337                         MenuShadeRect(
04338                                 (int)mainMenu.menuBox.x + (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowX,
04339                                 (int)mainMenu.menuBox.y + (int)mainMenu.menuBox.h,
04340                                 (int)mainMenu.menuBox.w,
04341                                 (int)DOSBoxMenu::dropshadowY - 1/*menubar border*/);
04342 
04343                         for (auto i=popup_stack.begin();i!=popup_stack.end();i++) {
04344                             if (mainMenu.get_item(*i).get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::submenu_type_id) {
04345                                 mainMenu.get_item(*i).drawBackground(mainMenu);
04346                                 mainMenu.get_item(*i).display_list.DrawDisplayList(mainMenu,/*updateScreen*/false);
04347                             }
04348                         }
04349 
04350 #if C_OPENGL
04351                         if (OpenGL_using()) {
04352 # if defined(C_SDL2)
04353                             SDL_GL_SwapWindow(sdl.window);
04354 # else
04355                             SDL_GL_SwapBuffers();
04356 # endif
04357                         }
04358                         else
04359 #endif
04360                             MenuFullScreenRedraw();
04361                     }
04362                 }
04363 
04364 #if defined(C_SDL2)
04365                 /* force touchscreen mapping to let go */
04366                 touchscreen_finger_lock = no_finger_id;
04367                 touchscreen_touch_lock = no_touch_id;
04368 #endif
04369 
04370                 /* then return */
04371                 GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04372                 GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04373                 if (!resized) {
04374                     MenuRestoreScreen();
04375                     if (!OpenGL_using())
04376                         MenuFullScreenRedraw();
04377                 }
04378                 MenuFreeScreen();
04379 
04380                 while (!popup_stack.empty()) {
04381                     DOSBoxMenu::item &item = mainMenu.get_item(popup_stack.back());
04382 
04383                     for (auto &id : item.display_list.get_disp_list()) {
04384                         mainMenu.get_item(id).setHilight(mainMenu,false);
04385                         mainMenu.get_item(id).setHover(mainMenu,false);
04386                     }
04387 
04388                     item.setHilight(mainMenu,false);
04389                     item.setHover(mainMenu,false);
04390                     popup_stack.pop_back();
04391                 }
04392 
04393                 if (OpenGL_using()) {
04394 #if C_OPENGL
04395                     glClearColor (0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 1.0);
04396                     glClear(GL_COLOR_BUFFER_BIT);
04397         
04398                     GFX_OpenGLRedrawScreen();
04399 
04400                     mainMenu.setRedraw();
04401                     GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
04402 
04403 # if defined(C_SDL2)
04404                     SDL_GL_SwapWindow(sdl.window);
04405 # else
04406                     SDL_GL_SwapBuffers();
04407 # endif
04408 
04409                     sdl_opengl.clear_countdown = 2;
04410                     sdl_opengl.menudraw_countdown = 2; // two GL buffers
04411 #endif
04412                 }
04413 
04414                 /* action! */
04415                 if (!resized && choice_item != DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle) {
04416                     DOSBoxMenu::item &item = mainMenu.get_item(choice_item);
04417 
04418                     if (item.get_type() == DOSBoxMenu::item_type_id && item.is_enabled())
04419                         mainMenu.dispatchItemCommand(item);
04420                 }
04421 
04422                 return;
04423             }
04424         }
04425         else {
04426             GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04427         }
04428     }
04429 #endif
04430 
04431     /* limit mouse input to whenever the cursor is on the screen, or near the edge of the screen. */
04432     if (is_paused)
04433         inputToScreen = false;
04434     else if (sdl.mouse.locked)
04435         inputToScreen = true;
04436     else if (!inMenu)
04437         inputToScreen = GFX_CursorInOrNearScreen(button->x, button->y);
04438 
04439     switch (button->state) {
04440     case SDL_PRESSED:
04441         if (inMenu || !inputToScreen) return;
04442         if (sdl.mouse.requestlock && !sdl.mouse.locked && mouse_notify_mode == 0) {
04443             CaptureMouseNotify();
04444             GFX_CaptureMouse();
04445             // Don't pass click to mouse handler
04446             break;
04447         }
04448         if (!sdl.mouse.autoenable && sdl.mouse.autolock && mouse_notify_mode == 0 && button->button == SDL_BUTTON_MIDDLE) {
04449             GFX_CaptureMouse();
04450             break;
04451         }
04452         switch (button->button) {
04453         case SDL_BUTTON_LEFT:
04454             Mouse_ButtonPressed(0);
04455             break;
04456         case SDL_BUTTON_RIGHT:
04457             Mouse_ButtonPressed(1);
04458             break;
04459         case SDL_BUTTON_MIDDLE:
04460             Mouse_ButtonPressed(2);
04461             break;
04462 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
04463         case SDL_BUTTON_WHEELUP: /* Ick, really SDL? */
04464             Mouse_ButtonPressed(100-1);
04465             break;
04466         case SDL_BUTTON_WHEELDOWN: /* Ick, really SDL? */
04467             Mouse_ButtonPressed(100+1);
04468             break;
04469 #endif
04470         }
04471         break;
04472     case SDL_RELEASED:
04473         switch (button->button) {
04474         case SDL_BUTTON_LEFT:
04475             Mouse_ButtonReleased(0);
04476             break;
04477         case SDL_BUTTON_RIGHT:
04478             Mouse_ButtonReleased(1);
04479             break;
04480         case SDL_BUTTON_MIDDLE:
04481             Mouse_ButtonReleased(2);
04482             break;
04483 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
04484         case SDL_BUTTON_WHEELUP: /* Ick, really SDL? */
04485             Mouse_ButtonReleased(100-1);
04486             break;
04487         case SDL_BUTTON_WHEELDOWN: /* Ick, really SDL? */
04488             Mouse_ButtonReleased(100+1);
04489             break;
04490 #endif
04491         }
04492         break;
04493     }
04494 }
04495 
04496 void GFX_LosingFocus(void) {
04497     sdl.laltstate=SDL_KEYUP;
04498     sdl.raltstate=SDL_KEYUP;
04499     MAPPER_LosingFocus();
04500     DoExtendedKeyboardHook(false);
04501 }

04504 static bool PasteClipboardNext(); // added emendelson from dbDOS
04505 #endif
04506 
04507 bool GFX_IsFullscreen(void) {
04508     return sdl.desktop.fullscreen;
04509 }

04511 void* GetSetSDLValue(int isget, std::string target, void* setval) {
04512     if (target == "wait_on_error") {
04513         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.wait_on_error;
04514         else sdl.wait_on_error = setval;
04515     }
04516     else if (target == "opengl.bilinear") {
04517 #if C_OPENGL
04518         if (isget) return (void*) sdl_opengl.bilinear;
04519         else sdl_opengl.bilinear = setval;
04520 #else
04521         if (isget) return (void*) 0;
04522 #endif
04523 /*
04524     } else if (target == "draw.callback") {
04525         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.draw.callback;
04526         else sdl.draw.callback = *static_cast<GFX_CallBack_t*>(setval);
04527     } else if (target == "desktop.full.width") {
04528         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.full.width;
04529         else sdl.desktop.full.width = *static_cast<Bit16u*>(setval);
04530     } else if (target == "desktop.full.height") {
04531         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.full.height;
04532         else sdl.desktop.full.height = *static_cast<Bit16u*>(setval);
04533     } else if (target == "desktop.full.fixed") {
04534         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.full.fixed;
04535         else sdl.desktop.full.fixed = setval;
04536     } else if (target == "desktop.window.width") {
04537         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.window.width;
04538         else sdl.desktop.window.width = *static_cast<Bit16u*>(setval);
04539     } else if (target == "desktop.window.height") {
04540         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.window.height;
04541         else sdl.desktop.window.height = *static_cast<Bit16u*>(setval);
04542 */
04543     } else if (target == "desktop.fullscreen") {
04544         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.fullscreen;
04545         else sdl.desktop.fullscreen = setval;
04546     } else if (target == "desktop.doublebuf") {
04547         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.doublebuf;
04548         else sdl.desktop.doublebuf = setval;
04549 /*
04550     } else if (target == "desktop.type") {
04551         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.type;
04552         else sdl.desktop.type = *static_cast<SCREEN_TYPES*>(setval);
04553 */
04554     } else if (target == "desktop.want_type") {
04555         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.desktop.want_type;
04556         else sdl.desktop.want_type = *static_cast<SCREEN_TYPES*>(setval);
04557 /*
04558     } else if (target == "surface") {
04559         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.surface;
04560         else sdl.surface = static_cast<SDL_Surface*>(setval);
04561     } else if (target == "overlay") {
04562         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.overlay;
04563         else sdl.overlay = static_cast<SDL_Overlay*>(setval);
04564 */
04565     } else if (target == "mouse.autoenable") {
04566         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.mouse.autoenable;
04567         else sdl.mouse.autoenable = setval;
04568 /*
04569     } else if (target == "overscan_width") {
04570         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.overscan_width;
04571         else sdl.overscan_width = *static_cast<Bitu*>(setval);
04572 */
04573 #if defined (WIN32)
04574     } else if (target == "using_windib") {
04575         if (isget) return (void*) sdl.using_windib;
04576         else sdl.using_windib = setval;
04577 #endif
04578     }
04579 
04580     return NULL;
04581 }
04582 
04583 #if defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(IGNORE_TOUCHSCREEN)
04584 static void FingerToFakeMouseMotion(SDL_TouchFingerEvent * finger) {
04585     SDL_MouseMotionEvent fake;
04586 
04587     memset(&fake,0,sizeof(fake));
04588     /* NTS: Windows versions of SDL2 do normalize the coordinates */
04589     fake.x = (Sint32)(finger->x * currentWindowWidth);
04590     fake.y = (Sint32)(finger->y * currentWindowHeight);
04591     fake.xrel = (Sint32)finger->dx;
04592     fake.yrel = (Sint32)finger->dy;
04593     HandleMouseMotion(&fake);
04594 
04595     if (finger->type == SDL_FINGERDOWN || finger->type == SDL_FINGERUP) {
04596         SDL_MouseButtonEvent fakeb;
04597 
04598         memset(&fakeb,0,sizeof(fakeb));
04599 
04600         fakeb.state = (finger->type == SDL_FINGERDOWN) ? SDL_PRESSED : SDL_RELEASED;
04601         fakeb.button = SDL_BUTTON_LEFT;
04602         fakeb.x = fake.x;
04603         fakeb.y = fake.y;
04604         HandleMouseButton(&fakeb);
04605     }
04606 }
04607 
04608 static void HandleTouchscreenFinger(SDL_TouchFingerEvent * finger) {
04609     /* Now that SDL2 can tell my mouse from my laptop touchscreen, let's
04610      * map tap events to the left mouse button. Now I can use my laptop
04611      * touchscreen with Windows 3.11 again! --J.C. */
04612     /* Now let's handle The Finger (har har) */
04613 
04614     /* NTS: This code is written to map ONLY one finger to the mouse.
04615      *      If multiple fingers are touching the screen, this code will
04616      *      only respond to the first finger that touched the screen. */
04617 
04618     if (finger->type == SDL_FINGERDOWN) {
04619         if (touchscreen_finger_lock == no_finger_id &&
04620             touchscreen_touch_lock == no_touch_id) {
04621             touchscreen_finger_lock = finger->fingerId;
04622             touchscreen_touch_lock = finger->touchId;
04623             FingerToFakeMouseMotion(finger);
04624         }
04625     }
04626     else if (finger->type == SDL_FINGERUP) {
04627         if (touchscreen_finger_lock == finger->fingerId &&
04628             touchscreen_touch_lock == finger->touchId) {
04629             touchscreen_finger_lock = no_finger_id;
04630             touchscreen_touch_lock = no_touch_id;
04631             FingerToFakeMouseMotion(finger);
04632         }
04633     }
04634     else if (finger->type == SDL_FINGERMOTION) {
04635         if (touchscreen_finger_lock == finger->fingerId &&
04636             touchscreen_touch_lock == finger->touchId) {
04637             FingerToFakeMouseMotion(finger);
04638         }
04639     }
04640 }
04641 #endif
04642 
04643 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS)
04644 void MSG_WM_COMMAND_handle(SDL_SysWMmsg &Message);
04645 #endif
04646 
04647 struct mouse_pos
04648 {
04649     long x = 0;
04650     long y = 0;
04651 } mouse_pos;
04652 
04653 bool mouse_inside = false;
04654 
04655 void GFX_EventsMouseProcess(const long x, const long y, const long rx, const long ry)
04656 {
04657     const auto x1 = sdl.clip.x;
04658     const auto x2 = x1 + sdl.clip.w - 1;
04659     const auto y1 = sdl.clip.y;
04660     const auto y2 = y1 + sdl.clip.h - 1;
04661     const auto in = x >= x1 && x <= x2 && y >= y1 && y <= y2;
04662 
04663     if (mouse_inside && !in)
04664     {
04665         const auto x3 = max((int)x1, min((int)x2, (int)x));
04666         const auto y3 = max((int)y1, min((int)y2, (int)y));
04667         SDL_Event  evt;
04668         evt.type         = SDL_MOUSEMOTION;
04669         evt.motion.state = 0;
04670         evt.motion.which = 0;
04671         evt.motion.x     = x3;
04672         evt.motion.y     = y3;
04673         evt.motion.xrel  = (Sint16)((rx >= 0) ? min(rx, 32767l) : max(rx, -32768l));
04674         evt.motion.yrel  = (Sint16)((ry >= 0) ? min(ry, 32767l) : max(ry, -32768l));
04675         SDL_PushEvent(&evt);
04676     }
04677 
04678     mouse_inside = in;
04679 }
04680 
04681 #if defined(WIN32)
04682 void GFX_EventsMouseWin32()
04683 {
04684     /* Compute relative mouse movement */
04685 
04686     POINT point;
04687 
04688     if (!GetCursorPos(&point))
04689         return;
04690 
04691     const auto hwnd = GetSurfaceHWND();
04692 
04693     if (hwnd == nullptr || !ScreenToClient(hwnd, &point))
04694         return;
04695 
04696     const auto x  = point.x;
04697     const auto y  = point.y;
04698     const auto rx = x - mouse_pos.x;
04699     const auto ry = y - mouse_pos.y;
04700 
04701     mouse_pos.x = x;
04702     mouse_pos.y = y;
04703 
04704     /* Let the method do the heavy uplifting */
04705     GFX_EventsMouseProcess(x, y, rx, ry);
04706 }
04707 #endif
04708 
04715 void GFX_EventsMouse()
04716 {
04717     if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen || sdl.mouse.locked)
04718         return;
04719 
04720 #if WIN32
04721     GFX_EventsMouseWin32();
04722 #else
04723     // TODO
04724 #endif
04725 }
04726 
04727 /* DOSBox SVN revision 4176:4177: For Linux/X11, Xorg 1.20.1
04728  * will make spurious focus gain and loss events when locking the mouse in windowed mode.
04729  *
04730  * This has not been tested with DOSBox-X yet becaus I do not run Xorg 1.20.1, yet */
04731 #if defined(LINUX)
04732 #define SDL_XORG_FIX 1
04733 #else
04734 #define SDL_XORG_FIX 0
04735 #endif
04736 /* end patch fragment */
04737 
04738 bool gfx_in_mapper = false;
04739 
04740 #if defined(MACOSX)
04741 #define DB_POLLSKIP 3
04742 #else
04743 //Not used yet, see comment below
04744 #define DB_POLLSKIP 1
04745 #endif
04746 
04747 void GFX_Events() {
04748     CheckMapperKeyboardLayout();
04749 #if defined(C_SDL2) /* SDL 2.x---------------------------------- */
04750     //Don't poll too often. This can be heavy on the OS, especially Macs.
04751     //In idle mode 3000-4000 polls are done per second without this check.
04752     //Macs, with this code,  max 250 polls per second. (non-macs unused default max 500)
04753     //Currently not implemented for all platforms, given the ALT-TAB stuff for WIN32.
04754 #if defined (MACOSX)
04755     static int last_check = 0;
04756     int current_check = GetTicks();
04757     if (current_check - last_check <=  DB_POLLSKIP) return;
04758     last_check = current_check;
04759 #endif
04760 
04761     SDL_Event event;
04762 #if defined (REDUCE_JOYSTICK_POLLING)
04763     static int poll_delay = 0;
04764     int time = GetTicks();
04765     if (time - poll_delay > 20) {
04766         poll_delay = time;
04767         if (sdl.num_joysticks > 0)
04768         {
04769             SDL_JoystickUpdate();
04770             MAPPER_UpdateJoysticks();
04771         }
04772     }
04773 #endif
04774 
04775     GFX_EventsMouse();
04776 
04777 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
04778     emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
04779 #endif
04780 
04781     while (SDL_PollEvent(&event)) {
04782         switch (event.type) {
04783         case SDL_WINDOWEVENT:
04784             switch (event.window.event) {
04785             case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_RESTORED:
04786                 GFX_ResetScreen();
04787                 continue;
04788             case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_RESIZED:
04789                 GFX_HandleVideoResize(event.window.data1, event.window.data2);
04790                 continue;
04791             case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_EXPOSED:
04792                 if (sdl.draw.callback) sdl.draw.callback( GFX_CallBackRedraw );
04793                 continue;
04794             case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_LEAVE:
04795 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW
04796                 void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
04797                 void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
04798 
04799                 GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04800                 GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04801 
04802                 GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
04803 #endif
04804                 break;
04805             case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_FOCUS_GAINED:
04806                 if (IsFullscreen() && !sdl.mouse.locked)
04807                     GFX_CaptureMouse();
04808                 SetPriority(sdl.priority.focus);
04809                 CPU_Disable_SkipAutoAdjust();
04810                 break;
04811             case SDL_WINDOWEVENT_FOCUS_LOST:
04812                 if (sdl.mouse.locked) {
04813                     CaptureMouseNotify();
04814                     GFX_CaptureMouse();
04815                 }
04816 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW
04817                 void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
04818                 void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
04819 
04820                 GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04821                 GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
04822 
04823                 GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
04824 #endif
04825                 SetPriority(sdl.priority.nofocus);
04826                 GFX_LosingFocus();
04827                 CPU_Enable_SkipAutoAdjust();
04828                 break;
04829             default:
04830                 ;
04831             }
04832 
04833             /* Non-focus priority is set to pause; check to see if we've lost window or input focus
04834              * i.e. has the window been minimised or made inactive?
04835              */
04836             if (sdl.priority.nofocus == PRIORITY_LEVEL_PAUSE) {
04837                 if ((event.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_FOCUS_LOST) || (event.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_MINIMIZED)) {
04838                     /* Window has lost focus, pause the emulator.
04839                      * This is similar to what PauseDOSBox() does, but the exit criteria is different.
04840                      * Instead of waiting for the user to hit Alt-Break, we wait for the window to
04841                      * regain window or input focus.
04842                      */
04843                     bool paused = true;
04844                     SDL_Event ev;
04845 
04846                     GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,true);
04847                     KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
04848 //                  SDL_Delay(500);
04849 //                  while (SDL_PollEvent(&ev)) {
04850                     // flush event queue.
04851 //                  }
04852 
04853                     while (paused) {
04854 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
04855                         emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
04856                         SDL_PollEvent(&ev);
04857 #else
04858                         // WaitEvent waits for an event rather than polling, so CPU usage drops to zero
04859                         SDL_WaitEvent(&ev);
04860 #endif
04861 
04862                         switch (ev.type) {
04863                         case SDL_QUIT:
04864                             throw(0);
04865                             break; // a bit redundant at linux at least as the active events gets before the quit event.
04866                         case SDL_WINDOWEVENT:     // wait until we get window focus back
04867                             if ((ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_FOCUS_LOST) || (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_MINIMIZED) || (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_FOCUS_GAINED) || (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_RESTORED) || (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_EXPOSED)) {
04868                                 // We've got focus back, so unpause and break out of the loop
04869                                 if ((ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_FOCUS_GAINED) || (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_RESTORED) || (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_EXPOSED)) {
04870                                     paused = false;
04871                                     GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,false);
04872                                 }
04873 
04874                                 /* Now poke a "release ALT" command into the keyboard buffer
04875                                  * we have to do this, otherwise ALT will 'stick' and cause
04876                                  * problems with the app running in the DOSBox.
04877                                  */
04878                                 KEYBOARD_AddKey(KBD_leftalt, false);
04879                                 KEYBOARD_AddKey(KBD_rightalt, false);
04880                                 if (ev.window.event == SDL_WINDOWEVENT_RESTORED) {
04881                                     // We may need to re-create a texture and more
04882                                     GFX_ResetScreen();
04883                                 }
04884                             }
04885                             break;
04886                         }
04887                     }
04888                 }
04889             }
04890             break;
04891         case SDL_MOUSEMOTION:
04892 #if defined(C_SDL2)
04893             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == no_finger_id &&
04894                 touchscreen_touch_lock == no_touch_id &&
04895                 event.motion.which != SDL_TOUCH_MOUSEID) { /* don't handle mouse events faked by touchscreen */
04896                 HandleMouseMotion(&event.motion);
04897             }
04898 #else
04899             HandleMouseMotion(&event.motion);
04900 #endif
04901             break;
04902         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN:
04903         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONUP:
04904 #if defined(C_SDL2)
04905             if (touchscreen_finger_lock == no_finger_id &&
04906                 touchscreen_touch_lock == no_touch_id &&
04907                 event.button.which != SDL_TOUCH_MOUSEID) { /* don't handle mouse events faked by touchscreen */
04908                 HandleMouseButton(&event.button);
04909             }
04910 #else
04911             HandleMouseButton(&event.button);
04912 #endif
04913             break;
04914 #if !defined(IGNORE_TOUCHSCREEN)
04915         case SDL_FINGERDOWN:
04916         case SDL_FINGERUP:
04917         case SDL_FINGERMOTION:
04918             HandleTouchscreenFinger(&event.tfinger);
04919             break;
04920 #endif
04921         case SDL_QUIT:
04922             throw(0);
04923             break;
04924 #if defined (MACOSX)
04925         case SDL_KEYDOWN:
04926         case SDL_KEYUP:
04927             /* On macs CMD-Q is the default key to close an application */
04928             if (event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_q &&
04929                     (event.key.keysym.mod == KMOD_RGUI ||
04930                      event.key.keysym.mod == KMOD_LGUI)
04931                ) {
04932                 KillSwitch(true);
04933                 break;
04934             }
04935 #endif
04936         default:
04937             gfx_in_mapper = true;
04938             void MAPPER_CheckEvent(SDL_Event * event);
04939             MAPPER_CheckEvent(&event);
04940             gfx_in_mapper = false;
04941         }
04942     }
04943 #else /* SDL 1.x---------------------------------- */
04944     SDL_Event event;
04945 #if defined (REDUCE_JOYSTICK_POLLING)
04946     static uint32_t poll_delay=0;
04947     uint32_t time=GetTicks();
04948     if ((int32_t)(time-poll_delay)>20) {
04949         poll_delay=time;
04950         if (sdl.num_joysticks>0)
04951         {
04952             SDL_JoystickUpdate();
04953             MAPPER_UpdateJoysticks();
04954         }
04955     }
04956 #endif
04957 
04958     GFX_EventsMouse();
04959 
04960 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
04961     emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
04962 #endif
04963 
04964     while (SDL_PollEvent(&event)) {
04965         /* DOSBox SVN revision 4176:4177: For Linux/X11, Xorg 1.20.1
04966          * will make spurious focus gain and loss events when locking the mouse in windowed mode.
04967          *
04968          * This has not been tested with DOSBox-X yet becaus I do not run Xorg 1.20.1, yet */
04969 #if SDL_XORG_FIX
04970         // Special code for broken SDL with Xorg 1.20.1, where pairs of inputfocus gain and loss events are generated
04971         // when locking the mouse in windowed mode.
04972         if (event.type == SDL_ACTIVEEVENT && event.active.state == SDL_APPINPUTFOCUS && event.active.gain == 0) {
04973             SDL_Event test; //Check if the next event would undo this one.
04974             if (SDL_PeepEvents(&test,1,SDL_PEEKEVENT,SDL_ACTIVEEVENTMASK) == 1 && test.active.state == SDL_APPINPUTFOCUS && test.active.gain == 1) {
04975                 // Skip both events.
04976                 SDL_PeepEvents(&test,1,SDL_GETEVENT,SDL_ACTIVEEVENTMASK);
04977                 continue;
04978             }
04979         }
04980 #endif
04981         /* end patch fragment */
04982 
04983         switch (event.type) {
04984 #ifdef __WIN32__
04985         case SDL_SYSWMEVENT : {
04986             switch( event.syswm.msg->msg ) {
04987 #if !defined(HX_DOS)
04988                 case WM_COMMAND:
04989                     MSG_WM_COMMAND_handle(/*&*/(*event.syswm.msg));
04990                     break;
04991 #endif
04992                 case WM_SYSCOMMAND:
04993                     switch (event.syswm.msg->wParam) {
04994                         case 0xF032: // FIXME: What is this?
04995                         case SC_MAXIMIZE:
04996                             userResizeWindowWidth = 0;
04997                             userResizeWindowHeight = 0;
04998                             menu.maxwindow = true;
04999                             break;
05000                         case 0xF122: // FIXME: What is this?
05001                         case SC_RESTORE:
05002                             if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen)
05003                                 GFX_SwitchFullScreen();
05004                             menu.maxwindow = false;
05005                             UpdateWindowDimensions();
05006                             RENDER_Reset();
05007                             if (OpenGL_using()) {
05008                                 UpdateWindowDimensions();
05009                                 RENDER_Reset();
05010                             }
05011                             break;
05012                         case ID_WIN_SYSMENU_RESTOREMENU:
05013                             /* prevent removing the menu in 3Dfx mode */
05014                             if (!GFX_GetPreventFullscreen()) {
05015                                 DOSBox_SetMenu();
05016                                 mainMenu.get_item("mapper_togmenu").check(!menu.toggle).refresh_item(mainMenu);
05017                             }
05018                             break;
05019                         case ID_WIN_SYSMENU_TOGGLEMENU:
05020                             /* prevent removing the menu in 3Dfx mode */
05021                             if (!GFX_GetPreventFullscreen())
05022                             {
05023                                 if (menu.toggle) DOSBox_NoMenu(); else DOSBox_SetMenu();
05024                                 mainMenu.get_item("mapper_togmenu").check(!menu.toggle).refresh_item(mainMenu);
05025                             }
05026                             break;
05027 #if !defined(HX_DOS)
05028                         case ID_WIN_SYSMENU_MAPPER:
05029                             extern void MAPPER_Run(bool pressed);
05030                             MAPPER_Run(false);
05031                             break;
05032                         case ID_WIN_SYSMENU_CFG_GUI:
05033                             extern void GUI_Run(bool pressed);
05034                             GUI_Run(false);
05035                             break;
05036                         case ID_WIN_SYSMENU_PAUSE:
05037                             extern void PauseDOSBox(bool pressed);
05038                             PauseDOSBox(true);
05039                             break;
05040 #endif
05041                     }
05042                 default:
05043                     break;
05044             }
05045         }
05046 #endif
05047         case SDL_ACTIVEEVENT:
05048                 if (event.active.state & (SDL_APPINPUTFOCUS | SDL_APPACTIVE)) {
05049                     if (event.active.gain) {
05050 #ifdef WIN32
05051                         if (!sdl.desktop.fullscreen) sdl.focus_ticks = GetTicks();
05052 #endif
05053                         if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen && !sdl.mouse.locked)
05054                             GFX_CaptureMouse();
05055                         SetPriority(sdl.priority.focus);
05056                         CPU_Disable_SkipAutoAdjust();
05057                         BIOS_SynchronizeNumLock();
05058                         BIOS_SynchronizeCapsLock();
05059                         BIOS_SynchronizeScrollLock();
05060                     } else {
05061                         if (sdl.mouse.locked)
05062                         {
05063                             CaptureMouseNotify();
05064                             GFX_CaptureMouse();
05065                         }
05066 
05067 #if defined(WIN32)
05068                         if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen)
05069                             GFX_ForceFullscreenExit();
05070 #endif
05071 
05072 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW
05073                         void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
05074                         void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
05075 
05076                         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
05077                         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
05078 #endif
05079 
05080                         SetPriority(sdl.priority.nofocus);
05081                         GFX_LosingFocus();
05082                         CPU_Enable_SkipAutoAdjust();
05083                     }
05084                 }
05085 
05086 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW
05087                 if (event.active.state & SDL_APPMOUSEFOCUS) {
05088                     if (!(event.active.gain & SDL_APPMOUSEFOCUS)) {
05089                         /* losing focus or moving the mouse outside the window should un-hilight the currently selected menu item */
05090                         void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
05091                         void GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(DOSBoxMenu &menu,DOSBoxMenu::item_handle_t item_id);
05092 
05093                         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHover(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
05094                         GFX_SDLMenuTrackHilight(mainMenu,DOSBoxMenu::unassigned_item_handle);
05095 
05096                     }
05097                 }
05098 
05099                 GFX_DrawSDLMenu(mainMenu,mainMenu.display_list);
05100 #endif
05101 
05102                 /* Non-focus priority is set to pause; check to see if we've lost window or input focus
05103                  * i.e. has the window been minimised or made inactive?
05104                  */
05105                 if (sdl.priority.nofocus == PRIORITY_LEVEL_PAUSE) {
05106                     if ((event.active.state & (SDL_APPINPUTFOCUS | SDL_APPACTIVE)) && (!event.active.gain)) {
05107                     /* Window has lost focus, pause the emulator.
05108                      * This is similar to what PauseDOSBox() does, but the exit criteria is different.
05109                      * Instead of waiting for the user to hit Alt-Break, we wait for the window to
05110                      * regain window or input focus.
05111                      */
05112                     bool paused = true;
05113                     SDL_Event ev;
05114 
05115                     GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,true);
05116                     KEYBOARD_ClrBuffer();
05117 //                  SDL_Delay(500);
05118 //                  while (SDL_PollEvent(&ev)) {
05119                         // flush event queue.
05120 //                  }
05121 
05122                     while (paused) {
05123 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
05124                         emscripten_sleep_with_yield(0);
05125                         SDL_PollEvent(&ev);
05126 #else
05127                         // WaitEvent waits for an event rather than polling, so CPU usage drops to zero
05128                         SDL_WaitEvent(&ev);
05129 #endif
05130 
05131                         switch (ev.type) {
05132                         case SDL_QUIT: throw(0); break; // a bit redundant at linux at least as the active events gets before the quit event.
05133                         case SDL_ACTIVEEVENT:     // wait until we get window focus back
05134                             if (ev.active.state & (SDL_APPINPUTFOCUS | SDL_APPACTIVE)) {
05135                                 // We've got focus back, so unpause and break out of the loop
05136                                 if (ev.active.gain) {
05137                                     paused = false;
05138                                     GFX_SetTitle(-1,-1,-1,false);
05139                                 }
05140 
05141                                 /* Now poke a "release ALT" command into the keyboard buffer
05142                                  * we have to do this, otherwise ALT will 'stick' and cause
05143                                  * problems with the app running in the DOSBox.
05144                                  */
05145                                 KEYBOARD_AddKey(KBD_leftalt, false);
05146                                 KEYBOARD_AddKey(KBD_rightalt, false);
05147                             }
05148                             break;
05149                         }
05150                     }
05151                 }
05152             }
05153             break;
05154         case SDL_MOUSEMOTION:
05155             HandleMouseMotion(&event.motion);
05156             break;
05157         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONDOWN:
05158         case SDL_MOUSEBUTTONUP:
05159             HandleMouseButton(&event.button);
05160             break;
05161         case SDL_VIDEORESIZE:
05162             UpdateWindowDimensions(); // FIXME: Use SDL window dimensions, except that on Windows, SDL won't tell us our actual dimensions
05163             HandleVideoResize(&event.resize);
05164             break;
05165         case SDL_QUIT:
05166             throw(0);
05167             break;
05168         case SDL_VIDEOEXPOSE:
05169             if (sdl.draw.callback) sdl.draw.callback( GFX_CallBackRedraw );
05170             break;
05171 #ifdef WIN32
05172         case SDL_KEYDOWN:
05173         case SDL_KEYUP:
05174             // ignore event alt+tab
05175             if (event.key.keysym.sym==SDLK_LALT) sdl.laltstate = event.key.type;
05176             if (event.key.keysym.sym==SDLK_RALT) sdl.raltstate = event.key.type;
05177             if (((event.key.keysym.sym==SDLK_TAB)) &&
05178                 ((sdl.laltstate==SDL_KEYDOWN) || (sdl.raltstate==SDL_KEYDOWN))) { MAPPER_LosingFocus(); break; }
05179             // This can happen as well.
05180             if (((event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_TAB )) && (event.key.keysym.mod & KMOD_ALT)) break;
05181             // ignore tab events that arrive just after regaining focus. (likely the result of alt-tab)
05182             if ((event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_TAB) && (GetTicks() - sdl.focus_ticks < 2)) break;
05183 #endif
05184 #if defined (MACOSX)            
05185         case SDL_KEYDOWN:
05186         case SDL_KEYUP:
05187             /* On macs CMD-Q is the default key to close an application */
05188             if (event.key.keysym.sym == SDLK_q && (event.key.keysym.mod == KMOD_RMETA || event.key.keysym.mod == KMOD_LMETA) ) {
05189                 KillSwitch(true);
05190                 break;
05191             } 
05192 #endif
05193         default:
05194             void MAPPER_CheckEvent(SDL_Event * event);
05195             MAPPER_CheckEvent(&event);
05196         }
05197     }
05198     // start emendelson from dbDOS
05199     // Disabled multiple characters per dispatch b/c occasionally
05200     // keystrokes get lost in the spew. (Prob b/c of DI usage on Win32, sadly..)
05201     // while (PasteClipboardNext());
05202     // Doesn't really matter though, it's fast enough as it is...
05203     static Bitu iPasteTicker = 0;
05204     if ((iPasteTicker++ % 20) == 0) // emendelson: was %2, %20 is good for WP51
05205         PasteClipboardNext();   // end added emendelson from dbDOS
05206 #endif
05207 }

05345 
05346 static std::string strPasteBuffer;
05347 // Just in case, to keep us from entering an unexpected KB state
05348 const  size_t      kPasteMinBufExtra = 4;
05350 static void GenKBStroke(const UINT uiScanCode, const bool bDepressed, const SDLMod keymods)
05351 {
05352     const SDLKey sdlkey = aryScanCodeToSDLKey[uiScanCode];
05353     if (sdlkey == SDLK_UNKNOWN)
05354         return;
05355 
05356     SDL_Event evntKeyStroke = { 0 };
05357     evntKeyStroke.type = bDepressed ? SDL_KEYDOWN : SDL_KEYUP;
05358     evntKeyStroke.key.keysym.scancode = (unsigned char)LOBYTE(uiScanCode);
05359     evntKeyStroke.key.keysym.sym = sdlkey;
05360     evntKeyStroke.key.keysym.mod = keymods;
05361     evntKeyStroke.key.keysym.unicode = 0;
05362     evntKeyStroke.key.state = bDepressed ? SDL_PRESSED : SDL_RELEASED;
05363     SDL_PushEvent(&evntKeyStroke);
05364 }
05365 
05366 static bool PasteClipboardNext()
05367 {
05368     if (strPasteBuffer.length() == 0)
05369         return false;
05370 
05371     if (!bScanCodeMapInited)
05372         PasteInitMapSCToSDLKey();
05373 
05374     const char cKey = strPasteBuffer[0];
05375     SHORT shVirKey = VkKeyScan(cKey); // If it fails then MapVirtK will also fail, so no bail yet
05376     UINT uiScanCode = MapVirtualKey(LOBYTE(shVirKey), MAPVK_VK_TO_VSC);
05377     if (uiScanCode)
05378     {
05379         const bool   bModShift = ((shVirKey & 0x0100) != 0);
05380         const bool   bModCntrl = ((shVirKey & 0x0200) != 0);
05381         const bool   bModAlt = ((shVirKey & 0x0400) != 0);
05382         const SDLMod sdlmModsOn = SDL_GetModState();
05383         const bool   bModShiftOn = ((sdlmModsOn & (KMOD_LSHIFT | KMOD_RSHIFT)) > 0);
05384         const bool   bModCntrlOn = ((sdlmModsOn & (KMOD_LCTRL | KMOD_RCTRL)) > 0);
05385         const bool   bModAltOn = ((sdlmModsOn & (KMOD_LALT | KMOD_RALT)) > 0);
05386         const UINT   uiScanCodeShift = MapVirtualKey(VK_SHIFT, MAPVK_VK_TO_VSC);
05387         const UINT   uiScanCodeCntrl = MapVirtualKey(VK_CONTROL, MAPVK_VK_TO_VSC);
05388         const UINT   uiScanCodeAlt = MapVirtualKey(VK_MENU, MAPVK_VK_TO_VSC);
05389         const SDLMod sdlmMods = (SDLMod)((sdlmModsOn & ~(KMOD_LSHIFT | KMOD_RSHIFT |
05390             KMOD_LCTRL | KMOD_RCTRL |
05391             KMOD_LALT | KMOD_RALT)) |
05392             (bModShiftOn ? KMOD_LSHIFT : 0) |
05393             (bModCntrlOn ? KMOD_LCTRL : 0) |
05394             (bModAltOn ? KMOD_LALT : 0));
05395 
05398         // Could be made more efficient, but would require tracking of more state,
05399         // so let's forgot that for now...
05400         size_t sStrokesRequired = 2; // At least the key & up/down
05401         if (bModShift != bModShiftOn) sStrokesRequired += 2; // To press/release Shift
05402         if (bModCntrl != bModCntrlOn) sStrokesRequired += 2; // To press/release Control
05403         if (bModAlt != bModAltOn) sStrokesRequired += 2; // To press/release Alt
05408         if (KEYBOARD_BufferSpaceAvail() < (sStrokesRequired + kPasteMinBufExtra))
05409             return false;
05410 
05411         if (bModShift != bModShiftOn) GenKBStroke(uiScanCodeShift, !bModShiftOn, sdlmMods);
05412         if (bModCntrl != bModCntrlOn) GenKBStroke(uiScanCodeCntrl, !bModCntrlOn, sdlmMods);
05413         if (bModAlt != bModAltOn) GenKBStroke(uiScanCodeAlt, !bModAltOn, sdlmMods);
05414         GenKBStroke(uiScanCode, true, sdlmMods);
05415         GenKBStroke(uiScanCode, false, sdlmMods);
05416         if (bModShift != bModShiftOn) GenKBStroke(uiScanCodeShift, bModShiftOn, sdlmMods);
05417         if (bModCntrl != bModCntrlOn) GenKBStroke(uiScanCodeCntrl, bModCntrlOn, sdlmMods);
05418         if (bModAlt != bModAltOn) GenKBStroke(uiScanCodeAlt, bModAltOn, sdlmMods);
05419         //putchar(cKey); // For debugging dropped strokes
05420     }
05421 
05422     // Pop head. Could be made more efficient, but this is neater.
05423     strPasteBuffer = strPasteBuffer.substr(1, strPasteBuffer.length()); // technically -1, but it clamps by itself anyways...
05424     return true;
05425 }
05426 
05427 void PasteClipboard(bool bPressed)
05428 {
05429     if (!bPressed) return;
05430     SDL_SysWMinfo wmiInfo;
05431     SDL_VERSION(&wmiInfo.version);
05432 
05433     if (SDL_GetWMInfo(&wmiInfo) != 1) return;
05434     if (!::OpenClipboard(wmiInfo.window)) return;
05435     if (!::IsClipboardFormatAvailable(CF_TEXT)) return;
05436 
05437     HANDLE hContents = ::GetClipboardData(CF_TEXT);
05438     if (!hContents) return;
05439 
05440     const char* szClipboard = (const char*)::GlobalLock(hContents);
05441     if (szClipboard)
05442     {
05443         // Create a copy of the string, and filter out Linefeed characters (ASCII '10')
05444         size_t sClipboardLen = strlen(szClipboard);
05445         char* szFilteredText = reinterpret_cast<char*>(alloca(sClipboardLen + 1));
05446         char* szFilterNextChar = szFilteredText;
05447         for (size_t i = 0; i < sClipboardLen; ++i)
05448             if (szClipboard[i] != 0x0A) // Skip linefeeds
05449             {
05450                 *szFilterNextChar = szClipboard[i];
05451                 ++szFilterNextChar;
05452             }
05453         *szFilterNextChar = '\0'; // Cap it.
05454 
05455         strPasteBuffer.append(szFilteredText);
05456         ::GlobalUnlock(hContents);
05457     }
05458 
05459     ::CloseClipboard();
05460 }
05462 #else // end emendelson from dbDOS
05463 void PasteClipboard(bool bPressed) {
05464     (void)bPressed;//UNUSED
05465     // stub
05466 }

05469 bool PasteClipboardNext() {
05470     // stub
05471     return false;
05472 }

05477 #if defined (WIN32)
05478 static BOOL WINAPI ConsoleEventHandler(DWORD event) {
05479     switch (event) {
05480     case CTRL_SHUTDOWN_EVENT:
05481     case CTRL_LOGOFF_EVENT:
05482     case CTRL_CLOSE_EVENT:
05483     case CTRL_BREAK_EVENT:
05484         raise(SIGTERM);
05485         return TRUE;
05486     case CTRL_C_EVENT:
05487     default: //pass to the next handler
05488         return FALSE;
05489     }
05490 }
05491 #endif

05493 void Null_Init(Section *sec);
05494 
05495 void SDL_OnSectionPropChange(Section *x) {
05496     (void)x;//UNUSED
05497     Section_prop * section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("sdl"));
05498 
05499     {
05500         bool cfg_want_menu = section->Get_bool("showmenu");
05501 
05502         /* -- -- decide whether to set menu */
05503         if (menu_gui && !control->opt_nomenu && cfg_want_menu)
05504             DOSBox_SetMenu();
05505         else
05506             DOSBox_NoMenu();
05507     }
05508 }
