05510 void SDL_SetupConfigSection() {
05511     Section_prop * sdl_sec=control->AddSection_prop("sdl",&Null_Init);
05512 
05513     Prop_bool* Pbool;
05514     Prop_string* Pstring;
05515     Prop_int* Pint;
05516     Prop_multival* Pmulti;
05517 
05518     Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("fullscreen",Property::Changeable::Always,false);
05519     Pbool->Set_help("Start dosbox directly in fullscreen. (Press ALT-Enter to go back)");
05520      
05521     Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("fulldouble",Property::Changeable::Always,false);
05522     Pbool->Set_help("Use double buffering in fullscreen. It can reduce screen flickering, but it can also result in a slow DOSBox.");
05523 
05524     //Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("sdlresize",Property::Changeable::Always,false);
05525     //Pbool->Set_help("Makes window resizable (depends on scalers)");
05526 
05527     Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("fullresolution",Property::Changeable::Always,"desktop");
05528     Pstring->Set_help("What resolution to use for fullscreen: original, desktop or a fixed size (e.g. 1024x768).\n"
05529                       "  Using your monitor's native resolution with aspect=true might give the best results.\n"
05530               "  If you end up with small window on a large screen, try an output different from surface.");
05531 
05532     Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("windowresolution",Property::Changeable::Always,"original");
05533     Pstring->Set_help("Scale the window to this size IF the output device supports hardware scaling.\n"
05534                       "  (output=surface does not!)");
05535 
05536     const char* outputs[] = {
05537         "surface", "overlay",
05538 #if C_OPENGL
05539         "opengl", "openglnb", "openglhq",
05540 #endif
05541         "ddraw",
05542 #if C_DIRECT3D
05543         "direct3d",
05544 #endif
05545         0 };
05546 #ifdef __WIN32__
05547 # if defined(HX_DOS)
05548         Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("output", Property::Changeable::Always, "surface"); /* HX DOS should stick to surface */
05549 # elif defined(__MINGW32__) && !(C_DIRECT3D) && !defined(C_SDL2)
05550         /* NTS: OpenGL output never seems to work in VirtualBox under Windows XP */
05551         Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("output", Property::Changeable::Always, isVirtualBox ? "surface" : "opengl"); /* MinGW builds do not yet have Direct3D */
05552 # else
05553         Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("output", Property::Changeable::Always, "direct3d");
05554 # endif
05555 #elif defined(MACOSX) && defined(C_OPENGL) && !defined(C_SDL2)
05556         /* NTS: Lately, especially on Macbooks with Retina displays, OpenGL gives better performance
05557                 than the CG bitmap-based "surface" output.
05558 
05559                 On my dev system, "top" shows a 20% CPU load doing 1:1 CG Bitmap output to the screen
05560                 on a High DPI setup, while ignoring High DPI and rendering through Cocoa at 2x size
05561                 pegs the CPU core DOSBox-X is running on at 100% and emulation stutters.
05562 
05563                 So for the best experience, default to OpenGL.
05564 
05565                 Note that "surface" yields good performance with SDL2 and OS X because SDL2 doesn't
05566                 use the CGBitmap system, it uses OpenGL or Metal underneath automatically. */
05567         Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("output", Property::Changeable::Always, "opengl");
05568 #else
05569         Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("output", Property::Changeable::Always, "surface");
05570 #endif
05571     Pstring->Set_help("What video system to use for output.");
05572     Pstring->Set_values(outputs);
05573 
05574     Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("autolock",Property::Changeable::Always, false);
05575     Pbool->Set_help("Mouse will automatically lock, if you click on the screen. (Press CTRL-F10 to unlock)");
05576 
05577     const char* feeds[] = { "none", "beep", "flash", nullptr};
05578     Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("autolock_feedback", Property::Changeable::Always, feeds[1]);
05579     Pstring->Set_help("Autolock status feedback type, i.e. visual, auditive, none.");
05580     Pstring->Set_values(feeds);
05581 
05582     Pmulti = sdl_sec->Add_multi("sensitivity",Property::Changeable::Always, ",");
05583     Pmulti->Set_help("Mouse sensitivity. The optional second parameter specifies vertical sensitivity (e.g. 100,-50).");
05584     Pmulti->SetValue("100");
05585     Pint = Pmulti->GetSection()->Add_int("xsens",Property::Changeable::Always,100);
05586     Pint->SetMinMax(-1000,1000);
05587     Pint = Pmulti->GetSection()->Add_int("ysens",Property::Changeable::Always,100);
05588     Pint->SetMinMax(-1000,1000);
05589 
05590     const char * emulation[] = {"integration", "locked", "always", "never", nullptr};
05591     Pstring  = sdl_sec->Add_string("mouse_emulation", Property::Changeable::Always, emulation[1]);
05592     Pstring->Set_help(
05593         "When is mouse emulated ?\n"
05594         "integration: when not locked\n"
05595         "locked:      when locked\n"
05596         "always:      every time\n"
05597         "never:       at no time\n"
05598         "If disabled, the mouse position in DOSBox-X is exactly where the host OS reports it.\n"
05599         "When using a high DPI mouse, the emulation of mouse movement can noticeably reduce the\n"
05600         "sensitiveness of your device, i.e. the mouse is slower but more precise.");
05601     Pstring->Set_values(emulation);
05602 
05603     Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("waitonerror",Property::Changeable::Always, true);
05604     Pbool->Set_help("Wait before closing the console if dosbox has an error.");
05605 
05606     Pmulti = sdl_sec->Add_multi("priority", Property::Changeable::Always, ",");
05607     Pmulti->SetValue("higher,normal",/*init*/true);
05608     Pmulti->Set_help("Priority levels for dosbox. Second entry behind the comma is for when dosbox is not focused/minimized.\n"
05609                      "  pause is only valid for the second entry.");
05610 
05611     const char* actt[] = { "lowest", "lower", "normal", "higher", "highest", "pause", 0};
05612     Pstring = Pmulti->GetSection()->Add_string("active",Property::Changeable::Always,"higher");
05613     Pstring->Set_values(actt);
05614 
05615     const char* inactt[] = { "lowest", "lower", "normal", "higher", "highest", "pause", 0};
05616     Pstring = Pmulti->GetSection()->Add_string("inactive",Property::Changeable::Always,"normal");
05617     Pstring->Set_values(inactt);
05618 
05619     Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_path("mapperfile",Property::Changeable::Always,MAPPERFILE);
05620     Pstring->Set_help("File used to load/save the key/event mappings from. Resetmapper only works with the default value.");
05621 
05622 #if C_DIRECT3D && C_D3DSHADERS
05623     Pmulti = sdl_sec->Add_multi("pixelshader",Property::Changeable::Always," ");
05624     Pmulti->SetValue("none",/*init*/true);
05625     Pmulti->Set_help("Pixelshader program (effect file must be in Shaders subdirectory). If 'forced' is appended,\n"
05626         "then the shader will be used even if the result might not be desired.");
05627 
05628     Pstring = Pmulti->GetSection()->Add_string("type",Property::Changeable::Always,"none");
05629     Pstring = Pmulti->GetSection()->Add_string("force",Property::Changeable::Always,"");
05630 #endif
05631 
05632     Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("usescancodes",Property::Changeable::Always,false);
05633     Pbool->Set_help("Avoid usage of symkeys, might not work on all operating systems.");
05634 
05635     Pint = sdl_sec->Add_int("overscan",Property::Changeable::Always, 0);
05636     Pint->SetMinMax(0,10);
05637     Pint->Set_help("Width of overscan border (0 to 10). (works only if output=surface)");
05638 
05639     Pstring = sdl_sec->Add_string("titlebar", Property::Changeable::Always, "");
05640     Pstring->Set_help("Change the string displayed in the DOSBox title bar.");
05641 
05642     Pbool = sdl_sec->Add_bool("showmenu", Property::Changeable::Always, true);
05643     Pbool->Set_help("Whether to show the menu bar (if supported). Default true.");
05644 
05645 //  Pint = sdl_sec->Add_int("overscancolor",Property::Changeable::Always, 0);
05646 //  Pint->SetMinMax(0,1000);
05647 //  Pint->Set_help("Value of overscan color.");
05648 }
05649 
05650 static void show_warning(char const * const message) {
05651     bool textonly = true;
05652 #ifdef WIN32
05653     textonly = false;
05654     if ( !sdl.inited && SDL_Init(SDL_INIT_VIDEO|SDL_INIT_NOPARACHUTE) < 0 ) textonly = true;
05655     sdl.inited = true;
05656 #endif
05657     LOG_MSG( "Warning: %s", message);
05658     if(textonly) return;
05659 #if defined(C_SDL2)
05660     if (!sdl.window)
05661         if (!GFX_SetSDLSurfaceWindow(640,400)) return;
05662     sdl.surface = SDL_GetWindowSurface(sdl.window);
05663 #else
05664     if(!sdl.surface) sdl.surface = SDL_SetVideoMode(640,400,0,SDL_RESIZABLE);
05665     sdl.deferred_resize = false;
05666     sdl.must_redraw_all = true;
05667 #endif
05668     if(!sdl.surface) return;
05669 #if SDL_BYTEORDER == SDL_BIG_ENDIAN
05670     Bit32u rmask = 0xff000000;
05671     Bit32u gmask = 0x00ff0000;
05672     Bit32u bmask = 0x0000ff00;
05673 #else
05674     Bit32u rmask = 0x000000ff;
05675     Bit32u gmask = 0x0000ff00;                    
05676     Bit32u bmask = 0x00ff0000;
05677 #endif
05678     SDL_Surface* splash_surf = SDL_CreateRGBSurface(SDL_SWSURFACE, 640, 400, 32, rmask, gmask, bmask, 0);
05679     if (!splash_surf) return;
05680 
05681     int x = 120,y = 20;
05682     std::string m(message),m2;
05683     std::string::size_type a,b,c,d;
05684    
05685     while(m.size()) { //Max 50 characters. break on space before or on a newline
05686         c = m.find('\n');
05687         d = m.rfind(' ',50);
05688         if(c>d) a=b=d; else a=b=c;
05689         if( a != std::string::npos) b++; 
05690         m2 = m.substr(0,a); m.erase(0,b);
05691         OutputString((unsigned int)x,(unsigned int)y,m2.c_str(),0xffffffffu,0,splash_surf);
05692         y += 20;
05693     }
05694    
05695     SDL_BlitSurface(splash_surf, NULL, sdl.surface, NULL);
05696 #if defined(C_SDL2)
05697     SDL_UpdateWindowSurface(sdl.window);
05698 #else
05699     SDL_Flip(sdl.surface);
05700 #endif
05701     SDL_Delay(12000);
05702 }

05704 static void launcheditor(std::string edit) {
05705     std::string path,file;
05706     Cross::CreatePlatformConfigDir(path);
05707     Cross::GetPlatformConfigName(file);
05708     path += file;
05709     FILE* f = fopen(path.c_str(),"r");
05710     if(!f && !control->PrintConfig(path.c_str())) {
05711         printf("tried creating %s. but failed.\n",path.c_str());
05712         exit(1);
05713     }
05714     if(f) fclose(f);
05715 
05716     execlp(edit.c_str(),edit.c_str(),path.c_str(),(char*) 0);
05717 
05718     //if you get here the launching failed!
05719     printf("can't find editor(s) specified at the command line.\n");
05720     exit(1);
05721 }
05722 #if C_DEBUG
05723 extern void DEBUG_ShutDown(Section * /*sec*/);
05724 #endif
05725 
05726 static void launchcaptures(std::string const& edit) {
05727     std::string path,file;
05728     struct stat cstat;
05729     Section* t = control->GetSection("dosbox");
05730     if(t) file = t->GetPropValue("captures");
05731     if(!t || file == NO_SUCH_PROPERTY) {
05732         printf("Config system messed up.\n");
05733         exit(1);
05734     }
05735     path = ".";
05736     path += CROSS_FILESPLIT;
05737     path += file;
05738 
05739     stat(path.c_str(),&cstat);
05740     if(cstat.st_mode & S_IFDIR) {
05741         execlp(edit.c_str(),edit.c_str(),path.c_str(),(char*) 0);
05742         //if you get here the launching failed!
05743         printf("can't find filemanager %s\n",edit.c_str());
05744         exit(1);
05745     } else {
05746         path = "";
05747         Cross::CreatePlatformConfigDir(path);
05748         path += file;
05749         Cross::CreateDir(path);
05750         stat(path.c_str(),&cstat);
05751         if((cstat.st_mode & S_IFDIR) == 0) {
05752             printf("%s doesn't exist or isn't a directory.\n",path.c_str());
05753             exit(1);
05754         }
05755         execlp(edit.c_str(),edit.c_str(),path.c_str(),(char*) 0);
05756         //if you get here the launching failed!
05757         printf("can't find filemanager %s\n",edit.c_str());
05758         exit(1);
05759     }
05760 }
05761

05792 static void printconfiglocation() {
05793     std::string path,file;
05794     Cross::CreatePlatformConfigDir(path);
05795     Cross::GetPlatformConfigName(file);
05796     path += file;
05797      
05798     FILE* f = fopen(path.c_str(),"r");
05799     if(!f && !control->PrintConfig(path.c_str())) {
05800         printf("tried creating %s. but failed",path.c_str());
05801         exit(1);
05802     }
05803     if(f) fclose(f);
05804     printf("%s\n",path.c_str());
05805     exit(0);
05806 }
05807 
05808 static void eraseconfigfile() {
05809     FILE* f = fopen("dosbox.conf","r");
05810     if(f) {
05811         fclose(f);
05812         show_warning("Warning: dosbox.conf exists in current working directory.\nThis will override the configuration file at runtime.\n");
05813     }
05814     std::string path,file;
05815     Cross::GetPlatformConfigDir(path);
05816     Cross::GetPlatformConfigName(file);
05817     path += file;
05818     f = fopen(path.c_str(),"r");
05819     if(!f) exit(0);
05820     fclose(f);
05821     unlink(path.c_str());
05822     exit(0);
05823 }
05824 
05825 static void erasemapperfile() {
05826     FILE* g = fopen("dosbox.conf","r");
05827     if(g) {
05828         fclose(g);
05829         show_warning("Warning: dosbox.conf exists in current working directory.\nKeymapping might not be properly reset.\n"
05830                      "Please reset configuration as well and delete the dosbox.conf.\n");
05831     }
05832 
05833     std::string path,file=MAPPERFILE;
05834     Cross::GetPlatformConfigDir(path);
05835     path += file;
05836     FILE* f = fopen(path.c_str(),"r");
05837     if(!f) exit(0);
05838     fclose(f);
05839     unlink(path.c_str());
05840     exit(0);
05841 }
05842 
05843 void SetNumLock(void) {
05844 #ifdef WIN32
05845     if (control->opt_disable_numlock_check)
05846         return;
05847 
05848     // Simulate a key press
05849     keybd_event(VK_NUMLOCK,0x45,KEYEVENTF_EXTENDEDKEY | 0,0);
05850 
05851     // Simulate a key release
05852     keybd_event(VK_NUMLOCK,0x45,KEYEVENTF_EXTENDEDKEY | KEYEVENTF_KEYUP,0);
05853 #endif
05854 }
05855 
05856 void CheckNumLockState(void) {
05857 #ifdef WIN32
05858     BYTE keyState[256];
05859 
05860     GetKeyboardState((LPBYTE)(&keyState));
05861     if (keyState[VK_NUMLOCK] & 1) {
05862         startup_state_numlock = true;
05863     }
05864 #endif
05865 }
05866 
05867 void CheckCapsLockState(void) {
05868 #ifdef WIN32
05869     BYTE keyState[256];
05870 
05871     GetKeyboardState((LPBYTE)(&keyState));
05872     if (keyState[VK_CAPITAL] & 1) {
05873         startup_state_capslock = true;
05874     }
05875 #endif
05876 }
05877 
05878 void CheckScrollLockState(void) {
05879 #ifdef WIN32
05880     BYTE keyState[256];
05881 
05882     GetKeyboardState((LPBYTE)(&keyState));
05883     if (keyState[VK_SCROLL] & 1) {
05884         startup_state_scrlock = true;
05885     }
05886 #endif
05887 }

05889 extern bool log_keyboard_scan_codes;
05890 
05891 bool showconsole_init = false;
05892 
05893 #if C_DEBUG
05894 bool DEBUG_IsDebuggerConsoleVisible(void);
05895 #endif
05896 
05897 void DOSBox_ShowConsole() {
05898 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
05899     CONSOLE_SCREEN_BUFFER_INFO csbi;
05900     COORD crd;
05901     HWND hwnd;
05902 
05903 #if C_DEBUG
05904     /* if the debugger has already taken the console, do nothing */
05905     if (DEBUG_IsDebuggerConsoleVisible())
05906         return;
05907 #endif
05908 
05909     /* if WE have already opened the console, do nothing */
05910     if (showconsole_init)
05911         return;
05912 
05913     /* Microsoft Windows: Allocate a console and begin spewing to it.
05914        DOSBox is compiled on Windows platforms as a Win32 application, and therefore, no console. */
05915     /* FIXME: What about "file handles" 0/1/2 emulated by C library, for use with _open/_close/_lseek/etc? */
05916     AllocConsole();
05917 
05918     GetConsoleScreenBufferInfo(GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE), &csbi);
05919     crd = csbi.dwSize;
05920     crd.X = 130;
05921     SetConsoleScreenBufferSize(GetStdHandle(STD_OUTPUT_HANDLE), crd);
05922 
05923     hwnd = GetConsoleWindow();
05924     ShowWindow(hwnd, SW_MAXIMIZE);
05925 
05926     freopen("CONIN$", "r", stdin);
05927     freopen("CONOUT$", "w", stdout);
05928     freopen("CONOUT$", "w", stderr);
05929 
05930     showconsole_init = true;
05931 #endif
05932 }
05933 
05934 void DOSBox_ConsolePauseWait() {
05935     char c;
05936 
05937     printf("Hit ENTER to continue\n");
05938     do {
05939         if (fread(&c, 1, 1, stdin) != 1) break;
05940     } while (!(c == 13 || c == 10)); /* wait for Enter key */
05941 }
05942 
05943 bool DOSBOX_parse_argv() {
05944     std::string optname,tmp;
05945 
05946     assert(control != NULL);
05947     assert(control->cmdline != NULL);
05948 
05949     control->cmdline->BeginOpt(true/*eat argv*/);
05950     while (control->cmdline->GetOpt(optname)) {
05951         std::transform(optname.begin(), optname.end(), optname.begin(), ::tolower);
05952 
05953         if (optname == "version") {
05954             DOSBox_ShowConsole();
05955 
05956             fprintf(stderr,"\nDOSBox version %s %s, copyright 2002-2019 DOSBox Team.\n\n",VERSION,SDL_STRING);
05957             fprintf(stderr,"DOSBox is written by the DOSBox Team (See AUTHORS file))\n");
05958             fprintf(stderr,"DOSBox comes with ABSOLUTELY NO WARRANTY.  This is free software,\n");
05959             fprintf(stderr,"and you are welcome to redistribute it under certain conditions;\n");
05960             fprintf(stderr,"please read the COPYING file thoroughly before doing so.\n\n");
05961 
05962 #if defined(WIN32)
05963             DOSBox_ConsolePauseWait();
05964 #endif
05965 
05966             return 0;
05967         }
05968         else if (optname == "h" || optname == "help") {
05969             DOSBox_ShowConsole();
05970 
05971             fprintf(stderr,"\ndosbox [options]\n");
05972             fprintf(stderr,"\nDOSBox version %s %s, copyright 2002-2019 DOSBox Team.\n\n",VERSION,SDL_STRING);
05973             fprintf(stderr,"  -h     -help                            Show this help\n");
05974             fprintf(stderr,"  -editconf                               Launch editor\n");
05975             fprintf(stderr,"  -opencaptures <param>                   Launch captures\n");
05976             fprintf(stderr,"  -opensaves <param>                      Launch saves\n");
05977             fprintf(stderr,"  -eraseconf                              Erase config file\n");
05978             fprintf(stderr,"  -resetconf                              Erase config file\n");
05979             fprintf(stderr,"  -printconf                              Print config file location\n");
05980             fprintf(stderr,"  -erasemapper                            Erase mapper file\n");
05981             fprintf(stderr,"  -resetmapper                            Erase mapper file\n");
05982             fprintf(stderr,"  -console                                Show console (win32)\n");
05983             fprintf(stderr,"  -noconsole                              Don't show console (debug+win32 only)\n");
05984             fprintf(stderr,"  -nogui                                  Don't show gui (win32 only)\n");
05985             fprintf(stderr,"  -nomenu                                 Don't show menu (win32 only)\n");
05986             fprintf(stderr,"  -userconf                               Create user level config file\n");
05987             fprintf(stderr,"  -conf <param>                           Use config file <param>\n");
05988             fprintf(stderr,"  -startui -startgui                      Start DOSBox-X with UI\n");
05989             fprintf(stderr,"  -startmapper                            Start DOSBox-X with mapper\n");
05990             fprintf(stderr,"  -showcycles                             Show cycles count\n");
05991             fprintf(stderr,"  -showrt                                 Show emulation speed relative to realtime\n");
05992             fprintf(stderr,"  -fullscreen                             Start in fullscreen\n");
05993             fprintf(stderr,"  -savedir <path>                         Save path\n");
05994             fprintf(stderr,"  -disable-numlock-check                  Disable numlock check (win32 only)\n");
05995             fprintf(stderr,"  -date-host-forced                       Force synchronization of date with host\n");
05996             fprintf(stderr,"  -debug                                  Set all logging levels to debug\n");
05997             fprintf(stderr,"  -early-debug                            Log early initialization messages in DOSBox (implies -console)\n");
05998             fprintf(stderr,"  -keydbg                                 Log all SDL key events (debugging)\n");
05999             fprintf(stderr,"  -lang <message file>                    Use specific message file instead of language= setting\n");
06000             fprintf(stderr,"  -nodpiaware                             Ignore (don't signal) Windows DPI awareness\n");
06001             fprintf(stderr,"  -securemode                             Enable secure mode\n");
06002             fprintf(stderr,"  -noautoexec                             Don't execute AUTOEXEC.BAT config section\n");
06003             fprintf(stderr,"  -exit                                   Exit after executing AUTOEXEC.BAT\n");
06004             fprintf(stderr,"  -c <command string>                     Execute this command in addition to AUTOEXEC.BAT.\n");
06005             fprintf(stderr,"                                          Make sure to surround the command in quotes to cover spaces.\n");
06006             fprintf(stderr,"  -break-start                            Break into debugger at startup\n");
06007             fprintf(stderr,"  -time-limit <n>                         Kill the emulator after 'n' seconds\n");
06008             fprintf(stderr,"  -fastbioslogo                           Fast BIOS logo (skip 1-second pause)\n");
06009             fprintf(stderr,"  -log-con                                Log CON output to a log file\n");
06010 
06011 #if defined(WIN32)
06012             DOSBox_ConsolePauseWait();
06013 #endif
06014 
06015             return 0;
06016         }
06017         else if (optname == "c") {
06018             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(tmp)) return false;
06019             control->opt_c.push_back(tmp);
06020         }
06021         else if (optname == "alt-vga") {
06022             control->opt_alt_vga_render = true;
06023         }
06024         else if (optname == "log-con") {
06025             control->opt_log_con = true;
06026         }
06027         else if (optname == "time-limit") {
06028             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(tmp)) return false;
06029             control->opt_time_limit = atof(tmp.c_str());
06030         }
06031         else if (optname == "break-start") {
06032             control->opt_break_start = true;
06033         }
06034         else if (optname == "exit") {
06035             control->opt_exit = true;
06036         }
06037         else if (optname == "noautoexec") {
06038             control->opt_noautoexec = true;
06039         }
06040         else if (optname == "securemode") {
06041             control->opt_securemode = true;
06042         }
06043         else if (optname == "nodpiaware") {
06044             control->opt_disable_dpi_awareness = true;
06045         }
06046         else if (optname == "keydbg") {
06047             log_keyboard_scan_codes = true;
06048         }
06049         else if (optname == "date-host-forced" || optname == "date_host_forced") {
06050             control->opt_date_host_forced = true;
06051         }
06052         else if (optname == "showrt") {
06053             control->opt_showrt = true;
06054         }
06055         else if (optname == "showcycles") {
06056             control->opt_showcycles = true;
06057         }
06058         else if (optname == "startmapper") {
06059             control->opt_startmapper = true;
06060         }
06061         else if (optname == "fullscreen") {
06062             control->opt_fullscreen = true;
06063         }
06064         else if (optname == "startui" || optname == "startgui") {
06065             control->opt_startui = true;
06066         }
06067         else if (optname == "disable-numlock-check" || optname == "disable_numlock_check") {
06068             /* mainline DOSBox expects -disable_numlock_check so we support that here too */
06069             control->opt_disable_numlock_check = true;
06070         }
06071         else if (optname == "savedir") {
06072             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(custom_savedir)) return false;
06073         }
06074         else if (optname == "userconf") {
06075             control->opt_userconf = true;
06076         }
06077         else if (optname == "lang") {
06078             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(control->opt_lang)) return false;
06079         }
06080         else if (optname == "fastbioslogo") {
06081             control->opt_fastbioslogo = true;
06082         }
06083         else if (optname == "conf") {
06084             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(tmp)) return false;
06085             control->config_file_list.push_back(tmp);
06086         }
06087         else if (optname == "editconf") {
06088             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(control->opt_editconf)) return false;
06089         }
06090         else if (optname == "opencaptures") {
06091             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(control->opt_opencaptures)) return false;
06092         }
06093         else if (optname == "opensaves") {
06094             if (!control->cmdline->NextOptArgv(control->opt_opensaves)) return false;
06095         }
06096         else if (optname == "eraseconf") {
06097             control->opt_eraseconf = true;
06098         }
06099         else if (optname == "resetconf") {
06100             control->opt_resetconf = true;
06101         }
06102         else if (optname == "printconf") {
06103             control->opt_printconf = true;
06104         }
06105         else if (optname == "erasemapper") {
06106             control->opt_erasemapper = true;
06107         }
06108         else if (optname == "resetmapper") {
06109             control->opt_resetmapper = true;
06110         }
06111         else if (optname == "noconsole") {
06112             control->opt_noconsole = true;
06113             control->opt_console = false;
06114         }
06115         else if (optname == "console") {
06116             control->opt_noconsole = false;
06117             control->opt_console = true;
06118         }
06119         else if (optname == "nomenu") {
06120             control->opt_nomenu = true;
06121         }
06122         else if (optname == "nogui") {
06123             control->opt_nogui = true;
06124         }
06125         else if (optname == "debug") {
06126             control->opt_debug = true;
06127         }
06128         else if (optname == "early-debug") {
06129             control->opt_earlydebug = true;
06130             control->opt_console = true;
06131         }
06132         else {
06133             printf("WARNING: Unknown option %s (first parsing stage)\n",optname.c_str());
06134         }
06135     }
06136 
06137     /* now that the above loop has eaten all the options from the command
06138      * line, scan the command line for batch files to run.
06139      * https://github.com/joncampbell123/dosbox-x/issues/369 */
06140     control->cmdline->BeginOpt(/*don't eat*/false);
06141     while (!control->cmdline->CurrentArgvEnd()) {
06142         control->cmdline->GetCurrentArgv(tmp);
06143 
06144         {
06145             struct stat st;
06146             const char *ext = strrchr(tmp.c_str(),'.');
06147             if (ext != NULL) { /* if it looks like a file... with an extension */
06148                 if (stat(tmp.c_str(), &st) == 0 && S_ISREG(st.st_mode)) {
06149                     if (!strcasecmp(ext,".bat") || !strcasecmp(ext,".exe") || !strcasecmp(ext,".com")) { /* .BAT files given on the command line trigger automounting C: to run it */
06150                         control->auto_bat_additional.push_back(tmp);
06151                         control->cmdline->EatCurrentArgv();
06152                         continue;
06153                     }
06154                 }
06155             }
06156         }
06157 
06158         control->cmdline->NextArgv();
06159     }
06160 
06161     return true;
06162 }

06235 #if defined(WIN32)
06236 // NTS: I intend to add code that not only indicates High DPI awareness but also queries the monitor DPI
06237 //      and then factor the DPI into DOSBox's scaler and UI decisions.
06238 void Windows_DPI_Awareness_Init() {
06239     // if the user says not to from the command line, or disables it from dosbox.conf, then don't enable DPI awareness.
06240     if (!dpi_aware_enable || control->opt_disable_dpi_awareness)
06241         return;
06242 
06243     /* log it */
06244     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Win32: I will announce High DPI awareness to Windows to eliminate upscaling");
06245 
06246     // turn off DPI scaling so DOSBox-X doesn't look so blurry on Windows 8 & Windows 10.
06247     // use GetProcAddress and LoadLibrary so that these functions are not hard dependencies that prevent us from
06248     // running under Windows 7 or XP.
06249     HRESULT (WINAPI *__SetProcessDpiAwareness)(PROCESS_DPI_AWARENESS) = NULL; // windows 8.1
06250     BOOL (WINAPI *__SetProcessDPIAware)(void) = NULL; // vista/7/8/10
06251     HMODULE __user32;
06252     HMODULE __shcore;
06253 
06254     __user32 = GetModuleHandle("USER32.DLL");
06255     __shcore = GetModuleHandle("SHCORE.DLL");
06256 
06257     if (__user32)
06258         __SetProcessDPIAware = (BOOL(WINAPI *)(void))GetProcAddress(__user32, "SetProcessDPIAware");
06259     if (__shcore)
06260         __SetProcessDpiAwareness = (HRESULT (WINAPI *)(PROCESS_DPI_AWARENESS))GetProcAddress(__shcore, "SetProcessDpiAwareness");
06261 
06262     if (__SetProcessDpiAwareness) {
06263         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("SHCORE.DLL exports SetProcessDpiAwareness function, calling it to signal we are DPI aware.");
06264         if (__SetProcessDpiAwareness(PROCESS_PER_MONITOR_DPI_AWARE) != S_OK)
06265             LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("SetProcessDpiAwareness failed");
06266     }
06267     if (__SetProcessDPIAware) {
06268         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("USER32.DLL exports SetProcessDPIAware function, calling it to signal we are DPI aware.");
06269         __SetProcessDPIAware();
06270     }
06271 }
06272 #endif
06273 
06274 bool VM_Boot_DOSBox_Kernel() {
06275     if (!dos_kernel_disabled) {
06276         RemoveEMSPageFrame();
06277         RemoveUMBBlock();
06278         DisableINT33();
06279         DOS_GetMemory_unmap();
06280         VFILE_Shutdown();
06281         PROGRAMS_Shutdown();
06282         DOS_UninstallMisc();
06283         SBLASTER_DOS_Shutdown();
06284         GUS_DOS_Shutdown();
06285         EMS_DoShutDown();
06286         XMS_DoShutDown();
06287         DOS_DoShutDown();
06288 
06289         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_SURPRISE_REBOOT); // <- apparently we rebooted without any notification (such as jmp'ing to FFFF:0000)
06290 
06291         dos_kernel_disabled = true;
06292 
06293 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
06294         int Reflect_Menu(void);
06295         Reflect_Menu();
06296 #endif
06297     }
06298 
06299     if (dos_kernel_disabled) {
06300         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_BOOT); // <- just starting the DOS kernel now
06301 
06302         /* DOS kernel init */
06303         dos_kernel_disabled = false; // FIXME: DOS_Init should install VM callback handler to set this
06304         void DOS_Startup(Section* sec);
06305         DOS_Startup(NULL);
06306 
06307 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
06308         int Reflect_Menu(void);
06309         Reflect_Menu();
06310 #endif
06311 
06312         void update_pc98_function_row(unsigned char setting,bool force_redraw=false);
06313 
06314         void DRIVES_Startup(Section *s);
06315         DRIVES_Startup(NULL);
06316 
06317         /* NEC's function key row seems to be deeply embedded in the CON driver. Am I wrong? */
06318         if (IS_PC98_ARCH) update_pc98_function_row(1);
06319 
06320         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_INIT_KERNEL_READY); // <- kernel is ready
06321 
06322         /* keyboard mapping, at this point in CONFIG.SYS parsing, right? */
06323         void DOS_KeyboardLayout_Startup(Section* sec);
06324         DOS_KeyboardLayout_Startup(NULL);
06325 
06326         /* Most MS-DOS installations have a DEVICE=C:\HIMEM.SYS somewhere near the top of their CONFIG.SYS */
06327         void XMS_Startup(Section *sec);
06328         XMS_Startup(NULL);
06329 
06330         /* And then after that, usually a DEVICE=C:\EMM386.EXE just after HIMEM.SYS */
06331         void EMS_Startup(Section* sec);
06332         EMS_Startup(NULL);
06333 
06334         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_INIT_CONFIG_SYS_DONE); // <- we just finished executing CONFIG.SYS
06335         SHELL_Init(); // <- NTS: this will change CPU instruction pointer!
06336         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_INIT_SHELL_READY); // <- we just finished loading the shell (COMMAND.COM)
06337 
06338         /* it's time to init parsing AUTOEXEC.BAT */
06339         void AUTOEXEC_Startup(Section *sec);
06340         AUTOEXEC_Startup(NULL);
06341 
06342         /* Most MS-DOS installations run MSCDEX.EXE from somewhere in AUTOEXEC.BAT. We do the same here, in a fashion. */
06343         /* TODO: Can we make this an OPTION if the user doesn't want to make MSCDEX.EXE resident? */
06344         /* TODO: When we emulate executing AUTOEXEC.BAT between INIT_SHELL_READY and AUTOEXEC_BAT_DONE, can we make a fake MSCDEX.EXE within drive Z:\
06345          *       and auto-add a Z:\MSCDEX.EXE to the top of AUTOEXEC.BAT, command line switches and all. if the user has not already added it? */
06346         void MSCDEX_Startup(Section* sec);
06347         MSCDEX_Startup(NULL);
06348 
06349         /* Some installations load the MOUSE.COM driver from AUTOEXEC.BAT as well */
06350         /* TODO: Can we make this an option? Can we add a fake MOUSE.COM to the Z:\ drive as well? */
06351         void MOUSE_Startup(Section *sec);
06352         MOUSE_Startup(NULL);
06353 
06354         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_INIT_AUTOEXEC_BAT_DONE); // <- we just finished executing AUTOEXEC.BAT
06355         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_INIT_AT_PROMPT); // <- now, we're at the DOS prompt
06356         SHELL_Run();
06357     }
06358 
06359     return true;
06360 }
06361 
06362 bool VM_PowerOn() {
06363     if (!guest_machine_power_on) {
06364         // powering on means power on event, followed by reset assert, then reset deassert
06365         guest_machine_power_on = true;
06366         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_POWERON);
06367         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_RESET);
06368         DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_RESET_END);
06369     }
06370 
06371     return true;
06372 }

06380 void update_pc98_clock_pit_menu(void) {
06381     Section_prop * dosbox_section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
06382 
06383     int pc98rate = dosbox_section->Get_int("pc-98 timer master frequency");
06384     if (pc98rate > 6) pc98rate /= 2;
06385     if (pc98rate == 0) pc98rate = 5; /* Pick the most likely to work with DOS games (FIXME: This is a GUESS!! Is this correct?) */
06386     else if (pc98rate < 5) pc98rate = 4;
06387     else pc98rate = 5;
06388 
06389     mainMenu.get_item("dos_pc98_pit_4mhz").check(pc98rate == 4).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06390     mainMenu.get_item("dos_pc98_pit_5mhz").check(pc98rate == 5).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06391 }
06392 
06393 bool dos_pc98_clock_menu_callback(DOSBoxMenu * const menu,DOSBoxMenu::item * const menuitem) {
06394     (void)menu;//UNUSED
06395     (void)menuitem;//UNUSED
06396     void TIMER_OnPowerOn(Section*);
06397     void TIMER_OnEnterPC98_Phase2_UpdateBDA(void);
06398 
06399     const char *ts = menuitem->get_name().c_str();
06400     if (!strncmp(ts,"dos_pc98_pit_",13))
06401         ts += 13;
06402     else
06403         return true;
06404 
06405     std::string tmp = "pc-98 timer master frequency=";
06406 
06407     {
06408         char tmp1[64];
06409         sprintf(tmp1,"%u",atoi(ts));
06410         tmp += tmp1;
06411     }
06412 
06413     Section_prop * dosbox_section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
06414     dosbox_section->HandleInputline(tmp.c_str());
06415 
06416     TIMER_OnPowerOn(NULL);
06417     TIMER_OnEnterPC98_Phase2_UpdateBDA();
06418 
06419     update_pc98_clock_pit_menu();
06420     return true;
06421 }

06493         // as if the initial setting in the dip switches

06500         if (gdc_5mhz_mode)
06501             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 start gdc at 5mhz=1");
06502         else
06503             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 start gdc at 5mhz=0");
06504 
06505         mainMenu.get_item("pc98_5mhz_gdc").check(gdc_5mhz_mode).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06506     }

06577 bool vid_pc98_enable_egc_menu_callback(DOSBoxMenu * const menu,DOSBoxMenu::item * const menuitem) {
06578     (void)menu;//UNUSED
06579     (void)menuitem;//UNUSED
06580     void gdc_egc_enable_update_vars(void);
06581     extern bool enable_pc98_egc;
06582     extern bool enable_pc98_grcg;
06583     extern bool enable_pc98_16color;
06584 //    extern bool enable_pc98_188usermod;
06585 
06586     if(IS_PC98_ARCH) {
06587         enable_pc98_egc = !enable_pc98_egc;
06588         gdc_egc_enable_update_vars();
06589 
06590         Section_prop * dosbox_section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
06591         if (enable_pc98_egc) {
06592             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 enable egc=1");
06593 
06594             if(!enable_pc98_grcg) { //Also enable GRCG if GRCG is disabled when enabling EGC
06595                 enable_pc98_grcg = !enable_pc98_grcg;
06596                 mem_writeb(0x54C,(enable_pc98_grcg ? 0x02 : 0x00) | (enable_pc98_16color ? 0x04 : 0x00));   
06597                 dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 enable grcg=1");
06598             }
06599         }
06600         else
06601             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 enable egc=0");
06602 
06603         mainMenu.get_item("pc98_enable_egc").check(enable_pc98_egc).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06604         mainMenu.get_item("pc98_enable_grcg").check(enable_pc98_grcg).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06605     }
06606     
06607     return true;
06608 }

06610 bool vid_pc98_enable_grcg_menu_callback(DOSBoxMenu * const menu,DOSBoxMenu::item * const menuitem) {
06611     (void)menu;//UNUSED
06612     (void)menuitem;//UNUSED
06613     extern bool enable_pc98_grcg;
06614     extern bool enable_pc98_egc;
06615     void gdc_grcg_enable_update_vars(void);
06616 
06617     if(IS_PC98_ARCH) {
06618         enable_pc98_grcg = !enable_pc98_grcg;
06619         gdc_grcg_enable_update_vars();
06620 
06621         Section_prop * dosbox_section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
06622         if (enable_pc98_grcg)
06623             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 enable grcg=1");
06624         else
06625             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 enable grcg=0");
06626 
06627         if ((!enable_pc98_grcg) && enable_pc98_egc) { // Also disable EGC if switching off GRCG
06628             void gdc_egc_enable_update_vars(void);
06629             enable_pc98_egc = !enable_pc98_egc;
06630             gdc_egc_enable_update_vars();   
06631             dosbox_section->HandleInputline("pc-98 enable egc=0");
06632         }
06633 
06634         mainMenu.get_item("pc98_enable_egc").check(enable_pc98_egc).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06635         mainMenu.get_item("pc98_enable_grcg").check(enable_pc98_grcg).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06636     }
06637 
06638     return true;
06639 }

06722 bool vsync_menu_callback(DOSBoxMenu * const menu,DOSBoxMenu::item * const menuitem) {
06723     (void)menu;//UNUSED
06724     (void)menuitem;//UNUSED
06725 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
06726     const char *val = menuitem->get_name().c_str();
06727     if (!strncmp(val,"vsync_",6))
06728         val += 6;
06729     else
06730         return true;
06731 
06732     SetVal("vsync", "vsyncmode", val);
06733 
06734     void change_output(int output);
06735     change_output(8);
06736 
06737     VGA_Vsync VGA_Vsync_Decode(const char *vsyncmodestr);

06753 bool output_menu_callback(DOSBoxMenu * const menu,DOSBoxMenu::item * const menuitem) {
06754     (void)menu;//UNUSED
06755 
06756     const char *what = menuitem->get_name().c_str();
06757 
06758     if (!strncmp(what,"output_",7))
06759         what += 7;
06760     else
06761         return true;
06762 
06763     if (!strcmp(what,"surface")) {
06764         if (sdl.desktop.want_type == SCREEN_SURFACE) return true;
06765         change_output(0);
06766     }
06767     else if (!strcmp(what,"opengl")) {
06768 #if C_OPENGL
06769         if (sdl.desktop.want_type == SCREEN_OPENGL && sdl_opengl.bilinear) return true;
06770         change_output(3);
06771 #endif
06772     }
06773     else if (!strcmp(what,"openglnb")) {
06774 #if C_OPENGL
06775         if (sdl.desktop.want_type == SCREEN_OPENGL && !sdl_opengl.bilinear) return true;
06776         change_output(4);
06777 #endif
06778     }
06779     else if (!strcmp(what,"direct3d")) {
06780 #if C_DIRECT3D
06781         if (sdl.desktop.want_type == SCREEN_DIRECT3D) return true;
06782         change_output(5);
06783 #endif
06784     }
06785 
06786     SetVal("sdl", "output", what);
06787     OutputSettingMenuUpdate();
06788     return true;
06789 }

06830 
06831 void CALLBACK_Idle(void);
06832 
06833 bool pausewithinterrupts_enable = false;
06834 
06835 void PauseWithInterruptsEnabled(Bitu /*val*/) {
06836     /* we can ONLY do this when the CPU is either in real mode or v86 mode.
06837      * doing this from protected mode will only crash the game.
06838      * also require that interrupts are enabled before pausing. */
06839     if (cpu.pmode) {
06840         if (!(reg_flags & FLAG_VM)) {
06841             PIC_AddEvent(PauseWithInterruptsEnabled,0.001);
06842             return;
06843         }
06844     }
06845 
06846     if (!(reg_flags & FLAG_IF)) {
06847         PIC_AddEvent(PauseWithInterruptsEnabled,0.001);
06848         return;
06849     }
06850 
06851     while (pausewithinterrupts_enable) CALLBACK_Idle();
06852 }
06853 
06854 void PauseWithInterrupts_mapper_shortcut(bool pressed) {
06855     if (!pressed) return;
06856 
06857     if (!pausewithinterrupts_enable) {
06858         pausewithinterrupts_enable = true;
06859         PIC_AddEvent(PauseWithInterruptsEnabled,0.001);
06860     }
06861     else {
06862         pausewithinterrupts_enable = false;
06863     }
06864 
06865     mainMenu.get_item("mapper_pauseints").check(pausewithinterrupts_enable).refresh_item(mainMenu);
06866 }

06876     return true;

06930     return x11_on_top;

06933 #endif

06957 #endif

07098 bool custom_bios = false;
07099 
07100 // OK why isn't this being set for Linux??
07101 #ifndef SDL_MAIN_NOEXCEPT
07102 #define SDL_MAIN_NOEXCEPT
07103 #endif
07104 
07105 //extern void UI_Init(void);
07106 int main(int argc, char* argv[]) SDL_MAIN_NOEXCEPT {
07107     CommandLine com_line(argc,argv);
07108     Config myconf(&com_line);
07109 
07110 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
07111     CoInitializeEx(NULL, COINIT_APARTMENTTHREADED);
07112 #endif
07113 
07114 #if 0 /* VGA_Draw_2 self test: dot clock */
07115     {
07116         const double start_time = 0;
07117         signed long long count = 0;
07118         VGA_Draw_2 t;
07119 
07120         fprintf(stderr,"VGA_Draw_2: 1000Hz\n");
07121 
07122         t.dotclock.set_rate(1000,start_time);/*hz*/
07123         for (int i=0;i < 10000;i++) {
07124             t.dotclock.update(start_time + i);
07125 
07126             if (labs(t.dotclock.ticks - (signed long long)i) > 1ll) { /* NTS: Expect possible +/- 1 error due to floating point */
07127                 fprintf(stderr,"* TEST FAILURE:\n");
07128                 fprintf(stderr,"   ticks=%lld ticks_prev=%lld\n",(signed long long)i,(signed long long)t.dotclock.ticks);
07129                 return 1;
07130             }
07131         }
07132 
07133         t.dotclock.reset(start_time);
07134         assert(t.dotclock.base == start_time);
07135         assert(t.dotclock.ticks_prev == 0);
07136         assert(t.dotclock.ticks == 0);
07137 
07138         fprintf(stderr,"VGA_Draw_2: 1000Hz incremental\n");
07139 
07140         count = 0;
07141         t.dotclock.set_rate(1000,start_time);/*hz*/
07142         for (int i=0;i < 10000;i++) {
07143             t.dotclock.update(start_time + i);
07144             count += t.dotclock.delta_get();
07145             assert(t.dotclock.ticks == t.dotclock.ticks_prev);
07146 
07147             if (labs(count - (signed long long)i) > 1ll) { /* NTS: Expect possible +/- 1 error due to floating point */
07148                 fprintf(stderr,"* TEST FAILURE:\n");
07149                 fprintf(stderr,"   count=%lld ticks=%lld ticks_prev=%lld\n",count,(signed long long)i,(signed long long)t.dotclock.ticks);
07150                 return 1;
07151             }
07152 
07153             signed long long rc = t.dotclock.ticks2pic(count);
07154             if (labs(rc - (signed long long)i) > 1ll) { /* NTS: Expect possible +/- 1 error due to floating point */
07155                 fprintf(stderr,"* TEST FAILURE:\n");
07156                 fprintf(stderr,"   count=%lld ticks=%lld ticks_prev=%lld rc=%lld\n",count,(signed long long)i,(signed long long)t.dotclock.ticks,rc);
07157                 return 1;
07158             }
07159         }
07160 
07161         fprintf(stderr,"VGA_Draw_2: 1000Hz inc then 100Hz inc\n");
07162 
07163         count = 0;
07164         t.dotclock.set_rate(100,start_time + 1000);/*hz, rate change*/
07165         for (int i=0;i < 10000;i++) {
07166             t.dotclock.update(start_time + 1000 + (i * 10));/*1ms * 10 = 10ms = 100Hz */
07167             count += t.dotclock.delta_get();
07168             assert(t.dotclock.ticks == t.dotclock.ticks_prev);
07169 
07170             if (labs(count - (signed long long)i) > 1ll) { /* NTS: Expect possible +/- 1 error due to floating point */
07171                 fprintf(stderr,"* TEST FAILURE:\n");
07172                 fprintf(stderr,"   count=%lld ticks=%lld ticks_prev=%lld\n",count,(signed long long)i,(signed long long)t.dotclock.ticks);
07173                 return 1;
07174             }
07175 
07176             signed long long rc = t.dotclock.ticks2pic(count);
07177             if (labs(rc - ((signed long long)(i * 10) + 1000 + start_time)) > 1ll) { /* NTS: Expect possible +/- 1 error due to floating point */
07178                 fprintf(stderr,"* TEST FAILURE:\n");
07179                 fprintf(stderr,"   count=%lld ticks=%lld ticks_prev=%lld rc=%lld\n",count,(signed long long)i,(signed long long)t.dotclock.ticks,rc);
07180                 return 1;
07181             }
07182         }
07183 
07184         return 0;
07185     }
07186 #endif
07187 
07188 #if C_EMSCRIPTEN
07189     control->opt_debug = true;
07190     control->opt_earlydebug = true;
07191 #endif
07192 
07193     bitop::self_test();
07194     ptrop::self_test();
07195 
07196     // initialize output libraries
07197     OUTPUT_SURFACE_Initialize();
07198 #if C_OPENGL
07199     OUTPUT_OPENGL_Initialize();
07200 #endif
07201 #if C_DIRECT3D
07202     OUTPUT_DIRECT3D_Initialize();
07203 #endif
07204 
07205     // initialize some defaults in SDL structure here
07206     sdl.srcAspect.x = 4; sdl.srcAspect.y = 3; 
07207     sdl.srcAspect.xToY = (double)sdl.srcAspect.x / sdl.srcAspect.y;
07208     sdl.srcAspect.yToX = (double)sdl.srcAspect.y / sdl.srcAspect.x;
07209 
07210     control=&myconf;
07211 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
07212     /* Microsoft's IME does not play nice with DOSBox */
07213     ImmDisableIME((DWORD)(-1));
07214 #endif
07215 
07216 #if defined(MACOSX)
07217     /* The resource system of DOSBox-X relies on being able to locate the Resources subdirectory
07218        within the DOSBox-X .app bundle. To do this, we have to first know where our own executable
07219        is, which Mac OS X helpfully puts int argv[0] for us */
07220     /* NTS: Experimental testing shows that when we are run from the desktop (double-clicking on
07221             the .app bundle from the Finder) the current working directory is / (fs root). */
07222     extern std::string MacOSXEXEPath;
07223     extern std::string MacOSXResPath;
07224     MacOSXEXEPath = argv[0];
07225 
07226     /* The path should be something like /blah/blah/dosbox-x.app/Contents/MacOS/DosBox */
07227     /* If that's true, then we can move one level up the tree and look for */
07228     /* /blah/blah/dosbox-x.app/Contents/Resources */
07229     {
07230         const char *ref = argv[0];
07231         const char *s = strrchr(ref,'/');
07232         if (s != NULL) {
07233             if (s > ref) s--;
07234             while (s > ref && *s != '/') s--;
07235             if (!strncasecmp(s,"/MacOS/",7)) {
07236                 MacOSXResPath = std::string(ref,(size_t)(s-ref)) + "/Resources";
07237             }
07238         }
07239     }
07240 
07241     /* If we were launched by the Finder, the current working directory will usually be
07242        the root of the filesystem (/) which is useless. If we see that, change instead
07243        to the user's home directory */
07244     {
07245         char *home = getenv("HOME");
07246         char cwd[512];
07247 
07248         cwd[0]=0;
07249         getcwd(cwd,sizeof(cwd)-1);
07250 
07251         if (!strcmp(cwd,"/")) {
07252             /* Only the Finder would do that.
07253                Even if the user somehow did this from the Terminal app, it's still
07254                worth changing to the home directory because certain directories
07255                including / are locked readonly even for sudo in Mac OS X */
07256             /* NTS: HOME is usually an absolute path */
07257             if (home != NULL) chdir(home);
07258         }
07259     }
07260 #endif
07261 
07262     {
07263         std::string tmp,config_path,config_combined;
07264 
07265         /* -- parse command line arguments */
07266         if (!DOSBOX_parse_argv()) return 1;
07267 
07268         if (control->opt_time_limit > 0)
07269             time_limit_ms = (Bitu)(control->opt_time_limit * 1000);
07270 
07271         if (control->opt_console)
07272             DOSBox_ShowConsole();
07273 
07274         /* -- Handle some command line options */
07275         if (control->opt_eraseconf || control->opt_resetconf)
07276             eraseconfigfile();
07277         if (control->opt_printconf)
07278             printconfiglocation();
07279         if (control->opt_erasemapper || control->opt_resetmapper)
07280             erasemapperfile();
07281 
07282         /* -- Early logging init, in case these details are needed to debug problems at this level */
07283         /*    If --early-debug was given this opens up logging to STDERR until Log::Init() */
07284         LOG::EarlyInit();
07285 
07286 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS)
07287         {
07288             DISPLAY_DEVICE dd;
07289             unsigned int i = 0;
07290 
07291             do {
07292                 memset(&dd, 0, sizeof(dd));
07293                 dd.cb = sizeof(dd);
07294                 if (!EnumDisplayDevices(NULL, i, &dd, 0)) break;
07295                 LOG_MSG("Win32 EnumDisplayDevices #%d: name=%s string=%s", i, dd.DeviceName, dd.DeviceString);
07296                 i++;
07297 
07298                 if (strstr(dd.DeviceString, "VirtualBox") != NULL)
07299                     isVirtualBox = true;
07300             } while (1);
07301         }
07302 #endif
07303 
07304         /* -- Init the configuration system and add default values */
07305         CheckNumLockState();
07306         CheckCapsLockState();
07307         CheckScrollLockState();
07308 
07309         /* -- setup the config sections for config parsing */
07310         LOG::SetupConfigSection();
07311         SDL_SetupConfigSection();
07312         DOSBOX_SetupConfigSections();
07313 
07314         /* -- Parse configuration files */
07315         Cross::GetPlatformConfigDir(config_path);
07316 
07317         /* -- -- first the user config file */
07318         if (control->opt_userconf) {
07319             tmp.clear();
07320             Cross::GetPlatformConfigDir(config_path);
07321             Cross::GetPlatformConfigName(tmp);
07322             config_combined = config_path + tmp;
07323 
07324             LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Loading config file according to -userconf from %s",config_combined.c_str());
07325             control->ParseConfigFile(config_combined.c_str());
07326             if (!control->configfiles.size()) {
07327                 //Try to create the userlevel configfile.
07328                 tmp.clear();
07329                 Cross::CreatePlatformConfigDir(config_path);
07330                 Cross::GetPlatformConfigName(tmp);
07331                 config_combined = config_path + tmp;
07332 
07333                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Attempting to write config file according to -userconf, to %s",config_combined.c_str());
07334                 if (control->PrintConfig(config_combined.c_str())) {
07335                     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_NORMAL)("Generating default configuration. Writing it to %s",config_combined.c_str());
07336                     //Load them as well. Makes relative paths much easier
07337                     control->ParseConfigFile(config_combined.c_str());
07338                 }
07339             }
07340         }
07341 
07342         /* -- -- second the -conf switches from the command line */
07343         for (size_t si=0;si < control->config_file_list.size();si++) {
07344             std::string &cfg = control->config_file_list[si];
07345             if (!control->ParseConfigFile(cfg.c_str())) {
07346                 // try to load it from the user directory
07347                 control->ParseConfigFile((config_path + cfg).c_str());
07348                 if (!control->ParseConfigFile((config_path + cfg).c_str())) {
07349                 LOG_MSG("CONFIG: Can't open specified config file: %s",cfg.c_str());
07350                 }
07351             }
07352         }
07353 
07354         /* -- -- if none found, use dosbox.conf */
07355         if (!control->configfiles.size()) control->ParseConfigFile("dosbox.conf");
07356 
07357         /* -- -- if none found, use userlevel conf */
07358         if (!control->configfiles.size()) {
07359             tmp.clear();
07360             Cross::GetPlatformConfigName(tmp);
07361             control->ParseConfigFile((config_path + tmp).c_str());
07362         }
07363 
07364 #if (ENVIRON_LINKED)
07365         /* -- parse environment block (why?) */
07366         control->ParseEnv(environ);
07367 #endif
07368 
07369         /* -- initialize logging first, so that higher level inits can report problems to the log file */
07370         LOG::Init();
07371 
07372 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2) && !defined(HX_DOS)
07373         {
07374             DISPLAY_DEVICE dd;
07375             unsigned int i = 0;
07376 
07377             do {
07378                 memset(&dd, 0, sizeof(dd));
07379                 dd.cb = sizeof(dd);
07380                 if (!EnumDisplayDevices(NULL, i, &dd, 0)) break;
07381                 LOG_MSG("Win32 EnumDisplayDevices #%d: name=%s string=%s", i, dd.DeviceName, dd.DeviceString);
07382                 i++;
07383             } while (1);
07384         }
07385 
07386         if (isVirtualBox) LOG_MSG("Win32 VirtualBox graphics adapter detected");
07387 #endif
07388 
07389         /* -- Welcome to DOSBox-X! */
07390         LOG_MSG("DOSBox-X version %s",VERSION);
07391         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_NORMAL)("Copyright 2002-2019 enhanced branch by The Great Codeholio, forked from the main project by the DOSBox Team, published under GNU GPL.");
07392 
07393 #if defined(MACOSX)

07396 #endif
07397 
07398         /* -- [debug] setup console */
07399 #if C_DEBUG

07407 # endif
07408 #endif

07413 #endif

07415 #if !defined(C_SDL2)

07421

07423             LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("DOSBox_CheckOS results: id=%u major=%u minor=%u",id,major,minor);
07424         }

07427         /* -- SDL init hackery */
07428 #if SDL_VERSION_ATLEAST(1, 2, 14)

07430          * with this variable they will work correctly. I've only tested the 1.2.14 behaviour against the windows version of libsdl */
07431         putenv(const_cast<char*>("SDL_DISABLE_LOCK_KEYS=1"));
07432         LOG(LOG_GUI,LOG_DEBUG)("SDL 1.2.14 hack: SDL_DISABLE_LOCK_KEYS=1");
07433 #endif
07434 
07435 #ifdef WIN32
07436         /* hack: Encourage SDL to use windib if not otherwise specified */
07437         if (getenv("SDL_VIDEODRIVER") == NULL) {
07438 #if defined(C_SDL2)
07439             LOG(LOG_GUI, LOG_DEBUG)("Win32 hack: setting SDL_VIDEODRIVER=windows because environ variable is not set");
07440             putenv("SDL_VIDEODRIVER=windows");
07441 #else
07442             LOG(LOG_GUI,LOG_DEBUG)("Win32 hack: setting SDL_VIDEODRIVER=windib because environ variable is not set");
07443             putenv("SDL_VIDEODRIVER=windib");
07444 #endif
07445             sdl.using_windib=true;
07446         }
07447 #endif
07448 
07449 #if defined(WIN32) && defined(C_SDL2)
07450         /* HACK: WASAPI output on Windows 10 isn't working... */

07453             putenv("SDL_AUDIODRIVER=directsound");

07457         sdl.init_ignore = true;
07458 
07459     {
07460         Section_prop *section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"));
07461         assert(section != NULL);
07462 
07463         // boot-time option whether or not to report ourself as "DPI aware" to Windows so the
07464         // DWM doesn't upscale our window for backwards compat.
07465         dpi_aware_enable = section->Get_bool("dpi aware");
07466     }
07467 
07468 #ifdef WIN32
07469         /* Windows Vista/7/8/10 DPI awareness. If we don't tell Windows we're high DPI aware, the DWM will
07470          * upscale our window to emulate a 96 DPI display which on high res screen will make our UI look blurry.
07471          * But we obey the user if they don't want us to do that. */
07472         Windows_DPI_Awareness_Init();
07473 #endif
07474 #if defined(MACOSX) && !defined(C_SDL2)

07521         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Initializing SDL joystick subsystem...");
07522         if (SDL_InitSubSystem(SDL_INIT_JOYSTICK) >= 0) {
07523             sdl.num_joysticks = (Bitu)SDL_NumJoysticks();
07524             LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("SDL reports %u joysticks",(unsigned int)sdl.num_joysticks);

07560             if (strcmp(sdl_videodrv,"directx")==0) sdl.using_windib = false;

07568         /* FIXME: We need a more general "init list", outside of the section-based design,
07569          *        that we then execute serially here. */
07570         /* TODO: Each section currently uses "AddDestroyFunction" per section. We need to
07571          *       change over that code to a global destroy callback list instead. */
07572         /* TODO: Get rid of "init" and "destroy" callback lists per section. */
07573         /* TODO: Add a global (within the Config object) init and destroy callback list.
07574          *       On each call, init functions are added to the end of the list, and
07575          *       destroy functions added to the beginning of the list. That way, init
07576          *       is lowest level to highest, destroy is highest level to lowest. */
07577         /* TODO: Config object should also have a "reset" callback list. On system
07578          *       reset each device would be notified so that it can emulate hardware
07579          *       reset (the RESET line on ISA/PCI bus), lowest level to highest. */
07580         /* TODO: Each "init" function should do the work of getting the section object,
07581          *       whatever section it wants to read, instead of us doing the work. When
07582          *       that's complete, the call to init should be without parameters (void).
07583          *       The hope is that the init functions can read whatever sections it wants,
07584          *       both newer DOSBox-X sections and existing DOSBox (mainline) compatible
07585          *       sections. */
07586 
07587         /* The order is important here:
07588          * Init functions are called low-level first to high level last,
07589          * because some init functions rely on others. */

08041 
08042 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_SDLDRAW

08044         mainMenu.screenHeight = (unsigned int)sdl.surface->h;
08045         mainMenu.updateRect();
08046 #endif
08047 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
08048         /* Windows 7 taskbar extension support */
08049         {
08050             HRESULT hr;
08051 
08052             hr = CoCreateInstance(CLSID_TaskbarList, NULL, CLSCTX_SERVER, IID_ITaskbarList3, (LPVOID*)(&winTaskbarList));
08053             if (hr == S_OK) {
08054                 LOG_MSG("Windows: IID_ITaskbarList3 is available");
08055 
08056 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
08057                 THUMBBUTTON buttons[8];
08058                 int buttoni = 0;

08102 #endif
08103         {
08104             Section_prop *section = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("SDL"));
08105             assert(section != NULL);
08106 
08107             bool cfg_want_menu = section->Get_bool("showmenu");
08108 
08109             /* -- -- decide whether to set menu */
08110             if (menu_gui && !control->opt_nomenu && cfg_want_menu)
08111                 DOSBox_SetMenu();
08112             else
08113                 DOSBox_NoMenu();

08115 
08116 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_HMENU
08117         int Reflect_Menu(void);
08118         Reflect_Menu();
08119 #endif
08120 
08121         bool reboot_dos;
08122         bool run_machine;
08123         bool wait_debugger;
08124         bool reboot_machine;
08125         bool dos_kernel_shutdown;
08126 
08127 fresh_boot:
08128         reboot_dos = false;
08129         run_machine = false;
08130         wait_debugger = false;
08131         reboot_machine = false;
08132         dos_kernel_shutdown = false;
08133         guest_msdos_mcb_chain = (Bit16u)(~0u);
08134 
08135         /* NTS: CPU reset handler, and BIOS init, has the instruction pointer poised to run through BIOS initialization,
08136          *      which will then "boot" into the DOSBox kernel, and then the shell, by calling VM_Boot_DOSBox_Kernel() */
08137         /* FIXME: throwing int() is a stupid and nondescriptive way to signal shutdown/reset. */
08138         try {
08139 #if C_DEBUG
08140             if (control->opt_break_start) DEBUG_EnableDebugger();
08141 #endif
08142             DOSBOX_RunMachine();
08143         } catch (int x) {
08144             if (x == 2) { /* booting a guest OS. "boot" has already done the work to load the image and setup CPU registers */
08145                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Emulation threw a signal to boot guest OS");
08146 
08147                 run_machine = true; /* make note. don't run the whole shebang from an exception handler! */
08148                 dos_kernel_shutdown = !dos_kernel_disabled; /* only if DOS kernel enabled */
08149             }
08150             else if (x == 3) { /* reboot the system */
08151                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Emulation threw a signal to reboot the system");
08152 
08153                 reboot_machine = true;
08154                 dos_kernel_shutdown = !dos_kernel_disabled; /* only if DOS kernel enabled */
08155             }
08156             else if (x == 5) { /* go to PC-98 mode */
08157                 E_Exit("Obsolete int signal");
08158             }
08159             else if (x == 6) { /* reboot DOS kernel */
08160                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Emulation threw a signal to reboot DOS kernel");
08161 
08162                 reboot_dos = true;
08163                 dos_kernel_shutdown = !dos_kernel_disabled; /* only if DOS kernel enabled */
08164             }
08165             else if (x == 7) { /* DOS kernel corruption error (need to restart the DOS kernel) */
08166                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Emulation threw a signal to reboot DOS kernel");
08167 
08168                 reboot_dos = true;
08169                 wait_debugger = true;
08170                 dos_kernel_shutdown = !dos_kernel_disabled; /* only if DOS kernel enabled */
08171             }
08172             else if (x == 8) { /* Booting to a BIOS, shutting down DOSBox BIOS */
08173                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Emulation threw a signal to boot into BIOS image");
08174 
08175                 reboot_machine = true;
08176                 dos_kernel_shutdown = !dos_kernel_disabled; /* only if DOS kernel enabled */
08177             }
08178             else {
08179                 LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Emulation threw DOSBox kill switch signal");
08180 
08181                 // kill switch (see instances of throw(0) and throw(1) elsewhere in DOSBox)
08182                 run_machine = false;
08183                 dos_kernel_shutdown = false;
08184             }
08185         }
08186         catch (...) {
08187             throw;
08188         }
08189 
08190 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
08191         int Reflect_Menu(void);
08192         Reflect_Menu();
08193 #endif
08194 
08195         if (dos_kernel_shutdown) {
08196             /* NTS: we take different paths depending on whether we're just shutting down DOS
08197              *      or doing a hard reboot. */
08198 
08199             if (wait_debugger) {
08200 #if C_DEBUG
08201                 Bitu DEBUG_EnableDebugger(void);
08202                 void DEBUG_WaitNoExecute(void);
08203 
08204                 LOG_MSG("Starting debugger.");
08205                 DEBUG_EnableDebugger();
08206                 DEBUG_WaitNoExecute();
08207 #endif
08208             }
08209 
08210             /* new code: fire event */
08211             if (reboot_machine)
08212                 DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_EXIT_REBOOT_BEGIN);
08213             else
08214                 DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_EXIT_BEGIN);
08215 
08216             /* older shutdown code */
08217             RemoveEMSPageFrame();
08218 
08219             /* remove UMB block */
08220             if (!keep_umb_on_boot) RemoveUMBBlock();
08221 
08222             /* disable INT 33h mouse services. it can interfere with guest OS paging and control of the mouse */
08223             DisableINT33();
08224 
08225             /* unmap the DOSBox kernel private segment. if the user told us not to,
08226              * but the segment exists below 640KB, then we must, because the guest OS
08227              * will trample it and assume control of that region of RAM. */
08228             if (!keep_private_area_on_boot || reboot_machine)
08229                 DOS_GetMemory_unmap();
08230             else if (DOS_PRIVATE_SEGMENT < 0xA000)
08231                 DOS_GetMemory_unmap();
08232 
08233             /* revector some dos-allocated interrupts */
08234             if (!reboot_machine) {
08235                 real_writed(0,0x01*4,(Bit32u)BIOS_DEFAULT_HANDLER_LOCATION);
08236                 real_writed(0,0x03*4,(Bit32u)BIOS_DEFAULT_HANDLER_LOCATION);
08237             }
08238 
08239             /* shutdown DOSBox's virtual drive Z */
08240             VFILE_Shutdown();
08241 
08242             /* shutdown the programs */
08243             PROGRAMS_Shutdown();        /* FIXME: Is this safe? Or will this cause use-after-free bug? */
08244 
08245             /* remove environment variables for some components */
08246             DOS_UninstallMisc();
08247             SBLASTER_DOS_Shutdown();
08248             GUS_DOS_Shutdown();
08249             /* disable Expanded Memory. EMM is a DOS API, not a BIOS API */
08250             EMS_DoShutDown();
08251             /* and XMS, also a DOS API */
08252             XMS_DoShutDown();
08253             /* and the DOS API in general */
08254             DOS_DoShutDown();
08255 
08256             /* set the "disable DOS kernel" flag so other parts of this program
08257              * do not attempt to manipulate now-defunct parts of the kernel
08258              * such as the environment block */
08259             dos_kernel_disabled = true;
08260 
08261             /* new code: fire event */
08262             if (reboot_machine)
08263                 DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_EXIT_REBOOT_KERNEL);
08264             else
08265                 DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_DOS_EXIT_KERNEL);
08266 
08267 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
08268             int Reflect_Menu(void);
08269             Reflect_Menu();
08270 #endif
08271         }
08272 
08273 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
08274         int Reflect_Menu(void);
08275         Reflect_Menu();
08276 #endif
08277 
08278         if (run_machine) {
08279             bool disable_a20 = static_cast<Section_prop *>(control->GetSection("dosbox"))->Get_bool("turn off a20 gate on boot");
08280 
08281             /* if instructed, turn off A20 at boot */
08282             if (disable_a20) MEM_A20_Enable(false);
08283 
08284             /* PC-98: hide the cursor */
08285             if (IS_PC98_ARCH) {
08286                 void PC98_show_cursor(bool show);
08287                 PC98_show_cursor(false);
08288             }
08289 
08290             /* new code: fire event */
08291             DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_GUEST_OS_BOOT);
08292 
08293             LOG_MSG("Alright: DOS kernel shutdown, booting a guest OS\n");
08294             LOG_MSG("  CS:IP=%04x:%04x SS:SP=%04x:%04x AX=%04x BX=%04x CX=%04x DX=%04x\n",
08295                 SegValue(cs),reg_ip,
08296                 SegValue(ss),reg_sp,
08297                 reg_ax,reg_bx,reg_cx,reg_dx);
08298 
08299 #if C_DEBUG
08300             if (boot_debug_break) {
08301                 boot_debug_break = false;
08302 
08303                 void DEBUG_Enable(bool pressed);
08304                 DEBUG_Enable(true);
08305             }
08306 #endif
08307 
08308             /* run again */
08309             goto fresh_boot;
08310         }
08311 
08312 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
08313         int Reflect_Menu(void);
08314         Reflect_Menu();
08315 #endif
08316 
08317         if (reboot_machine) {
08318             LOG_MSG("Rebooting the system\n");
08319 
08320             boothax = BOOTHAX_NONE;
08321             guest_msdos_LoL = 0;
08322             guest_msdos_mcb_chain = 0;
08323 
08324             void CPU_Snap_Back_Forget();
08325             /* Shutdown everything. For shutdown to work properly we must force CPU to real mode */
08326             CPU_Snap_Back_To_Real_Mode();
08327             CPU_Snap_Back_Forget();
08328 
08329             /* new code: fire event */
08330             DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_RESET);
08331 
08332             extern bool custom_bios;
08333             if (custom_bios) {
08334                 /* need to relocate BIOS allocations */
08335                 void ROMBIOS_InitForCustomBIOS(void);
08336                 ROMBIOS_InitForCustomBIOS();
08337 
08338                 void CALLBACK_Init();
08339                 CALLBACK_Init();
08340 
08341 #if C_DEBUG
08342                 void DEBUG_ReinitCallback(void);
08343                 DEBUG_ReinitCallback();
08344 #endif
08345             }
08346 
08347             DispatchVMEvent(VM_EVENT_RESET_END);
08348 
08349             /* HACK: EGA/VGA modes will need VGA BIOS mapped in, ready to go */
08350             if (IS_EGAVGA_ARCH) {
08351                 void INT10_Startup(Section *sec);
08352                 INT10_Startup(NULL);
08353             }
08354 
08355 #if C_DEBUG
08356             if (boot_debug_break) {
08357                 boot_debug_break = false;
08358 
08359                 void DEBUG_Enable(bool pressed);
08360                 DEBUG_Enable(true);
08361             }
08362 #endif
08363 
08364             /* run again */
08365             goto fresh_boot;
08366         }
08367         else if (reboot_dos) { /* typically (at this time) to enter/exit PC-98 mode */
08368             LOG_MSG("Rebooting DOS\n");
08369 
08370             void CPU_Snap_Back_Forget();
08371             /* Shutdown everything. For shutdown to work properly we must force CPU to real mode */
08372             CPU_Snap_Back_To_Real_Mode();
08373             CPU_Snap_Back_Forget();
08374 
08375             /* all hardware devices need to know to reregister themselves PC-98 style */
08376 
08377             /* begin booting DOS again. */
08378             void BIOS_Enter_Boot_Phase(void);
08379             BIOS_Enter_Boot_Phase();
08380 
08381             /* run again */
08382             goto fresh_boot;
08383         }
08384 
08385 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
08386         int Reflect_Menu(void);
08387         Reflect_Menu();
08388 #endif
08389 
08390         /* and then shutdown */
08391         GFX_ShutDown();
08392 
08393         void CPU_Snap_Back_Forget();
08394         /* Shutdown everything. For shutdown to work properly we must force CPU to real mode */
08395         CPU_Snap_Back_To_Real_Mode();
08396         CPU_Snap_Back_Forget();
08397 
08398         /* NTS: The "control" object destructor is called here because the "myconf" object leaves scope.
08399          * The destructor calls all section destroy functions here. After this point, all sections have
08400          * freed resources. */
08401     }
08402 
08403     void CALLBACK_Dump(void);
08404     CALLBACK_Dump();
08405 
08406     /* GUI font registry shutdown */
08407 #if !defined(C_SDL2)
08408     GUI::Font::registry_freeall();
08409 #endif
08410     DOS_ShutdownDrives();
08411     DOS_ShutdownFiles();
08412     DOS_ShutdownDevices();
08413     CALLBACK_Shutdown();
08414 #if C_DYNAMIC_X86
08415     CPU_Core_Dyn_X86_Shutdown();
08416 #endif
08417     FreeBIOSDiskList();
08418     MAPPER_Shutdown();
08419     VFILE_Shutdown();
08420     PROGRAMS_Shutdown();
08421     TIMER_ShutdownTickHandlers();
08422 #if C_DEBUG
08423     DEBUG_ShutDown(NULL);
08424 #endif
08425 
08426     sticky_keys(true); //Might not be needed if the shutdown function switches to windowed mode, but it doesn't hurt
08427 
08428     //Force visible mouse to end user. Somehow this sometimes doesn't happen
08429 #if defined(C_SDL2)
08430     SDL_SetRelativeMouseMode(SDL_FALSE);
08431 #else
08432     SDL_WM_GrabInput(SDL_GRAB_OFF);
08433 #endif
08434     SDL_ShowCursor(SDL_ENABLE);
08435 
08436     /* Exit functions */
08437     while (!exitfunctions.empty()) {
08438         Function_wrapper &ent = exitfunctions.front();
08439 
08440         LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Calling exit function (%p) '%s'",(void*)((uintptr_t)ent.function),ent.name.c_str());
08441         ent.function(NULL);
08442         exitfunctions.pop_front();
08443     }
08444 
08445     LOG::Exit();
08446 
08447 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(C_SDL2)
08448 # if !defined(HX_DOS)
08449     ShowWindow(GetHWND(), SW_HIDE);
08450     SDL1_hax_SetMenu(NULL);/* detach menu from window, or else Windows will destroy the menu out from under the C++ class */
08451 # endif
08452 #endif
08453 #if DOSBOXMENU_TYPE == DOSBOXMENU_NSMENU
08454     void sdl_hax_macosx_setmenu(void *nsMenu);
08455     sdl_hax_macosx_setmenu(NULL);
08456 #endif
08457 
08458     SDL_Quit();//Let's hope sdl will quit as well when it catches an exception
08459 
08460 #if defined(WIN32) && !defined(HX_DOS)
08461     if (winTaskbarList != NULL) {
08462         winTaskbarList->Release();
08463         winTaskbarList = NULL;
08464     }
08465 #endif
08466 
08467     mainMenu.unbuild();
08468     mainMenu.clear_all_menu_items();
08469 
08470     return 0;
08471 }

08487 void GFX_ShutDown(void) {
08488     LOG(LOG_MISC,LOG_DEBUG)("Shutting down GFX renderer");
08489     GFX_Stop();
08490     if (sdl.draw.callback) (sdl.draw.callback)( GFX_CallBackStop );
08491     if (sdl.mouse.locked) GFX_CaptureMouse();
08492     if (sdl.desktop.fullscreen) GFX_SwitchFullScreen();
08493 }

08511 void GUI_ResetResize(bool pressed) {
08512     void RENDER_CallBack( GFX_CallBackFunctions_t function );
08513 
08514     if (!pressed) return;
08515     userResizeWindowWidth = 0;
08516     userResizeWindowHeight = 0;
08517 
08518     if (GFX_GetPreventFullscreen())
08519         return;
08520 
08521     if (sdl.updating && !GFX_MustActOnResize()) {
08522         /* act on resize when updating is complete */
08523         sdl.deferred_resize = true;
08524     }
08525     else {
08526         sdl.deferred_resize = false;
08527         RENDER_CallBack(GFX_CallBackReset);
08528     }
08529 }
